# v0.8.1 Safety Stack — Implementation Plan

> **For agentic workers:** REQUIRED SUB-SKILL: Use superpowers:subagent-driven-development (recommended) or superpowers:executing-plans to implement this plan task-by-task. Steps use checkbox (`- [ ]`) syntax for tracking.

**Goal:** Ship the **first autonomy-enabling Flow release** — dispatch foundation only (post-rescope from codex round-4 RED #2). Wires worktree-per-task subagent dispatch + acceptance gate (5 type × 4 method executors) + Tier 1+2 notification + baseline test policy + post-merge integration verify + crash recovery. Replaces v0.8.0's `--auto-execute` exit-2 refusal with real execution behind a Notifier-only safety stack. **AFK timeout + budget enforcement + Phase 2 retry loop + in-loop staleness gate are all deferred to v0.8.2** (see "v0.8.2 deferred scope" section below). Staleness in v0.8.1 is doctor-only (out-of-band check via `flow doctor <slug>`), not gated in the dispatch loop. Phase 2 gates 1→3→4→5→6 run ONCE per dispatch — no retry.

**Hard rule:** Once `auto_engaged` event is written for a task, ANY subsequent path to interactive mode MUST go through `block + user choice`. NO orchestrator code path silently flips auto → interactive (caught by codex round 2 RED, reinforced by round 4 §6/§7 contradiction-fix).

**Design upstream:** `.flow/tasks/05-05-autonomous-mode-v0.8/design/v0.8.1-execution-semantics.md` (513 lines, 7 §s + §8 file schemas, all 16 Qs DECIDED through 4 codex consult rounds + round-3 design-pass RED→YELLOW→GREEN). Every task in this plan references specific design rows for acceptance criteria — implementers MUST consult the design before coding.

**Architecture (post-rescope; T17 AFK + T18 Budget deferred to v0.8.2):** Extend the v0.8.0 trio:
- `scripts/flow_contract.py` (T1–T3) — schema additions + ceiling enforcement
- `scripts/flow_state_writer.py` (T4–T6) — `acceptance-progress.jsonl` + `auto_prepare.lock` + 9 new event types
- `scripts/flow_orchestrator.py` (T10–T15, T19, T21) — real worktree dispatch + 8-gate runner (runs ONCE per dispatch, no retry loop) + crash recovery + 4-state auto_prepare detection + nested-autonomy guard
- `scripts/flow.py` (T22) — new `acceptance --run <slug>` subcommand for Phase 3 SKILL

Add three new modules:
- `scripts/flow_acceptance.py` (T7–T9) — 4 method executors + 6 type semantics + in-flight idempotent classification
- `scripts/flow_notification.py` (T16) — Tier 1+2 emitter (Tier 3 deferred per PRD §3 v0.8.2)
- `scripts/flow_subagent_dispatch.py` (T22) — concrete shim invoked by orchestrator dispatch loop's `_invoke_subagent_dispatch`

Extend two existing modules:
- `scripts/flow_doctor.py` (T20) — staleness check (5 triggers, doctor-only in v0.8.1; in-loop gate deferred to v0.8.2) + verification-worktree orphan recovery
- `claude/skills/flow/flow-phase2-execute/SKILL.md` + `flow-phase3-finish/SKILL.md` (T22) — replace v0.8.0 auto-mode guard with real auto-execute path; wire Phase 3 to `flow acceptance --run`

**Backward compat (preserved from v0.8.0):**
- Missing contract → interactive (zero regression for v0.6/0.7 plans)
- Unknown contract fields → accepted with warning (forward-compat per PRD §1.1)
- v0.8.1 schema version still `1` (additive fields don't bump version per Q2.2 + Y8 forward-compat decision)

**Forward compat:**
- v0.8.0 readers handle v0.8.1 contracts (additive fields ignored with warning)
- New `test_v080_unknown_field_compat.py` smoke verifies this

**Tech Stack:** Python 3.10+, stdlib only. Reuse `scripts/common/safe_io.py` (`atomic_write_text`, `atomic_write_json`, `append_jsonl_locked`) + `scripts/common/progress_meta.py` (frontmatter parser). Test framework: `unittest` via `tests/smoke/run.sh`. Subprocess pattern: `subprocess.run` (no asyncio — keeps wave dispatch synchronous and predictable for crash recovery).

---

## File Structure

### New scripts (3)

- `scripts/flow_acceptance.py` — `AcceptanceRunner` class. 4 method executors (cmd / file_exists / json_query / http) wired to 6 type semantics (unit / integration / e2e / smoke / behavior / regression). Runs each criterion; writes `acceptance-progress.jsonl` events; classifies in-flight idempotency (R8 hardened: default non-idempotent; allowlist OR rationale-required override); enforces per-criterion `timeout_sec` (R7); routes e2e timeout to `blocked_escalate` (Y1).
- `scripts/flow_notification.py` — `Notifier` class. Tier 1 writes `blocked.md` (always). Tier 2 emits OSC 9 + BEL (configurable via `notification.throttle_min` and `notification.tier2_enabled`; throttle key: `(task_id, issue_id)` 5-min default; BEL safety floor still fires unless `tier2_enabled=false`). Auto-detects terminal OSC 9 support via `$TERM_PROGRAM` (kitty / Ghostty / iTerm.app supported; falls back to BEL-only otherwise). Tier 3 (shell hook) accepted as schema field but NOT executed in v0.8.1 (deferred to v0.8.2 per PRD §3).
- `scripts/flow_subagent_dispatch.py` — concrete dispatch shim (T22). Resolves subagent invocation via `FLOW_SUBAGENT_DISPATCH_CMD` env var → `claude/capabilities/defaults.json::autonomy_orchestrator.dispatch_cmd` → fail-closed RuntimeError. Bridges orchestrator (Python) to subagent (Claude CLI / SKILL). Subprocess pattern; nonzero returncode is soft-warn (orchestrator handles via gates).

### Modified scripts (4)

- `scripts/flow_contract.py` — add new fields: `max_codex_rounds_per_task`, `notification.throttle_min`, `notification.tier2_enabled`, `idempotent_cmd_allowlist`, `post_merge_regression_optional`, criterion-level `idempotent` (object with rationale/timeout_sec/side_effect_class) / `timeout_sec` / `post_merge_skip`. Tighten validator: `contract_schema_version > CONTRACT_SCHEMA_VERSION_KNOWN_TO_RUNTIME` → fail-closed (R11). Defaults applied at parse time when fields missing.
- `scripts/flow_state_writer.py` — add `append_acceptance_progress(task_dir, event)` for `acceptance-progress.jsonl`; add `write_auto_prepare_lock(task_dir, lock)` + `consume_auto_prepare_lock(task_dir)` + `detect_auto_prepare_state(task_dir)` for the 4-state detection (Y8 emits `auto_prepare_consumed` event); add 9 new event constructors for `decisions.jsonl` (R3 / R4 / R6 / Y3 / Y8 — `task_ready_to_merge`, `merge_started`, `merge_applied`, `post_merge_verification_started`, `post_merge_verification_completed`, `post_merge_verify_failed`, `task_completed`, `auto_prepare_consumed`, `auto_prepare_interrupted`).
- `scripts/flow_orchestrator.py` — replace `--auto-execute` exit-2 stub with real dispatch loop:
  - `auto_prepare.lock` write before `auto_engaged`
  - per-task worktree creation (`<slug>+t<n>+<shortsha>`) with dual base commit recording (S6)
  - 8-gate runner (T12 + T13 — gates 1–6 in task worktree; gate 7 local merge; gate 8 post-merge verify in ephemeral verification worktree at `.claude/worktrees/verify/<run_id>+t<n>+<post_merge_sha>/`)
  - 9-step task completion transactional sequence with explicit gap-by-gap crash behavior (R3 + Y5)
  - Subagent-narrative-only return enforcement (orchestrator computes facts from git diff + test logs; subagent self-report fields ignored for audit trail)
  - Manifest violation detection (forbidden / shared / out_of_scope / allowed_writes precedence — extends v0.8.0 dry-run logic to enforcement)
  - Multi-task wave queue serialization (S1 — global block on `blocked_post_merge`; later tasks halt at `pending`)
  - Crash recovery dispatcher (T17 — 4 states: pre-`auto_prepare.lock`, lock+no-engaged+dead-pid, post-`auto_engaged`, mid-merge)
- `scripts/flow_doctor.py` — staleness checks (base branch / lockfile / prd.md mtime / dependencies version / baseline tests fail) + verification-worktree orphan detection.

### Modified config (1)

- `claude/capabilities/defaults.json` — promote `autonomy_orchestrator` from skip_if_not_available stub to real capability backed by v0.8.1's orchestrator. Promote `acceptance_verify` from stub to real capability backed by `flow_acceptance.AcceptanceRunner`.

### Modified skill prompts (2)

- `claude/skills/flow/flow-phase2-execute/SKILL.md` — REMOVE v0.8.0 auto-mode guard section. Replace with: "When `progress.md.autonomy_mode == auto`, invoke `flow orchestrator --auto-execute <slug>`; orchestrator handles dispatch, acceptance gates, post-merge verify, notification, and crash recovery. Subagent's role: execute the per-task prompt, return narrative summary only (orchestrator derives facts from worktree diff)."
- `claude/skills/flow/flow-phase3-finish/SKILL.md` — wire `flow acceptance --run <slug>` for the verify gate (replaces legacy test+codex-only gate when contract has `acceptance_criteria`).

### New tests (19)

## v0.8.2 deferred scope (route-A re-scope, codex round-4 RED #2)

The v0.8.1 plan was rescoped after codex round-4 flagged 6 structural concerns. The cleanest split (per "release workflow" pattern: small focused releases) defers the following to **v0.8.2** rather than cramming them into v0.8.1's first dispatch ship:

| Deferred component | What v0.8.1 ships instead | v0.8.2 adds |
|--------------------|----------------------------|-------------|
| **AFKDetector** (T17 originally) | Notifier (T16) ready to fire `aborted_afk` terminal events; no AFK loop owner. | `AFKDetector` class with `wait_with_24h_cap()` + S4 mechanical signals + `abort_now()`. Composes on top of T16 without API change. |
| **BudgetTracker** (T18 originally) | Contract `budget` dict parsed by T1 (forward-compat); no runtime enforcement. Fields accepted, ignored. | `BudgetTracker` class with 5 counters + Q3.2 dual-counter + paused-clock; wired into the Phase 2 retry loop. |
| **Phase 2 retry loop** | Gates 1→3→4→5→6 chain runs ONCE per dispatch; first non-pass halts and writes blocked.md (no retry). | `LOCAL_FIX_ALLOWED` retry around gates 4 + 5-unit/integration/behavior; gate 4 RED retry; semantic-diff comparison BEFORE-retry vs AFTER-retry; `max_retry_per_task` consumption via `BudgetTracker`. |
| **Staleness gate IN dispatch loop** (T20 partial defer) | T20's 5 triggers wired into `flow doctor` only (out-of-band check). User runs `flow doctor <slug>` manually. | T20's `StalenessChecker.check_all(include_baseline=False)` called BEFORE `auto_dispatch_task` in the dispatch loop; routes to block via shared Notifier. |
| **Y8 cross-cutting integration** (test_no_silent_mode_switch.py) | T22 owns creation; SKILL-routing assertions only. | Y8 budget-during-AFK-with-throttled-notification scenario added when AFK + Budget land. |

**Hard-rule preservation in v0.8.1**: the §7 "no silent mode switch" rule is fully enforced. Any path that would degrade auto → interactive goes through `block + user choice` via the Notifier. AFK timeout simply isn't a v0.8.1 trigger; budget cap simply isn't a v0.8.1 trigger. The contract still parses both fields (forward-compat), so v0.8.0 → v0.8.1 → v0.8.2 contract migration is monotonic.

**Why split**: codex round-4 identified that wiring retry + budget into the dispatch loop is a substantial design addition that needs dedicated thinking — better to ship the dispatch-and-recovery foundation first and use real usage feedback to design retry/budget semantics for v0.8.2.

---

## Task Detail (T1–T22)

> **Each task below contains: file paths, full step-by-step TDD checklist with failing tests + implementation + passing tests + commit. Implementers use `superpowers:subagent-driven-development` to dispatch each task to its own subagent in a worktree, OR `superpowers:executing-plans` to execute serially.**

### Task 1: Contract schema field additions + parse + defaults

**Files:**
- Modify: `scripts/flow_contract.py`
- Modify: `tests/smoke/test_contract.py`

**Design refs:** §2 Q2.2 (`max_codex_rounds_per_task`), §3 R8 (`idempotent_cmd_allowlist` + criterion-level `idempotent` object), §5 R9 (`notification.throttle_min`, `notification.tier2_enabled`), §6 R5 (criterion `type` + `method` orthogonal), §3 R7 (criterion `timeout_sec`), §3 S3 (`post_merge_regression_optional`), §6 Y1 (criterion `post_merge_skip` for non-regression types).

**Goal:** Extend the v0.8.0 `Contract` dataclass + `parse_contract()` to accept all v0.8.1 fields with sane defaults applied at parse time. Forward-compat preserved (unknown fields still warn-and-keep). Schema version stays at `1` (additive).

- [ ] **Step 1.1: Failing tests for new top-level budget field**

  Add to `tests/smoke/test_contract.py` `TestParseContract`:

  ```python
  def test_max_codex_rounds_per_task_default(self):
      """Q2.2: missing field → default 3"""
      path = self._write({
          "contract_schema_version": CONTRACT_SCHEMA_VERSION,
          "autonomy_mode": "interactive",
          "created_at": "2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
      })
      c = parse_contract(path)
      self.assertEqual(c.budget["max_codex_rounds_per_task"], 3)

  def test_max_codex_rounds_per_task_explicit(self):
      path = self._write({
          "contract_schema_version": CONTRACT_SCHEMA_VERSION,
          "autonomy_mode": "interactive",
          "created_at": "2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
          "budget": {"max_codex_rounds_per_task": 5},
      })
      c = parse_contract(path)
      self.assertEqual(c.budget["max_codex_rounds_per_task"], 5)
  ```

  Run: `python3 -m unittest tests.smoke.test_contract.TestParseContract.test_max_codex_rounds_per_task_default` → expect AttributeError or KeyError (failing test confirms the gap).

- [ ] **Step 1.2: Implement default-injection for `max_codex_rounds_per_task`**

  In `scripts/flow_contract.py` `parse_contract()`, after the existing budget construction:

  ```python
  # T1 round-3-fix Q2.2: max_codex_rounds_per_task default
  budget = dict(raw.get("budget") or {})
  budget.setdefault("max_codex_rounds_per_task", 3)
  ```

  Re-run the two tests → expect PASS.

  ```python
  if not isinstance(notif_raw, dict):
      raise ContractError("notification must be an object")
  notification = {
      "command": notif_raw.get("command"),
  ```

  ```python
  def test_idempotent_cmd_allowlist_default(self):
      """R8: missing → built-in allowlist"""

  def test_acceptance_criterion_with_idempotent_object(self):
      """R8: per-criterion override needs rationale + timeout_sec + side_effect_class"""
      path = self._write({
          "contract_schema_version": CONTRACT_SCHEMA_VERSION,
          "autonomy_mode": "auto",
          "created_at": "2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",

              "type": "smoke",

              "idempotent": {
                  "value": True,
                  "rationale": "GET against stub; no state mutation",
                  "timeout_sec": 30,
                  "side_effect_class": "read_only",
              },
              "post_merge_skip": False,
          }],
      })
      c = parse_contract(path)
      crit = c.acceptance_criteria[0]
      self.assertEqual(crit.method, "cmd")
      self.assertEqual(crit.timeout_sec, 30)
      self.assertTrue(crit.idempotent["value"])
      self.assertEqual(crit.idempotent["side_effect_class"], "read_only")

  def test_post_merge_skip_illegal_for_regression(self):
      """S3: regression type cannot have post_merge_skip=true unless contract.post_merge_regression_optional=true"""
      path = self._write({
          "contract_schema_version": CONTRACT_SCHEMA_VERSION,
          "autonomy_mode": "auto",
          "created_at": "2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
          "acceptance_criteria": [{
              "description": "main suite",
              "type": "regression",
              "method": "cmd",
              "command": "bash tests/smoke/run.sh",
              "post_merge_skip": True,
          }],
      })
      with self.assertRaises(ContractError):
          parse_contract(path)

  def test_post_merge_regression_optional_unlocks_skip(self):
      path = self._write({
          "contract_schema_version": CONTRACT_SCHEMA_VERSION,
          "autonomy_mode": "auto",
          "created_at": "2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
          "post_merge_regression_optional": True,
          "acceptance_criteria": [{
              "description": "main suite",
              "type": "regression",
              "method": "cmd",
              "command": "bash tests/smoke/run.sh",
              "post_merge_skip": True,
          }],
      })
      c = parse_contract(path)
      self.assertTrue(c.acceptance_criteria[0].post_merge_skip)

  def test_criterion_default_timeout_by_method(self):
      """R7: defaults — file_exists/json_query=30s, cmd=600s, http=60s, e2e=1800s"""
      path = self._write({
          "contract_schema_version": CONTRACT_SCHEMA_VERSION,
          "autonomy_mode": "auto",
          "created_at": "2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
          "acceptance_criteria": [
              {"description": "f", "type": "smoke", "method": "file_exists", "path": "VERSION"},
              {"description": "c", "type": "unit", "method": "cmd", "command": "true"},
              {"description": "h", "type": "integration", "method": "http", "url": "http://localhost/"},
              {"description": "e", "type": "e2e", "method": "cmd", "command": "playwright test"},
          ],
      })
      c = parse_contract(path)
      self.assertEqual(c.acceptance_criteria[0].timeout_sec, 30)   # file_exists
      self.assertEqual(c.acceptance_criteria[1].timeout_sec, 600)  # cmd
      self.assertEqual(c.acceptance_criteria[2].timeout_sec, 60)   # http
      self.assertEqual(c.acceptance_criteria[3].timeout_sec, 1800) # e2e
  ```

- [ ] **Step 1.6: Implement criterion + top-level fields**

  Extend `AcceptanceCriterion` dataclass:

  ```python
  @dataclass(frozen=True)
  class AcceptanceCriterion:
      description: str
      type: str          # unit | integration | e2e | smoke | behavior | regression
      method: str        # cmd | file_exists | json_query | http  (R5: orthogonal to type)
      command: str | None = None
      path: str | None = None
      url: str | None = None
      json_query: str | None = None
      timeout_sec: int | None = None    # R7
      idempotent: dict | None = None    # R8 hardened: {value, rationale, timeout_sec, side_effect_class}
      post_merge_skip: bool = False     # Y1 + S3
  ```

  Add to `Contract` dataclass:

  ```python
  idempotent_cmd_allowlist: list[str] = field(default_factory=lambda: [
      "pytest", "mypy", "eslint", "tsc", "cargo check", "go test",
      "flow doctor", "flow contract --validate",
  ])
  post_merge_regression_optional: bool = False
  notification: dict = field(default_factory=lambda: {
      "command": None, "throttle_min": 5, "tier2_enabled": True,
  })
  ```

  In `parse_contract()`:
  - Apply default `timeout_sec` per `method` if criterion omits it (constants `DEFAULT_TIMEOUT_BY_METHOD`).
  - Validate `idempotent` shape if present: must include `value` (bool), `rationale` (non-empty str), `timeout_sec` (int), `side_effect_class` ∈ {pure, read_only, cache_only, reversible}.
  - Cross-field rule: if any criterion has `type=regression` and `post_merge_skip=true`, require `raw.get("post_merge_regression_optional") is True`; else raise `ContractError("post_merge_skip illegal for type=regression unless post_merge_regression_optional set")`.

  Re-run all Step 1.5 tests → PASS.

### Task 2: Validator — `contract_schema_version` ceiling enforcement

**Files:**
- Modify: `scripts/flow_contract.py` (validator section)
- Modify: `scripts/flow_orchestrator.py` (must reject too-new schema in dispatch path, NOT just warn)
- Create: `tests/smoke/test_orchestrator_rejects_too_new_schema.py`

**Design refs:** R11 (v0.8.0 reader doesn't enforce ceiling; v0.8.1 must); §7 row "schema version too new" — KEEP fail-closed but make it teeth-bearing in v0.8.1 orchestrator.

**Goal:** Codex round-3 R11 finding: v0.8.0's `flow_orchestrator.py` calls `parse_contract()` without checking `contract_schema_version`. Orchestrator can ingest a v∞ contract because parse only warns. v0.8.1 must HARD-reject in dispatch path.

- [ ] **Step 2.1: Failing test — orchestrator dispatches against schema v=999 contract**

  ```python
  # tests/smoke/test_orchestrator_rejects_too_new_schema.py
  import json
  import os
  import subprocess
  import sys
  import tempfile
  import unittest
  from pathlib import Path

  REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent.parent
  FLOW = REPO_ROOT / "scripts" / "flow.py"


  class TestOrchestratorRejectsTooNewSchema(unittest.TestCase):
      def setUp(self):
          self.tmp = tempfile.mkdtemp()
          self.addCleanup(lambda: __import__("shutil").rmtree(self.tmp))
          slug_dir = Path(self.tmp) / ".flow" / "tasks" / "demo"
          slug_dir.mkdir(parents=True)
          (slug_dir / "progress.md").write_text(
              "---\nautonomy_mode: auto\ncontract_path: contract.json\n---\n\n"
              "## Tasks\n\n- [ ] T1 do thing — files: scripts/foo.py\n"
          )
          (slug_dir / "contract.json").write_text(json.dumps({
              "contract_schema_version": 999,  # too new
              "autonomy_mode": "auto",
              "created_at": "2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
          }))
          self.cwd = self.tmp

      def test_auto_execute_rejects_too_new_schema(self):
          r = subprocess.run(
              [sys.executable, str(FLOW), "orchestrator", "--auto-execute", "demo"],
              cwd=self.cwd,
              capture_output=True,
              text=True,
          )
          # Hard-reject, exit non-zero, message names the version mismatch
          self.assertNotEqual(r.returncode, 0)
          self.assertIn("schema_version", r.stderr.lower())
          self.assertIn("999", r.stderr)

      def test_dry_run_also_rejects_too_new(self):
          # Dry-run path should also fail-closed (no silent fallback to interactive)
          r = subprocess.run(
              [sys.executable, str(FLOW), "orchestrator", "--dry-run", "demo"],
              cwd=self.cwd,
              capture_output=True,
              text=True,
          )
          self.assertNotEqual(r.returncode, 0)
          self.assertIn("999", r.stderr)
  ```

  Run → expect FAIL: v0.8.0 orchestrator currently accepts v=999 (warns but proceeds).

- [ ] **Step 2.2: Implement ceiling check in orchestrator**

  In `scripts/flow_orchestrator.py`, after `parse_contract(contract_path)` in `build_plan()`:

  ```python
  if contract.contract_schema_version > CONTRACT_SCHEMA_VERSION:
      print(
          f"ERROR: contract.json declares schema_version={contract.contract_schema_version} "
          f"but this flow runtime knows up to {CONTRACT_SCHEMA_VERSION}. "
          f"Upgrade flow OR downgrade the contract.",
          file=sys.stderr,
      )
      sys.exit(1)
  ```

  Apply to BOTH `--dry-run` and `--auto-execute` paths. The contract validator already raises this as a hard error (not warn-prefixed); orchestrator was just not honoring it.

  Re-run → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 2.3: Cross-check that the validator catches it too**

  Add to `tests/smoke/test_contract.py`:

  ```python
  def test_validate_too_new_schema_hard_error(self):
      path = self._write({
          "contract_schema_version": 999,
          "autonomy_mode": "interactive",
          "created_at": "2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
      })
      ok, errors = validate_contract(path)
      self.assertFalse(ok)
      self.assertTrue(any("999" in e and "newer" in e.lower() for e in errors))
  ```

  This already passes from v0.8.0; new test just pins the contract.

- [ ] **Step 2.4: Commit**

  ```bash
  scripts/flow_orchestrator.py: after parse_contract(), hard-reject when
  contract_schema_version > CONTRACT_SCHEMA_VERSION known to runtime.
  Applies to BOTH --dry-run and --auto-execute paths. v0.8.0 orchestrator
  ```

### Task 3: Forward-compat smoke — v0.8.0 reader on v0.8.1 contract

**Files:**
- Create: `tests/smoke/test_v080_unknown_field_compat.py`
- (no source modifications — pure test)

**Design refs:** Q2.2 + Q5.1 + R8 forward-compat semantics; PRD §1.1 unknown-field-warning rule. **Y9 fix applied: test runs the v0.8.0 release tag's `flow_contract.py` against a v0.8.1 contract — isolates from current parser mutations.**

**Goal:** Prove that a v0.8.0 reader (the actual binary shipped in tag `v0.8.0`) does not crash when handed a contract written by v0.8.1. Forward-compat is the design's promise; this test binds the promise.

- [ ] **Step 3.1: Write the test using git-checked-out v0.8.0 tag binary**

  ```python
  # tests/smoke/test_v080_unknown_field_compat.py
  import json
  import os
  import subprocess
  import sys
  import tempfile
  import unittest
  from pathlib import Path

  REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent.parent


  class TestV080ReaderHandlesV081Contract(unittest.TestCase):
      """Y9 fix: run the actual v0.8.0 tag binary, not the live (mutated)
      parser. This isolates the test from T1/T2 changes.
      """

      def setUp(self):
          self.tmp = tempfile.mkdtemp()
          self.addCleanup(lambda: __import__("shutil").rmtree(self.tmp))

      def _v080_worktree(self):
          """Create an ephemeral worktree at v0.8.0 tag; return its path."""
          wt = Path(self.tmp) / "v080"
          subprocess.run(
              ["git", "worktree", "add", "--detach", str(wt), "v0.8.0"],
              cwd=REPO_ROOT, check=True, capture_output=True,
          )
          self.addCleanup(lambda: subprocess.run(
              ["git", "worktree", "remove", "--force", str(wt)],
              cwd=REPO_ROOT, capture_output=True,
          ))
          return wt

      def test_v080_reader_accepts_v081_fields_with_warning(self):
          v080 = self._v080_worktree()
          slug_dir = Path(self.tmp) / ".flow" / "tasks" / "demo"
          slug_dir.mkdir(parents=True)
          # v0.8.1-shape contract: includes max_codex_rounds_per_task,
          # notification.throttle_min/tier2_enabled, idempotent_cmd_allowlist,
          # post_merge_regression_optional, criterion-level new fields.
          (slug_dir / "contract.json").write_text(json.dumps({
              "contract_schema_version": 1,
              "autonomy_mode": "interactive",
              "created_at": "2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
              "budget": {"max_codex_rounds_per_task": 3},
              "notification": {"throttle_min": 5, "tier2_enabled": True},
              "idempotent_cmd_allowlist": ["pytest"],
              "post_merge_regression_optional": False,
              "acceptance_criteria": [{
                  "description": "smoke",
                  "type": "smoke",
                  "method": "cmd",
                  "command": "true",
                  "timeout_sec": 30,
                  "idempotent": {
                      "value": True, "rationale": "noop",
                      "timeout_sec": 30, "side_effect_class": "pure",
                  },
                  "post_merge_skip": False,
              }],
          }))
          # Run v0.8.0's flow contract --validate against the v0.8.1 contract
          r = subprocess.run(
              [sys.executable, str(v080 / "scripts" / "flow.py"),
               "contract", "--validate", "demo"],
              cwd=str(self.tmp),
              capture_output=True,
              text=True,
          )
          # v0.8.0 should not crash. May warn about unknown fields, but
          # exit code is 0 (validation passed; warnings don't flip OK).
          self.assertEqual(r.returncode, 0,
              f"v0.8.0 reader crashed on v0.8.1 contract:\n"
              f"stdout: {r.stdout}\nstderr: {r.stderr}")
          # Either no warnings (if v0.8.0 silently ignores unknown nested
          # keys) OR explicit warnings — both acceptable per design.
          self.assertNotIn("Traceback", r.stderr)
          self.assertNotIn("Traceback", r.stdout)
  ```

  Run → expect PASS if v0.8.0's parser is forward-compat as designed; FAIL if v0.8.0 crashes on unknown nested keys (would indicate a bug in the v0.8.0 ship that must be patched before v0.8.1 lands).

- [ ] **Step 3.2: If FAIL, escalate**

  This test is a hard correctness check: v0.8.0's forward-compat promise is binding. If FAIL, do NOT patch the test — patch v0.8.0's behavior or rethink what "schema version stays 1" means. Surface to user before continuing T4+.

- [ ] **Step 3.3: Commit**

  ```bash
  git add tests/smoke/test_v080_unknown_field_compat.py
  git commit -m "$(cat <<'EOF'
  test(v0.8.1): v0.8.0 reader forward-compat smoke against v0.8.1 contract (T3)

  tests/smoke/test_v080_unknown_field_compat.py: ephemeral worktree at
  v0.8.0 tag runs `flow contract --validate` against a v0.8.1-shape
  contract (with all new top-level + nested fields). Asserts v0.8.0
  does not crash and exit code stays 0. Implements Y9 fix from codex
  round-3 plan review: test runs the actual v0.8.0 tag binary, NOT
  the live (mutated) parser, so T1/T2 changes don't leak into the
  forward-compat assertion.

  Suite: 301 → 302 passing.

  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.7 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>
  EOF
  )"
  ```

  **Group A complete.** Contract schema additions + ceiling enforcement + forward-compat smoke all green.

### Task 4: `acceptance-progress.jsonl` writer + full schema

**Files:**
- Modify: `scripts/flow_state_writer.py`
- Modify: `tests/smoke/test_state_writer.py`

**Design refs:** §6 Q6.1 (start+complete events for in-flight resume), §6 R5 (split `type` from `method`), §6 S2 (`attempt_id` + `retry_idx`), §6 S3 (`exit_code` / `duration_ms` / `stdout_log_path` / `stderr_log_path` / `command_hash`), §6 Y7 (`criterion_hash` over normalized criterion — distinct from `command_hash`).

**Goal:** Add `AcceptanceProgressEvent` dataclass + `append_acceptance_progress(task_dir, ev)` helper. Per-criterion lifecycle: one `started` line written before invocation, one `completed`/`timeout` line after. Tail-read drives T9 in-flight resume; this task lands the **producer** side only — the read path lives in `flow_acceptance.py` (T9).

**Schema (per §6 line 261 + Y7) — 24 fields**:

| Field | Type | Notes |
|-------|------|-------|
| `event_id` | str | uuid4-12 — unique per line |
| `ts` | str | ISO 8601 UTC |
| `slug` | str | task slug (parity with `decisions.jsonl`) |
| `task_id` | str | per-criterion task ID |
| `run_id` | str | matches `auto_engaged.run_id` |
| `worktree_id` | str | per §4 Q4.1 naming (`<slug>+t<n>+<shortsha>`) |
| `attempt_id` | str | retry attempt id; increments per acceptance retry (S2) |
| `retry_idx` | int | 0-indexed within attempt (S2) |
| `criterion_id` | str | stable id from contract |
| `criterion_idx` | int | 0-indexed within `acceptance_criteria[]` |
| `criterion_hash` | str | sha256 over normalized criterion object (Y7) |
| `type` | str | `unit` \| `integration` \| `e2e` \| `smoke` \| `behavior` \| `regression` |
| `method` | str | `cmd` \| `file_exists` \| `json_query` \| `http` |
| `idempotent` | str | `"true"` \| `"false"` \| `"unknown"` (string for forward-compat) |
| `event` | str | `started` \| `completed` \| `timeout` |
| `started_at` | str | ISO 8601 — set on every event |
| `completed_at` | str/null | null on `started` |
| `timeout_sec` | int | criterion timeout (R7) |
| `status` | str/null | null on `started`; `pass` / `fail` / `inconclusive` / `interrupted` / `timed_out` otherwise |
| `exit_code` | int/null | cmd/http only; null otherwise |
| `duration_ms` | int/null | null on `started` |
| `stdout_log_path` | str/null | absolute path; null on `started` or non-cmd methods |
| `stderr_log_path` | str/null | as above |
| `command_hash` | str/null | sha256 of resolved command line; distinct from `criterion_hash` |

(Rare lock gap → mirror v0.8.0 pattern: log to stderr, proceed.)

- [ ] **Step 4.1: Failing test — `AcceptanceProgressEvent` dataclass shape + JSON roundtrip**

  Add `TestAcceptanceProgressEvent` to `test_state_writer.py`:

  ```python
  def test_event_dataclass_round_trip(self):
      from flow_state_writer import AcceptanceProgressEvent
      ev = AcceptanceProgressEvent(
          event_id="evt-1", ts="2026-05-06T00:00:00Z", slug="demo",
          task_id="T1", run_id="run-1", worktree_id="demo+t1+abc1234",
          attempt_id="att-1", retry_idx=0,
          criterion_id="c1", criterion_idx=0, criterion_hash="a"*64,
          type="unit", method="cmd", idempotent="true", event="started",
          started_at="2026-05-06T00:00:00Z", completed_at=None,
          timeout_sec=600, status=None, exit_code=None, duration_ms=None,
          stdout_log_path=None, stderr_log_path=None, command_hash=None,
      )
      d = asdict(ev)
      self.assertEqual(d["event"], "started")
      self.assertIsNone(d["completed_at"])
      json.loads(json.dumps(d))  # JSON-serializable end to end
  ```

  Run → expect `ImportError` / `NameError` for `AcceptanceProgressEvent`.

  ```python
  VALID_PROGRESS_EVENTS = ("started", "completed", "timeout")
  VALID_PROGRESS_STATUSES = (
      "pass", "fail", "inconclusive", "interrupted", "timed_out",
  )
  VALID_PROGRESS_TYPES = (
      "unit", "integration", "e2e", "smoke", "behavior", "regression",
  )
  VALID_PROGRESS_METHODS = ("cmd", "file_exists", "json_query", "http")
  VALID_PROGRESS_IDEMPOTENT = ("true", "false", "unknown")


  @dataclass
  class AcceptanceProgressEvent:
      event_id: str
      ts: str
      slug: str
      task_id: str
      run_id: str
      worktree_id: str
      attempt_id: str
      retry_idx: int
      criterion_id: str
      criterion_idx: int
      criterion_hash: str
      type: str
      method: str
      idempotent: str
      event: str
      started_at: str
      completed_at: Optional[str]
      timeout_sec: int
      status: Optional[str]
      exit_code: Optional[int]
      duration_ms: Optional[int]
      stdout_log_path: Optional[str]
      stderr_log_path: Optional[str]
      command_hash: Optional[str]
  ```

- [ ] **Step 4.4: Implement `append_acceptance_progress` + `_validate_progress_event`**

  ```python
  def append_acceptance_progress(
      task_dir: Path, ev: AcceptanceProgressEvent,
  ) -> None:
      _validate_progress_event(ev)
      path = task_dir / "acceptance-progress.jsonl"
      path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
      ok = append_jsonl_locked(path, asdict(ev))
      if not ok:
          # Mirror v0.8.0 decision-write pattern: audit gap → stderr.
          print(
              f"WARN: lock contention on {path}; "
              f"acceptance-progress event dropped: {ev.event_id} ({ev.event})",
              file=sys.stderr,
          )


  def _validate_progress_event(ev: AcceptanceProgressEvent) -> None:
      if ev.event not in VALID_PROGRESS_EVENTS:
          raise ValueError(
              f"event must be in {VALID_PROGRESS_EVENTS}, got {ev.event!r}"
          )
      if ev.status is not None and ev.status not in VALID_PROGRESS_STATUSES:
          raise ValueError(
              f"status must be in {VALID_PROGRESS_STATUSES} or None, "
              f"got {ev.status!r}"
          )
      if ev.type not in VALID_PROGRESS_TYPES:
          raise ValueError(
              f"type must be in {VALID_PROGRESS_TYPES}, got {ev.type!r}"
          )
      if ev.method not in VALID_PROGRESS_METHODS:
          raise ValueError(
              f"method must be in {VALID_PROGRESS_METHODS}, got {ev.method!r}"
          )
      if ev.idempotent not in VALID_PROGRESS_IDEMPOTENT:
          raise ValueError(
              f"idempotent must be in {VALID_PROGRESS_IDEMPOTENT}, "
              f"got {ev.idempotent!r}"
          )
      # Lifecycle invariants (Q6.1 schema):
      if ev.event == "started":
          if ev.completed_at is not None or ev.status is not None or ev.duration_ms is not None:
              raise ValueError(
                  "started event must have completed_at/status/duration_ms = None"
              )
      else:  # completed / timeout
          if ev.completed_at is None or ev.status is None or ev.duration_ms is None:
              raise ValueError(
                  f"{ev.event} event requires completed_at + status + duration_ms"
              )
  ```

  Re-run Step 4.3 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 4.5: Failing tests — `compute_criterion_hash` determinism (Y7)**

  ```python
  def test_criterion_hash_stable_for_same_criterion(self):
      crit = {
          "description": "smoke", "type": "smoke", "method": "cmd",
          "command": "true", "timeout_sec": 30,
      }
      h1 = compute_criterion_hash(crit)
      h2 = compute_criterion_hash({**crit})
      self.assertEqual(h1, h2)
      self.assertEqual(len(h1), 64)  # sha256 hex

  def test_criterion_hash_changes_when_command_changes(self):
      h1 = compute_criterion_hash(
          {"description": "x", "type": "unit", "method": "cmd", "command": "true"})
      h2 = compute_criterion_hash(
          {"description": "x", "type": "unit", "method": "cmd", "command": "false"})
      self.assertNotEqual(h1, h2)

  def test_criterion_hash_ignores_key_order(self):
      h1 = compute_criterion_hash(
          {"description": "x", "type": "unit", "method": "cmd", "command": "true"})
      h2 = compute_criterion_hash(
          {"command": "true", "method": "cmd", "type": "unit", "description": "x"})
      self.assertEqual(h1, h2)
  ```

- [ ] **Step 4.6: Implement `compute_criterion_hash`**

  Add `import hashlib` to module imports. Then:

  ```python
  def compute_criterion_hash(criterion: dict) -> str:
      """Y7: sha256 over key-sorted JSON of the normalized criterion. Stable
      across runs / processes; distinct from command_hash (which is just
      sha256 of the resolved command line). Used for audit identity in
      `acceptance-progress.jsonl`.
      """
      norm = json.dumps(criterion, sort_keys=True, ensure_ascii=False)
      return hashlib.sha256(norm.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
  ```

  Re-run Step 4.5 → PASS.

### Task 5: `auto_prepare.lock` write/consume/detect + 4-state recovery

**Files:**
- Modify: `scripts/flow_state_writer.py`
- Create: `tests/smoke/test_auto_prepare_lock_crash_blocks.py`
- Modify: `tests/smoke/test_state_writer.py`

**Design refs:** §8.1 (lock file path / schema / state machine), §6 R10 (boundary marker rationale + 4 detection states), §6 Y8 (`auto_prepare_consumed` event proves lock consumption), §1 row 17 (`blocked_auto_prepare` status routing).

**Goal:** Ship the 3-call surface + crash-recovery state machine:
- `write_auto_prepare_lock(task_dir, lock)` — atomic write at contract-parse time, **before** the `auto_engaged` event
- `consume_auto_prepare_lock(task_dir, *, slug, run_id, task_id)` — rename to `auto_prepare.consumed` **after** `auto_engaged` succeeds; emit `auto_prepare_consumed` event (Y8)
- `detect_auto_prepare_state(task_dir, *, run_id, task_id, current_contract_hash)` — return one of {`no_run`, `active_run`, `clean_post_engagement`, `interrupted_dead_pid`, `interrupted_contract_changed`, `orphan_lock_post_engaged`}; orchestrator (T19) routes per §6 / §8.1.

**Lock schema (per §8.1 — 13 fields)**:

```python
@dataclass
class AutoPrepareLock:
    lock_version: int
    slug: str
    run_id: str
    task_id: str
    contract_path: str
    contract_hash: str
    contract_schema_version: int
    created_at: str
    pid: int
    host: str
    cwd: str
    target_branch: str
    intended_first_task_dispatch_at: str
```

**Detection state machine (per §8.1 table)**:

| Lock present? | `auto_engaged` for run_id+task_id? | pid alive? | contract_hash matches current? | Returned state |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| no | no | n/a | n/a | `no_run` |
| no | yes | n/a | n/a | `clean_post_engagement` |
| yes | yes | n/a | n/a | `orphan_lock_post_engaged` (consume + warn) |
| yes | no | alive | n/a | `active_run` (do not interfere) |
| yes | no | dead | match | `interrupted_dead_pid` → block per R10 |
| yes | no | n/a | mismatch | `interrupted_contract_changed` → block per §8.1 |

- [ ] **Step 5.1: Failing test — `write_auto_prepare_lock` atomic + reject-when-present**

  Add `TestAutoPrepareLock` to `test_state_writer.py`:

  ```python
  def _make_lock(self, **overrides) -> "AutoPrepareLock":
      from flow_state_writer import AutoPrepareLock
      defaults = dict(
          lock_version=1, slug="demo", run_id="run-1", task_id="T1",
          contract_path="/tmp/c.json", contract_hash="a"*64,
          contract_schema_version=1, created_at="2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
          pid=os.getpid(), host="testhost", cwd="/tmp",
          target_branch="master",
          intended_first_task_dispatch_at="2026-05-06T00:00:01Z",
      )
      defaults.update(overrides)
      return AutoPrepareLock(**defaults)

  def test_write_lock_creates_file(self):
      with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as td:
          path = write_auto_prepare_lock(Path(td), self._make_lock())
          self.assertTrue(path.exists())
          self.assertEqual(path.name, "auto_prepare.lock")
          rec = json.loads(path.read_text())
          self.assertEqual(rec["slug"], "demo")
          self.assertEqual(rec["lock_version"], 1)

  def test_write_lock_rejects_when_lock_already_present(self):
      """§8.1: NEVER live alongside another unconsumed lock."""
      with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as td:
          write_auto_prepare_lock(Path(td), self._make_lock())
          with self.assertRaises(FileExistsError):
              write_auto_prepare_lock(Path(td), self._make_lock())
  ```

- [ ] **Step 5.2: Implement `AutoPrepareLock` + `write_auto_prepare_lock`**

  Add `from safe_io import atomic_write_json` to imports. Then:

  ```python
  AUTO_PREPARE_LOCK_FILENAME = "auto_prepare.lock"
  AUTO_PREPARE_CONSUMED_FILENAME = "auto_prepare.consumed"


  @dataclass
  class AutoPrepareLock:
      lock_version: int
      slug: str
      run_id: str
      task_id: str
      contract_path: str
      contract_hash: str
      contract_schema_version: int
      created_at: str
      pid: int
      host: str
      cwd: str
      target_branch: str
      intended_first_task_dispatch_at: str


  def write_auto_prepare_lock(task_dir: Path, lock: AutoPrepareLock) -> Path:
      task_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
      path = task_dir / AUTO_PREPARE_LOCK_FILENAME
      if path.exists():
          raise FileExistsError(
              f"auto_prepare.lock already present at {path}; "
              f"detect_auto_prepare_state() before retry"
          )
      atomic_write_json(path, asdict(lock))
      return path
  ```

  Re-run Step 5.1 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 5.4: Implement `consume_auto_prepare_lock`**

  Add `import uuid` to imports. Then:

  ```python
  def _new_event_id() -> str:
      """12-hex uuid suffix — used by all autonomy events (§8.4)."""
      return uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]


  def consume_auto_prepare_lock(
      task_dir: Path, *, slug: str, run_id: str, task_id: str,
  ) -> Path:
      lock_path = task_dir / AUTO_PREPARE_LOCK_FILENAME
      if not lock_path.exists():
          raise FileNotFoundError(
              f"no auto_prepare.lock to consume at {lock_path}"
          )
      consumed_path = task_dir / AUTO_PREPARE_CONSUMED_FILENAME
      os.replace(lock_path, consumed_path)  # atomic rename within fs
      consumed_at = datetime.datetime.now(datetime.UTC).strftime(
          "%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ"
      )
      # Y8: emit auto_prepare_consumed event. T6 wires append_autonomy_event
      # with required-field validation; here we use the raw helper because
      # T6 hasn't landed yet. T6 Step 6.4 refactors this to call
      # append_autonomy_event(EVENT_AUTO_PREPARE_CONSUMED, ...).
      append_jsonl_locked(
          task_dir / "decisions.jsonl",
          {
              "event_id": _new_event_id(),
              "ts": consumed_at,
              "event": "auto_prepare_consumed",
              "slug": slug,
              "run_id": run_id,
              "task_id": task_id,
              "lock_path": str(consumed_path),
              "consumed_at": consumed_at,
          },
      )
      return consumed_path
  ```

  Add `import os` if not already imported. Re-run Step 5.3 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 5.5: Failing tests — `detect_auto_prepare_state` 6 cases**

  ```python
  def test_state_no_run(self):
      with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as td:
          self.assertEqual(
              detect_auto_prepare_state(
                  Path(td), run_id="r", task_id="T1",
                  current_contract_hash="abc")["state"],

  def test_state_active_run_when_pid_alive(self):
      with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as td:
          write_auto_prepare_lock(Path(td), self._make_lock(pid=os.getpid()))
          r = detect_auto_prepare_state(
              Path(td), run_id="run-1", task_id="T1",
              current_contract_hash="a"*64)
          self.assertEqual(r["state"], "active_run")

  def test_state_interrupted_dead_pid(self):
      with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as td:
          # Pid 2**31 - 1 is well outside the OS pid range — guaranteed dead.
          write_auto_prepare_lock(Path(td), self._make_lock(pid=2**31 - 1))
          r = detect_auto_prepare_state(
              Path(td), run_id="run-1", task_id="T1",

          self.assertEqual(r["state"], "interrupted_dead_pid")
          self.assertEqual(r["block_type"], "auto_prepare_interrupted")

  def test_state_interrupted_contract_changed(self):
      with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as td:
          write_auto_prepare_lock(Path(td),
              self._make_lock(pid=os.getpid(), contract_hash="a"*64))
          r = detect_auto_prepare_state(
              Path(td), run_id="run-1", task_id="T1",
              current_contract_hash="b"*64)  # mismatch
          self.assertEqual(r["state"], "interrupted_contract_changed")
          self.assertEqual(r["block_type"], "auto_prepare_interrupted")

  def test_state_orphan_lock_post_engaged(self):
      """Lock present AND auto_engaged event present → orphan; consume + warn."""
      with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as td:
          task_dir = Path(td)
          write_auto_prepare_lock(task_dir,
              self._make_lock(pid=os.getpid()))

          r = detect_auto_prepare_state(
              task_dir, run_id="run-1", task_id="T1",
              current_contract_hash="a"*64)
          self.assertEqual(r["state"], "orphan_lock_post_engaged")

  def test_state_clean_post_engagement(self):
      """No lock, but auto_engaged exists for this run → normal post-engagement."""
      with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as td:
          task_dir = Path(td)
          append_jsonl_locked(task_dir / "decisions.jsonl", {
              "event": "auto_engaged", "run_id": "run-1", "task_id": "T1",
          })
          r = detect_auto_prepare_state(
              task_dir, run_id="run-1", task_id="T1",
              current_contract_hash="a"*64)
          self.assertEqual(r["state"], "clean_post_engagement")
  ```

- [ ] **Step 5.6: Implement `detect_auto_prepare_state` + `_is_pid_alive` + `_has_auto_engaged_for`**

  ```python
  def _is_pid_alive(pid: int) -> bool:
      """POSIX `kill(pid, 0)`. ESRCH = dead; EPERM = alive (different uid)."""
      if pid <= 0:
          return False
      try:
          os.kill(pid, 0)
          return True
      except ProcessLookupError:
          return False
      except PermissionError:
          return True


  def _has_auto_engaged_for(
      task_dir: Path, run_id: str, task_id: str,
  ) -> bool:
      path = task_dir / "decisions.jsonl"
      if not path.is_file():
          return False
      for line in path.read_text(encoding="utf-8").splitlines():
          try:
              rec = json.loads(line)
          except json.JSONDecodeError:
              continue
          if (rec.get("event") == "auto_engaged"
                  and rec.get("run_id") == run_id
                  and rec.get("task_id") == task_id):
              return True
      return False


  def detect_auto_prepare_state(
      task_dir: Path, *,
      run_id: str, task_id: str, current_contract_hash: str,
  ) -> dict:
      lock_path = task_dir / AUTO_PREPARE_LOCK_FILENAME
      lock_present = lock_path.is_file()
      engaged = _has_auto_engaged_for(task_dir, run_id, task_id)

      if not lock_present and not engaged:
          return {"state": "no_run"}
      if not lock_present and engaged:
          return {"state": "clean_post_engagement"}
      if lock_present and engaged:
          return {
              "state": "orphan_lock_post_engaged",
              "action": "consume_with_warning",
          }

      # lock_present and not engaged — distinguish the three sub-cases.
      lock = json.loads(lock_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
      if lock.get("contract_hash") != current_contract_hash:
          return {
              "state": "interrupted_contract_changed",
              "block_type": "auto_prepare_interrupted",
              "lock": lock,
          }
      if _is_pid_alive(int(lock.get("pid", -1))):
          return {"state": "active_run", "lock": lock}
      return {
          "state": "interrupted_dead_pid",
          "block_type": "auto_prepare_interrupted",
          "lock": lock,
      }
  ```

  Re-run Step 5.5 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 5.7: New smoke `test_auto_prepare_lock_crash_blocks.py` — ship-required gate**

  This smoke is one of the 11 ship-required tests (per design §7). T5 lands the writer/detector half only — the orchestrator subprocess + `blocked.md` assertion is grown in T19's recovery dispatcher. T5's smoke pins the detect-side contract so T19 has a stable foundation:

  ```python
  # tests/smoke/test_auto_prepare_lock_crash_blocks.py
  import json
  import os
  import sys
  import tempfile
  import unittest
  from pathlib import Path

  REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent.parent
  sys.path.insert(0, str(REPO_ROOT / "scripts"))
  from flow_state_writer import (
      AutoPrepareLock,
      write_auto_prepare_lock,
      detect_auto_prepare_state,
  )


  class TestAutoPrepareLockCrashDetected(unittest.TestCase):
      """T5 phase: writer/detector contract.
      T19 grows this with orchestrator subprocess + blocked.md assertion.
      """

      def test_dead_pid_lock_classified_as_interrupted(self):
          with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as td:
              lock = AutoPrepareLock(
                  lock_version=1, slug="demo", run_id="r", task_id="T1",
                  contract_path="/c.json", contract_hash="a"*64,
                  contract_schema_version=1,
                  created_at="2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
                  pid=2**31 - 1,  # outside OS pid range
                  host="x", cwd=td, target_branch="master",
                  intended_first_task_dispatch_at="2026-05-06T00:00:01Z",
              )
              write_auto_prepare_lock(Path(td), lock)
              r = detect_auto_prepare_state(
                  Path(td), run_id="r", task_id="T1",
                  current_contract_hash="a"*64,
              )
              self.assertEqual(r["state"], "interrupted_dead_pid")
              self.assertEqual(r["block_type"], "auto_prepare_interrupted")

      def test_contract_change_under_lock_classified_as_interrupted(self):
          with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as td:
              lock = AutoPrepareLock(
                  lock_version=1, slug="demo", run_id="r", task_id="T1",
                  contract_path="/c.json", contract_hash="old"*22,
                  contract_schema_version=1,
                  created_at="2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
                  pid=os.getpid(), host="x", cwd=td,
                  target_branch="master",
                  intended_first_task_dispatch_at="2026-05-06T00:00:01Z",
              )
              write_auto_prepare_lock(Path(td), lock)
              r = detect_auto_prepare_state(
                  Path(td), run_id="r", task_id="T1",
                  current_contract_hash="new"*22,  # mismatch
              )
              self.assertEqual(r["state"], "interrupted_contract_changed")
              self.assertEqual(r["block_type"], "auto_prepare_interrupted")


  if __name__ == "__main__":
      unittest.main()
  ```

  Comment header noting `# T19 will extend this with orchestrator subprocess + blocked.md assertion` so the next implementer knows the gap.

### Task 6: 10 new `decisions.jsonl` event types

**Files:**
- Modify: `scripts/flow_state_writer.py`
- Modify: `tests/smoke/test_state_writer.py`

**Design refs:** §8.4 (event table — 10 events listed in Y4 fix), §6 R3 (atomic merge events: `task_ready_to_merge` / `merge_started` / `merge_applied` / `task_completed`), §6 R4 (post-merge verify events: `post_merge_verification_started` / `post_merge_verification_completed` / `post_merge_verify_failed`), §6 R6 + Y3 (`auto_engaged` schema with worktree / lifecycle fields), §6 Y8 (`auto_prepare_consumed` — already emitted in T5; declared here for symmetry), §6 R10 + §8.1 (`auto_prepare_interrupted`), §6 S2 (`run_id` carried by all merge events), §6 Q6.2 (`supersedes: [ids]` LIST on retry-success).

**Goal:** Wire 10 event-name constants + a single internal helper `append_autonomy_event(task_dir, event, fields)` that validates `event ∈ ALL_AUTONOMY_EVENTS` and `fields` covers `EVENT_REQUIRED_FIELDS[event]`. T5 already emits `auto_prepare_consumed`; this task introduces the validated helper and refactors T5 to use it (gains required-field validation, behavior unchanged). Also promote `DecisionRecord.supersedes` to `list[str]` per Q6.2 — with v0.8.0 string-shape forward-compat normalization in `__post_init__`.

**Event coverage (Y4 — count = 10)**:

| # | Event | Source row | Required fields (per §8.4) |
|---|-------|-----------|----------------------------|
| 1 | `auto_engaged` | R6 + Y3 | `event_id, ts, slug, run_id, task_id, worktree_id, worktree_path, original_base_commit, current_base_commit, lifecycle_state, checkpoint_id, contract_path, contract_hash, contract_schema_version` |
| 2 | `task_ready_to_merge` | R3 | `event_id, ts, slug, run_id, task_id, worktree_id, worktree_path, original_base_commit, current_base_commit, lifecycle_state, diff_hash, target_commit_pre_merge` |
| 3 | `merge_started` | R3 | `event_id, ts, slug, run_id, task_id, worktree_id, worktree_path, integration_target, target_commit_pre_merge` |
| 4 | `merge_applied` | R3 | `event_id, ts, slug, run_id, task_id, worktree_id, target_commit_post_merge, merge_strategy` |
| 5 | `post_merge_verification_started` | R4 | `event_id, ts, slug, run_id, task_id, verification_worktree_id, verification_worktree_path, target_commit_post_merge` |
| 6 | `post_merge_verification_completed` | R4 | `event_id, ts, slug, run_id, task_id, verification_worktree_id, status, criteria_results` |
| 7 | `post_merge_verify_failed` | R3 + R4 | `event_id, ts, slug, run_id, task_id, verification_worktree_id, blocked_md_path, user_choices` |
| 8 | `task_completed` | R3 | `event_id, ts, slug, run_id, task_id, worktree_id, final_diff_hash, target_commit_post_merge` |
| 9 | `auto_prepare_consumed` | Y8 | `event_id, ts, slug, run_id, task_id, lock_path, consumed_at` |
| 10 | `auto_prepare_interrupted` | R10 | `event_id, ts, slug, run_id, task_id, lock_path, blocked_md_path` |

(`run_id` on every row per S2.)

**Note**: existing v0.8.0 `DecisionRecord` (Phase decision summaries) is preserved untouched. T6 events live in a separate event-namespace — every autonomy event has an `event` field naming its kind; v0.8.0 decision records do not. Readers tell them apart by presence/absence of `event`.

- [ ] **Step 6.4: Implement `append_autonomy_event` + refactor T5 to use it**

  ```python
  def append_autonomy_event(
      task_dir: Path, event: str, fields: dict,
  ) -> None:
      """Append a v0.8.1 autonomy event to decisions.jsonl. Validates that
      `event` is in ALL_AUTONOMY_EVENTS and that `fields` covers the
      required-field set per §8.4. Raises ValueError on either failure.
      Lock contention falls back to stderr warning (audit gap).
      """
      if event not in ALL_AUTONOMY_EVENTS:
          raise ValueError(
              f"unknown autonomy event: {event!r}; "
              f"must be in {ALL_AUTONOMY_EVENTS}"
          )
      required = EVENT_REQUIRED_FIELDS[event]
      missing = required - set(fields.keys())
      if missing:
          raise ValueError(
              f"event {event!r} missing required fields: {sorted(missing)}"
          )
      record = {"event": event, **fields}
      path = task_dir / "decisions.jsonl"
      path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
      ok = append_jsonl_locked(path, record)
      if not ok:
          print(
              f"WARN: lock contention on {path}; "
              f"autonomy event dropped: {event}/{fields.get('event_id')}",
              file=sys.stderr,
          )
  ```

  Refactor T5's `consume_auto_prepare_lock` to call this instead of the raw `append_jsonl_locked` (preserving Y8 emission, gaining required-field validation):

  ```python
  # Inside consume_auto_prepare_lock, replace the ad-hoc append with:
  append_autonomy_event(
      task_dir, EVENT_AUTO_PREPARE_CONSUMED,
      {
          "event_id": _new_event_id(),
          "ts": consumed_at,
          "slug": slug,
          "run_id": run_id,
          "task_id": task_id,
          "lock_path": str(consumed_path),
          "consumed_at": consumed_at,
      },
  )
  ```

  Re-run Step 6.3 + Step 5.3/5.4 (regression) → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 6.5: Failing test — `DecisionRecord.supersedes` list semantics (Q6.2)**

  Q6.2 promotes `DecisionRecord.supersedes` from `Optional[str]` (v0.8.0 ship) to `list[str]` (codex-refined). v0.8.0 tail records may have a single string — accept and normalize.

  ```python
  def test_decision_record_supersedes_list(self):
      """Q6.2: list semantics — one retry can resolve multiple prior failed decisions."""
      with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as td:
          rec = DecisionRecord(
              id="d-3", ts="2026-05-06T00:00:00Z", phase=2, task="T1",
              decision="land fix",
              reason="resolved RED issues from rounds 1 and 2",
              supersedes=["d-1", "d-2"],
          )
          append_decision(Path(td), rec)
          line = (Path(td) / "decisions.jsonl").read_text().splitlines()[-1]
          self.assertEqual(json.loads(line)["supersedes"], ["d-1", "d-2"])

  def test_decision_record_supersedes_default_empty_list(self):
      rec = DecisionRecord(
          id="d-1", ts="t", phase=1, task="T1",
          decision="x", reason="y",
      )
      self.assertEqual(rec.supersedes, [])

  def test_decision_record_v080_string_supersedes_normalized(self):
      """Forward-compat: v0.8.0-shape single string normalizes to [str]."""
      rec = DecisionRecord(
          id="d-2", ts="t", phase=1, task="T1",
          decision="x", reason="y",
          supersedes="d-1",  # v0.8.0 shape
      )
      self.assertEqual(rec.supersedes, ["d-1"])

  def test_decision_record_supersedes_none_normalized_to_empty(self):
      rec = DecisionRecord(
          id="d-2", ts="t", phase=1, task="T1",
          decision="x", reason="y", supersedes=None,
      )
      self.assertEqual(rec.supersedes, [])
  ```

- [ ] **Step 6.6: Implement `supersedes: list[str]` with v0.8.0-string normalization**

  ```python
  @dataclass
  class DecisionRecord:
      id: str
      ts: str
      phase: int
      task: str
      decision: str
      reason: str
      alternatives: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
      files_affected: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
      review_status: str = "pending"
      supersedes: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)

      def __post_init__(self) -> None:
          # Q6.2 forward-compat: accept legacy single-string shape and None.
          if self.supersedes is None:
              self.supersedes = []
          elif isinstance(self.supersedes, str):
              self.supersedes = [self.supersedes]
  ```

  ```python
  def test_v080_decision_and_v081_event_coexist_in_jsonl(self):
      """Reader disambiguates by presence/absence of `event` field."""
      with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as td:
          task_dir = Path(td)
          # v0.8.0-shape decision (no `event` field)
          append_decision(task_dir, DecisionRecord(
              id="d-1", ts="2026-05-06T00:00:00Z", phase=1, task="T1",
              decision="x", reason="y",
          ))

          append_autonomy_event(task_dir, EVENT_AUTO_ENGAGED,
              self._auto_engaged_fields())
          lines = (task_dir / "decisions.jsonl").read_text().splitlines()
          self.assertEqual(len(lines), 2)
          rec0, rec1 = (json.loads(l) for l in lines)
          self.assertNotIn("event", rec0)
          self.assertEqual(rec1["event"], "auto_engaged")
  ```

  Confirms readers can disambiguate without crashing on either shape.

### Task 7: 4 method executors + per-criterion timeout + idempotency defaults

**Files:**
- Create: `scripts/flow_acceptance.py`
- Create: `tests/smoke/test_acceptance.py` (general per-method coverage)
- Create: `tests/smoke/test_criterion_timeout_blocks.py` (ship-required Y1 smoke)

**Design refs:** §6 R8 (idempotency table — default non-idempotent for `cmd`; allowlist OR rationale override; e2e never overrideable), §6 R7 (per-criterion `timeout_sec`; defaults by method: `file_exists`/`json_query`=30s, `cmd`=600s, `http`=60s; e2e default 1800s as type-level override per design line 277), §6 Y1 (e2e timeout → §1 row 6 `blocked_escalate`, NOT row 5 — `extend_timeout_and_retry` disallowed for e2e), §6 Y7 (`criterion_hash` from T4 — used as audit identity), §1 row 5/6 (block routing on acceptance fail).

**Goal:** Stand up `scripts/flow_acceptance.py` with the `AcceptanceRunner` class that evaluates one criterion via its declared `method`. Per-method executor returns a `RunResult` with `{status, exit_code, duration_ms, stdout_log_path, stderr_log_path, command_hash, escalate}`. `started` + `completed`/`timeout` events emitted to `acceptance-progress.jsonl` via T4's writer. **Phase 2 vs Phase 3 retry decisions live in T8.** **Tail-scan resume + override resolution live in T9.**

**Non-goals (T7)**:
- No retry decision logic — T8 owns `§3 R1` (Phase 2 allow local for unit/integration/behavior) + `§3 R2` (Phase 3 behavior/e2e never local).
- No `idempotent_cmd_allowlist` resolution or per-criterion `idempotent` object override — T9 owns. T7 produces only the **default** idempotency string per R8 table.
- No HTTP method beyond GET. AcceptanceCriterion currently has no `http_method` field; non-GET acceptance is expressed as `cmd: curl -X POST -f ...` (documented in migration doc T22). Forward-compat: when v0.8.2 adds `http_method`, T7's classifier extends.

**`RunResult` schema**:

```python
@dataclass
class RunResult:
    status: str                          # pass | fail | inconclusive | timed_out
    exit_code: Optional[int] = None      # cmd/http only
    duration_ms: int = 0
    stdout_log_path: Optional[str] = None
    stderr_log_path: Optional[str] = None
    command_hash: Optional[str] = None
    escalate: bool = False               # Y1: e2e timeout / e2e fail forces True
    error_msg: Optional[str] = None      # human-readable diagnostic
```

**Per-method default timeout (R7 table)**:

| Method | Default `timeout_sec` (when criterion omits) |
|--------|----------------------------------------------|
| `file_exists` | 30 |
| `json_query` | 30 |
| `cmd` | 600 |
| `http` | 60 |
| (any method × `type=e2e`) | 1800 |

T1 already injects per-method defaults at parse time, so T7 may rely on `criterion.timeout_sec` always being non-None. T7 still defends against `None` for safety (raises `ValueError` — caller bug).

- [ ] **Step 7.1: Create `scripts/flow_acceptance.py` skeleton + `RunResult` + `AcceptanceRunner` hull**

  ```python
  """flow_acceptance — per-criterion executors + idempotency + timeout.

  Owns 4 method executors (cmd / file_exists / json_query / http) wired to
  the v0.8.1 contract's `acceptance_criteria` list. Each executor returns
  a RunResult; the AcceptanceRunner emits started + completed/timeout
  events into acceptance-progress.jsonl (via flow_state_writer T4).

  Phase 2 vs Phase 3 retry decisions live in flow_orchestrator.py via T8's
  evaluate_criterion(). Tail-scan resume + override resolution live in T9.
  """
  from __future__ import annotations

  import datetime
  import hashlib
  import json
  import subprocess
  import sys
  import time
  import urllib.error
  import urllib.request
  import uuid
  from dataclasses import dataclass, field
  from pathlib import Path
  from typing import Optional

  sys.path.insert(0, str(Path(__file__).resolve().parent / "common"))

  from flow_contract import AcceptanceCriterion  # type: ignore
  from flow_state_writer import (                # type: ignore
      AcceptanceProgressEvent,
      append_acceptance_progress,
      compute_criterion_hash,
  )


  DEFAULT_TIMEOUT_BY_METHOD = {
      "file_exists": 30,
      "json_query": 30,
      "cmd": 600,
      "http": 60,
  }
  E2E_TYPE_TIMEOUT = 1800  # design line 277


  @dataclass
  class RunResult:
      status: str
      exit_code: Optional[int] = None
      duration_ms: int = 0
      stdout_log_path: Optional[str] = None
      stderr_log_path: Optional[str] = None
      command_hash: Optional[str] = None
      escalate: bool = False
      error_msg: Optional[str] = None


  class AcceptanceRunner:
      """Per-criterion executor. T7 ships method-dispatch + timeout + default
      idempotency. T8 wires Phase 2/3 retry routing. T9 wires resume +
      override classification.
      """

      def __init__(
          self,
          *,
          worktree_root: Path,
          log_dir: Path,
          slug: str,
          task_id: str,
          run_id: str,
          worktree_id: str,
      ):
          self.worktree_root = worktree_root
          self.log_dir = log_dir
          self.slug = slug
          self.task_id = task_id
          self.run_id = run_id
          self.worktree_id = worktree_id
          self.log_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

      def run_one(
          self,
          criterion: AcceptanceCriterion,
          *,
          criterion_idx: int,
          attempt_id: str,
          retry_idx: int,
          task_dir: Path,
      ) -> RunResult:
          """Execute one criterion end-to-end:
          1. Emit `started` event into acceptance-progress.jsonl.
          2. Dispatch to the per-method executor.
          3. Emit `completed` (or `timeout`) event with the RunResult fields.
          """
          # Implementation lands in Steps 7.3 / 7.5 / 7.7 / 7.9 / 7.11; this
          # is the orchestration shell.
          raise NotImplementedError("see Steps 7.3+")
  ```

  Run `python3 -m unittest discover tests/smoke -p 'test_acceptance*.py'` → expect "no tests" (file is bare). The point is to confirm the module imports cleanly without circular-import issues against T1's `flow_contract.py` and T4's `flow_state_writer.py`.

  ```python
  import os

  REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent.parent

  from flow_acceptance import AcceptanceRunner, RunResult  # type: ignore

  class TestCmdMethod(unittest.TestCase):
  ```

- [ ] **Step 7.3: Implement `_run_cmd`**

  ```python
  def _run_cmd(self, criterion: AcceptanceCriterion) -> RunResult:
      if not criterion.command:
          return RunResult(
              status="inconclusive",
              error_msg="cmd method requires `command` field",
          )
      timeout = self._effective_timeout(criterion)
      command_hash = hashlib.sha256(criterion.command.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
      stdout_path = self.log_dir / f"{self.task_id}_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}.stdout"
      stderr_path = self.log_dir / f"{self.task_id}_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}.stderr"
      t0 = time.monotonic()
      try:
          with stdout_path.open("w") as out, stderr_path.open("w") as err:
              proc = subprocess.run(
                  criterion.command,
                  shell=True,
                  cwd=str(self.worktree_root),
                  timeout=timeout,
                  stdout=out,
                  stderr=err,
              )
          duration_ms = int((time.monotonic() - t0) * 1000)
          return RunResult(
              status="pass" if proc.returncode == 0 else "fail",
              exit_code=proc.returncode,
              duration_ms=duration_ms,
              stdout_log_path=str(stdout_path),
              stderr_log_path=str(stderr_path),
              command_hash=command_hash,
          )
      except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
          duration_ms = int((time.monotonic() - t0) * 1000)
          return RunResult(
              status="timed_out",
              exit_code=None,
              duration_ms=duration_ms,
              stdout_log_path=str(stdout_path),
              stderr_log_path=str(stderr_path),
              command_hash=command_hash,
              # escalate flag set in Step 7.13 if criterion.type == "e2e"
              error_msg=f"cmd exceeded timeout_sec={timeout}",
          )
  ```

  And `_effective_timeout` helper (used by all 4 executors):

  ```python
  def _effective_timeout(self, criterion: AcceptanceCriterion) -> int:
      if criterion.timeout_sec is not None:
          return int(criterion.timeout_sec)
      if criterion.type == "e2e":
          return E2E_TYPE_TIMEOUT
      return DEFAULT_TIMEOUT_BY_METHOD.get(criterion.method, 60)
  ```

  Re-run Step 7.2 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 7.5: Implement `_run_file_exists`**

  ```python
  def _run_file_exists(self, criterion: AcceptanceCriterion) -> RunResult:
      if not criterion.path:
          return RunResult(
              status="inconclusive",
              error_msg="file_exists method requires `path` field",
          )
      target = self.worktree_root / criterion.path
      t0 = time.monotonic()
      exists = target.is_file()
      duration_ms = int((time.monotonic() - t0) * 1000)
      return RunResult(
          status="pass" if exists else "fail",
          duration_ms=duration_ms,
      )
  ```

- [ ] **Step 7.7: Implement `_run_json_query`**

  ```python
  def _run_json_query(self, criterion: AcceptanceCriterion) -> RunResult:
      if not criterion.path or not criterion.json_query:
          return RunResult(
              status="inconclusive",
              error_msg="json_query method requires `path` + `json_query`",
          )
      target = self.worktree_root / criterion.path
      if not target.is_file():
          return RunResult(
              status="inconclusive",
              error_msg=f"json file not found: {target}",
          )
      t0 = time.monotonic()
      try:
          obj = json.loads(target.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
      except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
          return RunResult(
              status="inconclusive",
              duration_ms=int((time.monotonic() - t0) * 1000),
              error_msg=f"json parse error: {e}",
          )
      # Minimal dotted-path resolver — supports `a.b.c` only (no array index).
      # Forward-compat: real jsonpath in v0.8.2 if users ask for it.
      val: object = obj
      for part in criterion.json_query.split("."):
          if isinstance(val, dict) and part in val:
              val = val[part]
          else:
              return RunResult(
                  status="fail",
                  duration_ms=int((time.monotonic() - t0) * 1000),
                  error_msg=f"json_query path missing at: {part}",
              )
      duration_ms = int((time.monotonic() - t0) * 1000)
      return RunResult(
          status="pass" if val else "fail",
          duration_ms=duration_ms,
      )
  ```

  Re-run Step 7.6 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 7.8: Failing test — `_run_http` GET 2xx pass; non-2xx fail; refused fail**

  Use stdlib `http.server` for a localhost test fixture:

  ```python
  import http.server
  import threading

  class _StubHTTPHandler(http.server.BaseHTTPRequestHandler):
      def do_GET(self):
          if self.path == "/ok":
              self.send_response(200); self.end_headers()
              self.wfile.write(b"ok")
          else:
              self.send_response(503); self.end_headers()
      def log_message(self, *a, **kw):  # silence
          pass


  class TestHttpMethod(unittest.TestCase):
      @classmethod
      def setUpClass(cls):
          cls.server = http.server.HTTPServer(("127.0.0.1", 0), _StubHTTPHandler)
          cls.port = cls.server.server_address[1]
          cls.thread = threading.Thread(target=cls.server.serve_forever, daemon=True)
          cls.thread.start()

      @classmethod
      def tearDownClass(cls):
          cls.server.shutdown()
          cls.server.server_close()

      def setUp(self):
          self.tmp = tempfile.mkdtemp()
          self.addCleanup(lambda: __import__("shutil").rmtree(self.tmp))
          self.runner = AcceptanceRunner(
              worktree_root=Path(self.tmp),
              log_dir=Path(self.tmp) / "logs",
              slug="demo", task_id="T1", run_id="r1", worktree_id="w",
          )

      def test_http_2xx_pass(self):
          crit = AcceptanceCriterion(
              description="ok", type="integration", method="http",
              url=f"http://127.0.0.1:{self.port}/ok", timeout_sec=10,
          )
          r = self.runner._run_http(crit)
          self.assertEqual(r.status, "pass")
          self.assertEqual(r.exit_code, 200)

      def test_http_5xx_fail(self):
          crit = AcceptanceCriterion(
              description="bad", type="integration", method="http",
              url=f"http://127.0.0.1:{self.port}/missing", timeout_sec=10,
          )
          r = self.runner._run_http(crit)
          self.assertEqual(r.status, "fail")
          self.assertEqual(r.exit_code, 503)

      def test_http_refused_fail(self):
          crit = AcceptanceCriterion(
              description="dead", type="integration", method="http",
              url="http://127.0.0.1:1/", timeout_sec=2,
          )
          r = self.runner._run_http(crit)
          # Refused connection → fail (not inconclusive — server unreachable
          # is a deterministic verdict for an acceptance criterion).
          self.assertEqual(r.status, "fail")
          self.assertIsNone(r.exit_code)
  ```

- [ ] **Step 7.9: Implement `_run_http`**

  ```python
  def _run_http(self, criterion: AcceptanceCriterion) -> RunResult:
      if not criterion.url:
          return RunResult(
              status="inconclusive",
              error_msg="http method requires `url` field",
          )
      timeout = self._effective_timeout(criterion)
      command_hash = hashlib.sha256(
          f"GET {criterion.url}".encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
      t0 = time.monotonic()
      try:
          req = urllib.request.Request(criterion.url, method="GET")
          with urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=timeout) as resp:
              status_code = resp.status
              duration_ms = int((time.monotonic() - t0) * 1000)
              return RunResult(
                  status="pass" if 200 <= status_code < 300 else "fail",
                  exit_code=status_code,
                  duration_ms=duration_ms,
                  command_hash=command_hash,
              )
      except urllib.error.HTTPError as e:
          duration_ms = int((time.monotonic() - t0) * 1000)
          return RunResult(
              status="fail",
              exit_code=e.code,
              duration_ms=duration_ms,
              command_hash=command_hash,
              error_msg=f"http {e.code}",
          )
      except (urllib.error.URLError, TimeoutError, OSError) as e:
          duration_ms = int((time.monotonic() - t0) * 1000)
          # urllib raises URLError on socket.timeout too — distinguish.
          if isinstance(getattr(e, "reason", None), TimeoutError) or \
                  isinstance(e, TimeoutError):
              return RunResult(
                  status="timed_out",
                  duration_ms=duration_ms,
                  command_hash=command_hash,
                  error_msg=f"http exceeded timeout_sec={timeout}",
              )
          return RunResult(
              status="fail",
              duration_ms=duration_ms,
              command_hash=command_hash,
              error_msg=f"http error: {e}",
          )
  ```

  Re-run Step 7.8 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 7.10: Failing tests — per-method default timeout via `_effective_timeout`**

  ```python
  class TestEffectiveTimeout(unittest.TestCase):
      def setUp(self):
          self.r = AcceptanceRunner(
              worktree_root=Path("/tmp"),
              log_dir=Path("/tmp/logs"),
              slug="d", task_id="T", run_id="r", worktree_id="w",
          )

      def _crit(self, **kw):
          return AcceptanceCriterion(
              description="x", type=kw.get("type", "unit"),
              method=kw.get("method", "cmd"),
              timeout_sec=kw.get("timeout_sec"),
          )

      def test_explicit_timeout_wins(self):
          self.assertEqual(self.r._effective_timeout(
              self._crit(timeout_sec=42)), 42)

      def test_default_per_method(self):
          self.assertEqual(self.r._effective_timeout(
              self._crit(method="cmd")), 600)
          self.assertEqual(self.r._effective_timeout(
              self._crit(method="file_exists")), 30)
          self.assertEqual(self.r._effective_timeout(
              self._crit(method="json_query")), 30)
          self.assertEqual(self.r._effective_timeout(
              self._crit(method="http")), 60)

      def test_e2e_type_overrides_to_1800(self):
          self.assertEqual(self.r._effective_timeout(
              self._crit(method="cmd", type="e2e")), 1800)
  ```
