- [ ] **Step 7.13: Implement Y1 escalate-flag routing in `run_one`**

  Method-level executors stay type-blind (cleaner separation). Y1 routing happens in the orchestration shell `run_one`:

  ```python
  def run_one(
      self,
      criterion: AcceptanceCriterion,
      *,
      criterion_idx: int,
      attempt_id: str,
      retry_idx: int,
      task_dir: Path,
  ) -> RunResult:
      # 1. Emit started event (T4)
      criterion_id = self._criterion_id(criterion, criterion_idx)
      criterion_hash = compute_criterion_hash(criterion.__dict__ if hasattr(
          criterion, "__dict__") else dict(criterion))
      started_at = self._now_iso()
      idempotent = self.default_idempotency(criterion)
      append_acceptance_progress(task_dir, AcceptanceProgressEvent(
          event_id=uuid.uuid4().hex[:12], ts=started_at,
          slug=self.slug, task_id=self.task_id, run_id=self.run_id,
          worktree_id=self.worktree_id, attempt_id=attempt_id,
          retry_idx=retry_idx, criterion_id=criterion_id,
          criterion_idx=criterion_idx, criterion_hash=criterion_hash,
          type=criterion.type, method=criterion.method,
          idempotent=idempotent, event="started",
          started_at=started_at, completed_at=None,
          timeout_sec=self._effective_timeout(criterion),
          status=None, exit_code=None, duration_ms=None,
          stdout_log_path=None, stderr_log_path=None, command_hash=None,
      ))

      # 2. Dispatch
      result = self._dispatch_method(criterion)

      # 3. Y1: e2e timeout AND e2e fail both force escalate=True so T8/§1 row 6
      # routes to blocked_escalate (not row 5 blocked).
      if criterion.type == "e2e" and result.status in ("timed_out", "fail"):
          result.escalate = True

      # 4. Emit completed/timeout event
      completed_at = self._now_iso()
      append_acceptance_progress(task_dir, AcceptanceProgressEvent(
          event_id=uuid.uuid4().hex[:12], ts=completed_at,
          slug=self.slug, task_id=self.task_id, run_id=self.run_id,
          worktree_id=self.worktree_id, attempt_id=attempt_id,
          retry_idx=retry_idx, criterion_id=criterion_id,
          criterion_idx=criterion_idx, criterion_hash=criterion_hash,
          type=criterion.type, method=criterion.method,
          idempotent=idempotent,
          event="timeout" if result.status == "timed_out" else "completed",
          started_at=started_at, completed_at=completed_at,
          timeout_sec=self._effective_timeout(criterion),
          status=result.status, exit_code=result.exit_code,
          duration_ms=result.duration_ms,
          stdout_log_path=result.stdout_log_path,
          stderr_log_path=result.stderr_log_path,
          command_hash=result.command_hash,
      ))
      return result

  def _dispatch_method(self, criterion: AcceptanceCriterion) -> RunResult:
      if criterion.method == "cmd":
          return self._run_cmd(criterion)
      if criterion.method == "file_exists":
          return self._run_file_exists(criterion)
      if criterion.method == "json_query":
          return self._run_json_query(criterion)
      if criterion.method == "http":
          return self._run_http(criterion)
      return RunResult(
          status="inconclusive",
          error_msg=f"unknown method: {criterion.method!r}",
      )

  @staticmethod
  def _now_iso() -> str:
      return datetime.datetime.now(datetime.UTC).strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ")

  @staticmethod
  def _criterion_id(criterion: AcceptanceCriterion, idx: int) -> str:
      # Stable id from idx + hash — orchestrator may override with contract-supplied id later.
      h = compute_criterion_hash(criterion.__dict__ if hasattr(
          criterion, "__dict__") else dict(criterion))[:8]
      return f"c{idx}_{h}"
  ```

  Re-run Step 7.12 → PASS.

  Add a sibling test for e2e fail (non-timeout) escalate:

  ```python
  def test_e2e_cmd_fail_sets_escalate_flag(self):
      with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as td:
          runner = AcceptanceRunner(
              worktree_root=Path(td), log_dir=Path(td) / "l",
              slug="d", task_id="T", run_id="r", worktree_id="w",
          )
          crit = AcceptanceCriterion(
              description="bad e2e", type="e2e", method="cmd",
              command="false", timeout_sec=30,
          )
          r = runner.run_one(crit, criterion_idx=0,
                              attempt_id="a", retry_idx=0,
                              task_dir=Path(td))
          self.assertEqual(r.status, "fail")
          self.assertTrue(r.escalate)
  ```

- [ ] **Step 7.14: Failing tests — `default_idempotency` per R8 table**

  ```python
  class TestDefaultIdempotency(unittest.TestCase):
      def setUp(self):
          self.r = AcceptanceRunner(
              worktree_root=Path("/tmp"), log_dir=Path("/tmp/l"),
              slug="d", task_id="T", run_id="r", worktree_id="w",
          )

      def _crit(self, type_="unit", method="cmd"):
          return AcceptanceCriterion(
              description="x", type=type_, method=method, timeout_sec=30,
          )

      def test_file_exists_default_true(self):
          self.assertEqual(
              self.r.default_idempotency(self._crit(method="file_exists")),
              "true")

      def test_json_query_default_true(self):
          self.assertEqual(
              self.r.default_idempotency(self._crit(method="json_query")),
              "true")

      def test_cmd_default_false(self):
          """R8 hardened: cmd default non-idempotent; allowlist + rationale
          are override paths owned by T9."""
          self.assertEqual(
              self.r.default_idempotency(self._crit(method="cmd")),
              "false")

      def test_http_get_default_true(self):
          """T7 only supports GET; defaults to true. Non-GET awaits v0.8.2."""
          self.assertEqual(
              self.r.default_idempotency(self._crit(method="http")),
              "true")

      def test_e2e_type_always_false_no_override(self):
          """Design line 275: e2e always non-idempotent, NO override accepted."""
          self.assertEqual(
              self.r.default_idempotency(
                  self._crit(type_="e2e", method="cmd")),
              "false")
          self.assertEqual(
              self.r.default_idempotency(
                  self._crit(type_="e2e", method="http")),
              "false")
  ```

- [ ] **Step 7.15: Implement `default_idempotency`**

  ```python
  def default_idempotency(self, criterion: AcceptanceCriterion) -> str:
      """R8 table — DEFAULT idempotency (no override resolution).

      T9 owns the override path: contract.idempotent_cmd_allowlist + per-criterion
      `idempotent: {value, rationale, side_effect_class}`. T7 returns only the
      method-level + type-level defaults so T9 has a starting point.

      Returns one of {"true", "false", "unknown"} — string for the
      acceptance-progress.jsonl schema field (Y7 forward-compat).
      """
      if criterion.type == "e2e":
          # design line 275: NO override accepted
          return "false"
      if criterion.method in ("file_exists", "json_query"):
          return "true"
      if criterion.method == "cmd":
          return "false"  # R8 hardened
      if criterion.method == "http":
          # GET only in T7 — defaults to true. T9 + v0.8.2 add http_method.
          return "true"
      return "unknown"
  ```

  Re-run Step 7.14 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 7.16: New ship-required smoke `test_criterion_timeout_blocks.py`**

  Per design §7 line 318: this smoke is one of the 11 ship-required tests. Y1 says e2e timeout → `blocked_escalate` (not `blocked`). T7 exposes the `escalate` flag on `RunResult`; full block-routing lands in T8 + orchestrator wiring (T15). T7's smoke pins the half-the-test that's pinnable now: e2e timeout sets `escalate=True`; non-e2e timeout sets `escalate=False`.

  ```python
  # tests/smoke/test_criterion_timeout_blocks.py
  import sys, tempfile, unittest
  from pathlib import Path

  REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent.parent
  sys.path.insert(0, str(REPO_ROOT / "scripts"))
  from flow_acceptance import AcceptanceRunner       # type: ignore
  from flow_contract import AcceptanceCriterion      # type: ignore


  class TestCriterionTimeoutBlocks(unittest.TestCase):
      """T7 phase: timeout → status=timed_out + escalate flag.
      T8 wires the §1 row 5 (block) vs row 6 (blocked_escalate) routing
      via evaluate_criterion(); T15 wires the orchestrator block emission.
      This smoke pins the runner-side contract.
      """

      def _runner(self, td: str) -> AcceptanceRunner:
          return AcceptanceRunner(
              worktree_root=Path(td),
              log_dir=Path(td) / "logs",
              slug="demo", task_id="T1", run_id="r1", worktree_id="w",
          )

      def test_unit_cmd_timeout_blocks_without_escalate(self):
          with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as td:
              crit = AcceptanceCriterion(
                  description="long unit", type="unit", method="cmd",
                  command="sleep 5", timeout_sec=1,
              )
              r = self._runner(td).run_one(
                  crit, criterion_idx=0, attempt_id="a", retry_idx=0,
                  task_dir=Path(td))
              self.assertEqual(r.status, "timed_out")
              self.assertFalse(r.escalate)  # §1 row 5 (block)

      def test_e2e_cmd_timeout_blocks_with_escalate(self):
          """Y1: e2e timeout MUST escalate; T8 will route to §1 row 6."""
          with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as td:
              crit = AcceptanceCriterion(
                  description="long e2e", type="e2e", method="cmd",
                  command="sleep 5", timeout_sec=1,
              )
              r = self._runner(td).run_one(
                  crit, criterion_idx=0, attempt_id="a", retry_idx=0,
                  task_dir=Path(td))
              self.assertEqual(r.status, "timed_out")
              self.assertTrue(r.escalate)  # §1 row 6 (blocked_escalate)


  if __name__ == "__main__":
      unittest.main()
  ```

### Task 8: 6 type semantics + Phase 2/3 retry split

**Files:**
- Modify: `scripts/flow_acceptance.py` (add `evaluate_criterion`)
- Create: `tests/smoke/test_acceptance_retry_matrix.py` (ship-required)
- Create: `tests/smoke/test_phase3_behavior_e2e_no_retry.py` (ship-required)

**Design refs:** §3 R1 (Phase 2 allow local fix for unit/integration/behavior — gate 4 + 5-unit/integration/behavior in retry whitelist), §3 R2 (Phase 3 behavior/e2e/regression always escalate; never local), §3 R8 + R9 (whitelist semantic-diff check — defer to T13 codex review side; T8 only consumes the decision), §3 line 132–137 (per-gate retry table), §1 row 5 vs row 6 routing.

**Goal:** Add `evaluate_criterion(criterion, *, phase, runner_result)` to `AcceptanceRunner`. Inputs: a criterion + phase context (2 = task execution, 3 = post-merge verify) + the `RunResult` from T7's `run_one`. Output: `EvalDecision` describing the next routing step — `pass` / `local_fix_allowed` / `block_row5` / `blocked_escalate_row6` / `inconclusive`.

**Type × Phase decision matrix (per §3 line 130–137 + Y1)**:

| Type | Phase 2 (in worktree) | Phase 3 (post-merge verify) |
|------|----------------------|------------------------------|
| `unit` | pass→continue / fail→`local_fix_allowed` / timeout→`block_row5` | pass→continue / fail→`block_row5` (no retry; §3 line 134 "regression"-class severity post-merge) |
| `integration` | as `unit` | as `unit` Phase 3 |
| `behavior` | as `unit` (Phase 2 allows local — R1) | fail→`blocked_escalate_row6` (R2: never local in Phase 3) |
| `e2e` | fail/timeout→`blocked_escalate_row6` (always; PRD §1.3 + Y1) | fail/timeout→`blocked_escalate_row6` (always) |
| `smoke` | as `unit` Phase 2 | as `unit` Phase 3 |
| `regression` | fail/timeout→`block_row5` (never local; §3 line 134) | fail/timeout→`block_row5` |

(**`escalate=True` from `RunResult` (Y1) is honored**: even unit/integration with `escalate=True` route to `blocked_escalate_row6`. T7 sets `escalate` only for e2e at present; future contract additions could extend.)

**`EvalDecision` enum**:
```python
class EvalDecision(str, enum.Enum):
    PASS = "pass"
    LOCAL_FIX_ALLOWED = "local_fix_allowed"   # Phase 2 retry whitelist applies
    BLOCK_ROW5 = "block_row5"                 # §1 row 5: regular block
    BLOCKED_ESCALATE_ROW6 = "blocked_escalate_row6"  # §1 row 6: choices = {abort, interactive, split}
    INCONCLUSIVE = "inconclusive"             # T9 in-flight resume / contract bug
```

  ```python
  def test_phase2_unit_pass(self):
      runner = self._runner()
      crit = self._crit(type_="unit", method="cmd")
      result = RunResult(status="pass", exit_code=0, duration_ms=5)
      d = runner.evaluate_criterion(crit, phase=2, runner_result=result)
      self.assertEqual(d, EvalDecision.PASS)

  def test_phase2_unit_fail_allows_local_fix(self):
      crit = self._crit(type_="unit", method="cmd")
      result = RunResult(status="fail", exit_code=1, duration_ms=5)
      d = self._runner().evaluate_criterion(crit, phase=2, runner_result=result)
      self.assertEqual(d, EvalDecision.LOCAL_FIX_ALLOWED)

  def test_phase2_unit_timeout_blocks_row5(self):
      crit = self._crit(type_="unit", method="cmd")
      result = RunResult(status="timed_out", duration_ms=1000)
      d = self._runner().evaluate_criterion(crit, phase=2, runner_result=result)
      self.assertEqual(d, EvalDecision.BLOCK_ROW5)

  def test_phase2_e2e_fail_escalates_row6(self):
      crit = self._crit(type_="e2e", method="cmd")
      result = RunResult(status="fail", exit_code=1,
                         duration_ms=5, escalate=True)
      d = self._runner().evaluate_criterion(crit, phase=2, runner_result=result)
      self.assertEqual(d, EvalDecision.BLOCKED_ESCALATE_ROW6)

  def test_phase2_regression_fail_blocks_row5(self):
      """§3 line 134: regression type never local."""
      crit = self._crit(type_="regression", method="cmd")
      result = RunResult(status="fail", exit_code=1, duration_ms=5)
      d = self._runner().evaluate_criterion(crit, phase=2, runner_result=result)
      self.assertEqual(d, EvalDecision.BLOCK_ROW5)
  ```

- [ ] **Step 8.2: Implement `evaluate_criterion` skeleton**

  ```python
  import enum

  class EvalDecision(str, enum.Enum):
      PASS = "pass"
      LOCAL_FIX_ALLOWED = "local_fix_allowed"
      BLOCK_ROW5 = "block_row5"
      BLOCKED_ESCALATE_ROW6 = "blocked_escalate_row6"
      INCONCLUSIVE = "inconclusive"


  # Per design §3: types that allow Phase 2 local fix (gate 4 + gates
  # 5-unit/integration/behavior). e2e/regression/smoke escalate or block.
  PHASE2_LOCAL_FIX_TYPES = frozenset({"unit", "integration", "behavior", "smoke"})
  # Phase 3 types that never local (R2): behavior + e2e + regression.
  PHASE3_NEVER_LOCAL_TYPES = frozenset({"behavior", "e2e", "regression"})
  # E2E always escalates regardless of phase.
  ALWAYS_ESCALATE_TYPES = frozenset({"e2e"})


  class AcceptanceRunner:
      ...

      def evaluate_criterion(
          self,
          criterion: AcceptanceCriterion,
          *,
          phase: int,
          runner_result: RunResult,
      ) -> EvalDecision:
          if phase not in (2, 3):
              raise ValueError(f"phase must be 2 or 3, got {phase!r}")
          status = runner_result.status

          if status == "pass":
              return EvalDecision.PASS
          if status == "inconclusive":
              return EvalDecision.INCONCLUSIVE

          # Y1 + always-escalate: e2e always row 6 regardless of phase.
          if (criterion.type in ALWAYS_ESCALATE_TYPES
                  or runner_result.escalate):
              return EvalDecision.BLOCKED_ESCALATE_ROW6

          # Type-class routing
          if criterion.type == "regression":
              # §3 line 134: regression never local.
              return EvalDecision.BLOCK_ROW5

          if phase == 3 and criterion.type in PHASE3_NEVER_LOCAL_TYPES:
              # R2: behavior in Phase 3 escalates.
              return EvalDecision.BLOCKED_ESCALATE_ROW6

          if (phase == 2
                  and status == "fail"
                  and criterion.type in PHASE2_LOCAL_FIX_TYPES):
              # R1: Phase 2 fail for whitelist types → retry path.
              return EvalDecision.LOCAL_FIX_ALLOWED

          # Catch-all: timeout / non-whitelisted phase-2 fail / phase-3 fail.
          return EvalDecision.BLOCK_ROW5
  ```

  Re-run Step 8.1 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 8.3: Failing tests — `evaluate_criterion` Phase 3 (R2 enforcement)**

  ```python
  def test_phase3_behavior_fail_escalates_row6(self):
      """R2: behavior in Phase 3 NEVER local — must escalate."""
      crit = self._crit(type_="behavior", method="cmd")
      result = RunResult(status="fail", exit_code=1, duration_ms=5)
      d = self._runner().evaluate_criterion(crit, phase=3, runner_result=result)
      self.assertEqual(d, EvalDecision.BLOCKED_ESCALATE_ROW6)

  def test_phase3_e2e_fail_escalates_row6(self):
      crit = self._crit(type_="e2e", method="cmd")
      result = RunResult(status="fail", exit_code=1,
                         duration_ms=5, escalate=True)
      d = self._runner().evaluate_criterion(crit, phase=3, runner_result=result)
      self.assertEqual(d, EvalDecision.BLOCKED_ESCALATE_ROW6)

  def test_phase3_unit_fail_blocks_row5_no_retry(self):
      """Post-merge verify: unit fail blocks but does NOT enter retry whitelist."""
      crit = self._crit(type_="unit", method="cmd")
      result = RunResult(status="fail", exit_code=1, duration_ms=5)
      d = self._runner().evaluate_criterion(crit, phase=3, runner_result=result)
      self.assertEqual(d, EvalDecision.BLOCK_ROW5)
      self.assertNotEqual(d, EvalDecision.LOCAL_FIX_ALLOWED)
  ```

- [ ] **Step 8.5: New ship-required smoke `test_acceptance_retry_matrix.py`**

  Per design §7 line 314: 11 ship-required smokes. This one fuzzes the (gate × type × phase) cells in §3 retry table. T8 owns the runner-side decision; orchestrator dispatch (which actually consumes `LOCAL_FIX_ALLOWED` and re-runs the criterion) lives in T13 (codex review whitelist) + T15 (gate harness loop).

  ```python
  # tests/smoke/test_acceptance_retry_matrix.py
  import sys, tempfile, unittest
  from pathlib import Path

  REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent.parent
  sys.path.insert(0, str(REPO_ROOT / "scripts"))
  from flow_acceptance import AcceptanceRunner, RunResult, EvalDecision
  from flow_contract import AcceptanceCriterion


  class TestAcceptanceRetryMatrix(unittest.TestCase):
      """Iterate every (type, phase, status) cell from §3 line 130–137 +
      Y1 e2e routing. Asserts EvalDecision exactly matches the design row."""

      MATRIX = [
          # (type, method, phase, status, escalate, expected)
          # Phase 2 — local-fix-allowed types
          ("unit",        "cmd", 2, "fail",      False, EvalDecision.LOCAL_FIX_ALLOWED),
          ("integration", "cmd", 2, "fail",      False, EvalDecision.LOCAL_FIX_ALLOWED),
          ("behavior",    "cmd", 2, "fail",      False, EvalDecision.LOCAL_FIX_ALLOWED),
          ("smoke",       "cmd", 2, "fail",      False, EvalDecision.LOCAL_FIX_ALLOWED),
          # Phase 2 — never-local types
          ("regression",  "cmd", 2, "fail",      False, EvalDecision.BLOCK_ROW5),
          ("e2e",         "cmd", 2, "fail",      True,  EvalDecision.BLOCKED_ESCALATE_ROW6),
          # Phase 2 — timeout always blocks (e2e escalates per Y1)
          ("unit",        "cmd", 2, "timed_out", False, EvalDecision.BLOCK_ROW5),
          ("e2e",         "cmd", 2, "timed_out", True,  EvalDecision.BLOCKED_ESCALATE_ROW6),
          # Phase 3 — behavior + e2e escalate (R2)
          ("behavior",    "cmd", 3, "fail",      False, EvalDecision.BLOCKED_ESCALATE_ROW6),
          ("e2e",         "cmd", 3, "fail",      True,  EvalDecision.BLOCKED_ESCALATE_ROW6),
          # Phase 3 — unit/integration block (no retry post-merge)
          ("unit",        "cmd", 3, "fail",      False, EvalDecision.BLOCK_ROW5),
          ("integration", "cmd", 3, "fail",      False, EvalDecision.BLOCK_ROW5),
          # Pass propagates regardless of type/phase
          ("unit",        "cmd", 2, "pass",      False, EvalDecision.PASS),
          ("e2e",         "cmd", 3, "pass",      False, EvalDecision.PASS),
      ]

      def test_full_matrix(self):
          with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as td:
              runner = AcceptanceRunner(
                  worktree_root=Path(td), log_dir=Path(td) / "l",
                  slug="d", task_id="T", run_id="r", worktree_id="w",
              )
              for tup in self.MATRIX:
                  type_, method, phase, status, escalate, expected = tup
                  with self.subTest(cell=tup):
                      crit = AcceptanceCriterion(
                          description="x", type=type_, method=method,
                          command="x" if method == "cmd" else None,
                          timeout_sec=30,
                      )
                      result = RunResult(
                          status=status,
                          exit_code=(0 if status == "pass" else 1),
                          duration_ms=5,
                          escalate=escalate,
                      )
                      self.assertEqual(
                          runner.evaluate_criterion(
                              crit, phase=phase, runner_result=result),
                          expected,
                      )


  if __name__ == "__main__":
      unittest.main()
  ```

- [ ] **Step 8.6: New ship-required smoke `test_phase3_behavior_e2e_no_retry.py`**

  Per design §7 line 315: focused R2 enforcement test.

  ```python
  # tests/smoke/test_phase3_behavior_e2e_no_retry.py
  import sys, tempfile, unittest
  from pathlib import Path

  REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent.parent
  sys.path.insert(0, str(REPO_ROOT / "scripts"))
  from flow_acceptance import AcceptanceRunner, RunResult, EvalDecision
  from flow_contract import AcceptanceCriterion


  class TestPhase3BehaviorE2eNoRetry(unittest.TestCase):
      """R2: in Phase 3 (post-merge verify), behavior and e2e MUST always
      escalate — never enter LOCAL_FIX_ALLOWED, regardless of status."""

      def setUp(self):
          self.tmp = tempfile.mkdtemp()
          self.addCleanup(lambda: __import__("shutil").rmtree(self.tmp))
          self.runner = AcceptanceRunner(
              worktree_root=Path(self.tmp), log_dir=Path(self.tmp) / "l",
              slug="d", task_id="T", run_id="r", worktree_id="w",
          )

      def _crit(self, type_):
          return AcceptanceCriterion(
              description="x", type=type_, method="cmd",
              command="bash tests/smoke/run.sh", timeout_sec=600,
          )

      def test_phase3_behavior_fail_never_local(self):
          for status in ("fail", "timed_out"):
              with self.subTest(status=status):
                  result = RunResult(status=status, duration_ms=5)
                  d = self.runner.evaluate_criterion(
                      self._crit("behavior"), phase=3, runner_result=result)
                  self.assertNotEqual(d, EvalDecision.LOCAL_FIX_ALLOWED)
                  self.assertEqual(d, EvalDecision.BLOCKED_ESCALATE_ROW6)

      def test_phase3_e2e_fail_never_local(self):
          for status in ("fail", "timed_out"):
              with self.subTest(status=status):
                  # T7 sets escalate=True for e2e fail/timeout
                  result = RunResult(status=status, duration_ms=5, escalate=True)
                  d = self.runner.evaluate_criterion(
                      self._crit("e2e"), phase=3, runner_result=result)
                  self.assertNotEqual(d, EvalDecision.LOCAL_FIX_ALLOWED)
                  self.assertEqual(d, EvalDecision.BLOCKED_ESCALATE_ROW6)

      def test_phase2_behavior_fail_DOES_allow_local(self):
          """Sibling assertion: Phase 2 behavior IS allowed local fix (R1)."""
          result = RunResult(status="fail", duration_ms=5)
          d = self.runner.evaluate_criterion(
              self._crit("behavior"), phase=2, runner_result=result)
          self.assertEqual(d, EvalDecision.LOCAL_FIX_ALLOWED)


  if __name__ == "__main__":
      unittest.main()
  ```

  ```bash
      - status=pass → PASS regardless of type/phase.
  ```

### Task 9: In-flight resume + override resolution + idempotent classification

**Files:**
- Modify: `scripts/flow_acceptance.py` (add resume + override resolver)
- Create: `tests/unit/test_idempotent_in_flight_resume.py` (ship-required unit)
- Modify: `tests/smoke/run.sh` — extend test discovery to `tests/unit/test_*.py`

**Design refs:** §6 Q6.1 (resume from #N (last completed + 1) via `acceptance-progress.jsonl` tail-scan; codex-refined: `started` + `completed` events), §6 R8 hardened (in-flight idempotency table — auto-rerun vs block per (method, default-or-override, in-flight-status) cell), §6 Y8 (lock-state context informs resume — orchestrator already passed through `detect_auto_prepare_state` from T5 before reaching T9), §3 Q3.1 (baseline runs inside worktree — affects retry-attempt boundary, not in-flight scope).

**Goal:** Wire two new pieces on `AcceptanceRunner`:

1. **`find_resume_point(task_dir, attempt_id)`** — tail-scans `acceptance-progress.jsonl`, returns `ResumePoint(next_idx, in_flight_criterion_idx, in_flight_event)`. If `started` exists with no matching `completed`/`timeout` for the same `(attempt_id, criterion_idx)`, the criterion was in-flight when the orchestrator crashed.

2. **`resolve_in_flight_idempotency(criterion, contract, in_flight_event)`** — applies the R8 hardened table to decide `auto_rerun` vs `block`. Inputs: criterion's method+type, contract's `idempotent_cmd_allowlist`, criterion's `idempotent` override object, the in-flight event recovered by `find_resume_point`. Output: `IdempotencyVerdict(decision, reason)` where `decision ∈ {auto_rerun, block_in_flight}` and `reason` is human-readable for the `blocked.md` body.

(`tests/unit/` is new in v0.8.1; this task adds the directory + extends `tests/smoke/run.sh` to discover it.)

**R8 in-flight idempotency table (per design line 268–275)**:

| Method | Default | Override path | In-flight-after-crash policy |
|--------|---------|---------------|------------------------------|
| `file_exists` | idempotent (read-only) | n/a | safe — auto-rerun |
| `json_query` | idempotent (read-only) | n/a | safe — auto-rerun |
| `cmd` | **non-idempotent** | (a) command binary in `contract.idempotent_cmd_allowlist`; OR (b) per-criterion `idempotent: {value, rationale, timeout_sec, side_effect_class}` | block unless overridden via (a) or (b) |
| `http` | GET=idempotent / POST/PUT/PATCH/DELETE=non-idempotent (RFC 7231) | per-criterion `idempotent: {...}` (same shape as cmd) | by default; override via field |
| `e2e` (type) | always non-idempotent | **NO override accepted** (PRD §1.3) | always block on in-flight interrupt |

**Ordering with T5**: orchestrator's startup sequence is `detect_auto_prepare_state` (T5) → if `state ∈ {clean_post_engagement, no_run}` and contract has `acceptance_criteria` → `find_resume_point` (T9). T9 does not re-derive lock state.

- [ ] **Step 9.1: Failing test — `find_resume_point` with no events returns idx=0**

  Create `tests/unit/test_idempotent_in_flight_resume.py`:

  ```python
  import os, sys, tempfile, unittest
  from pathlib import Path

  REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent.parent
  sys.path.insert(0, str(REPO_ROOT / "scripts"))
  from flow_acceptance import (
      AcceptanceRunner, ResumePoint, IdempotencyVerdict,
  )
  from flow_contract import AcceptanceCriterion, Contract
  from flow_state_writer import (
      AcceptanceProgressEvent, append_acceptance_progress,
  )


  class TestFindResumePoint(unittest.TestCase):
      def setUp(self):
          self.tmp = tempfile.mkdtemp()
          self.addCleanup(lambda: __import__("shutil").rmtree(self.tmp))
          self.runner = AcceptanceRunner(
              worktree_root=Path(self.tmp), log_dir=Path(self.tmp) / "l",
              slug="d", task_id="T", run_id="r", worktree_id="w",
          )

      def test_no_events_resume_at_zero(self):
          rp = self.runner.find_resume_point(Path(self.tmp), attempt_id="a1")
          self.assertEqual(rp.next_idx, 0)
          self.assertIsNone(rp.in_flight_criterion_idx)

      def test_completed_chain_resumes_at_next(self):
          for idx in (0, 1, 2):
              # Use shared fixture builder to write started + completed
              self._write_completed_pair(idx, attempt_id="a1")
          rp = self.runner.find_resume_point(Path(self.tmp), attempt_id="a1")
          self.assertEqual(rp.next_idx, 3)
          self.assertIsNone(rp.in_flight_criterion_idx)

      def test_started_without_completed_marks_in_flight(self):
          self._write_completed_pair(0, attempt_id="a1")
          self._write_started_only(1, attempt_id="a1")
          rp = self.runner.find_resume_point(Path(self.tmp), attempt_id="a1")
          self.assertEqual(rp.in_flight_criterion_idx, 1)
          self.assertEqual(rp.in_flight_event["criterion_idx"], 1)

      def test_other_attempts_ignored(self):
          """Different attempt_id (e.g., prior retry) does NOT count
          as in-flight for the current attempt."""
          self._write_completed_pair(0, attempt_id="prior")
          self._write_started_only(1, attempt_id="prior")
          rp = self.runner.find_resume_point(Path(self.tmp), attempt_id="current")
          self.assertEqual(rp.next_idx, 0)
          self.assertIsNone(rp.in_flight_criterion_idx)
  ```

- [ ] **Step 9.2: Implement `ResumePoint` + `find_resume_point`**

  ```python
  @dataclass
  class ResumePoint:
      next_idx: int                         # criterion_idx to start from
      in_flight_criterion_idx: Optional[int]  # None if no crash mid-criterion
      in_flight_event: Optional[dict]       # the started event (raw json) if any


  class AcceptanceRunner:
      ...

      def find_resume_point(
          self, task_dir: Path, *, attempt_id: str,
      ) -> ResumePoint:
          """Tail-scan acceptance-progress.jsonl for the given attempt_id.
          Returns where to resume + whether a criterion was in-flight when
          the orchestrator crashed.
          """
          path = task_dir / "acceptance-progress.jsonl"
          if not path.is_file():
              return ResumePoint(0, None, None)

          # Per-criterion last-seen event (within this attempt)
          last_event_per_idx: dict[int, dict] = {}
          for line in path.read_text(encoding="utf-8").splitlines():
              try:
                  rec = json.loads(line)
              except json.JSONDecodeError:
                  continue
              if rec.get("attempt_id") != attempt_id:
                  continue
              idx = rec.get("criterion_idx")
              if not isinstance(idx, int):
                  continue
              # Newer event for the same idx supersedes older
              last_event_per_idx[idx] = rec

          # Find in-flight (started without matching completed/timeout)
          in_flight_idx = None
          in_flight_event = None
          completed_indices: set[int] = set()
          for idx, ev in last_event_per_idx.items():
              if ev.get("event") == "started":
                  in_flight_idx = idx
                  in_flight_event = ev
              elif ev.get("event") in ("completed", "timeout"):
                  completed_indices.add(idx)

          # next_idx = max(completed) + 1 OR 0 if none completed
          next_idx = (max(completed_indices) + 1) if completed_indices else 0
          # If in_flight is at an idx <= last completed, the in-flight
          # event is stale (came from a prior, retried iteration);
          # treat it as None.
          if in_flight_idx is not None and in_flight_idx < next_idx:
              in_flight_idx = None
              in_flight_event = None

          return ResumePoint(next_idx, in_flight_idx, in_flight_event)
  ```

  Re-run Step 9.1 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 9.3: Failing tests — `resolve_in_flight_idempotency` for R8 cells**

  Iterate every (method, type, override-state) cell from design line 268–275:

  ```python
  class TestResolveInFlightIdempotency(unittest.TestCase):
      def setUp(self):
          self.tmp = tempfile.mkdtemp()
          self.addCleanup(lambda: __import__("shutil").rmtree(self.tmp))
          self.runner = AcceptanceRunner(
              worktree_root=Path(self.tmp), log_dir=Path(self.tmp) / "l",
              slug="d", task_id="T", run_id="r", worktree_id="w",
          )

      def _contract(self, **overrides) -> Contract:
          # Minimal Contract instance — only fields read by the resolver.
          return Contract(
              contract_schema_version=1, autonomy_mode="auto",
              created_at="2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
              **overrides,
          )

      def _crit(self, **kw):
          return AcceptanceCriterion(
              description="x", type=kw.get("type", "unit"),
              method=kw.get("method", "cmd"),
              command=kw.get("command", "true"),
              path=kw.get("path"),
              url=kw.get("url"),
              json_query=kw.get("json_query"),
              timeout_sec=kw.get("timeout_sec", 30),
              idempotent=kw.get("idempotent"),
          )

      # --- read-only methods always auto-rerun ---
      def test_file_exists_in_flight_auto_reruns(self):
          v = self.runner.resolve_in_flight_idempotency(
              self._crit(method="file_exists", path="VERSION"),
              contract=self._contract(),
              in_flight_event={"event": "started"})
          self.assertEqual(v.decision, "auto_rerun")

      def test_json_query_in_flight_auto_reruns(self):
          v = self.runner.resolve_in_flight_idempotency(
              self._crit(method="json_query", path="c.json", json_query="x"),
              contract=self._contract(),
              in_flight_event={"event": "started"})
          self.assertEqual(v.decision, "auto_rerun")

      # --- cmd: default block; allowlist or rationale unblocks ---
      def test_cmd_in_flight_default_blocks(self):
          v = self.runner.resolve_in_flight_idempotency(
              self._crit(method="cmd", command="rm -rf build"),
              contract=self._contract(),
              in_flight_event={"event": "started"})
          self.assertEqual(v.decision, "block_in_flight")
          self.assertIn("non-idempotent", v.reason.lower())

      def test_cmd_in_flight_allowlist_unblocks(self):
          v = self.runner.resolve_in_flight_idempotency(
              self._crit(method="cmd", command="pytest tests/smoke"),
              contract=self._contract(idempotent_cmd_allowlist=[
                  "pytest", "mypy"]),
              in_flight_event={"event": "started"})
          self.assertEqual(v.decision, "auto_rerun")
          self.assertIn("allowlist", v.reason.lower())

      def test_cmd_in_flight_rationale_unblocks(self):
          v = self.runner.resolve_in_flight_idempotency(
              self._crit(method="cmd", command="curl -s http://x/health",
                         idempotent={
                             "value": True,
                             "rationale": "GET against stub",
                             "timeout_sec": 30,
                             "side_effect_class": "read_only",
                         }),
              contract=self._contract(),
              in_flight_event={"event": "started"})
          self.assertEqual(v.decision, "auto_rerun")

      def test_cmd_rationale_value_false_does_not_unblock(self):
          v = self.runner.resolve_in_flight_idempotency(
              self._crit(method="cmd", command="x",
                         idempotent={
                             "value": False,
                             "rationale": "side effects",
                             "timeout_sec": 30,
                             "side_effect_class": "reversible",
                         }),
              contract=self._contract(),
              in_flight_event={"event": "started"})
          self.assertEqual(v.decision, "block_in_flight")

      # --- e2e: ALWAYS block (no override accepted; design line 275) ---
      def test_e2e_type_always_blocks_no_override(self):
          v = self.runner.resolve_in_flight_idempotency(
              self._crit(type="e2e", method="cmd",
                         command="playwright test",
                         idempotent={
                             "value": True,
                             "rationale": "stub-only",
                             "timeout_sec": 30,
                             "side_effect_class": "read_only",
                         }),
              contract=self._contract(idempotent_cmd_allowlist=["playwright"]),
              in_flight_event={"event": "started"})
          self.assertEqual(v.decision, "block_in_flight")
          self.assertIn("e2e", v.reason.lower())
  ```

- [ ] **Step 9.4: Implement `IdempotencyVerdict` + `resolve_in_flight_idempotency`**

  ```python
  @dataclass
  class IdempotencyVerdict:
      decision: str   # "auto_rerun" | "block_in_flight"
      reason: str     # human-readable; goes into blocked.md body if block


  class AcceptanceRunner:
      ...

      def resolve_in_flight_idempotency(
          self,
          criterion: AcceptanceCriterion,
          *,
          contract,  # Contract — type-imported lazily to avoid circular
          in_flight_event: dict,
      ) -> IdempotencyVerdict:
          """R8 hardened decision: given a criterion that was in-flight when
          the orchestrator crashed, decide whether to auto-rerun or block.

          e2e bypasses overrides (design line 275). Read-only methods always
          rerun. cmd defaults to block; rationale-object OR allowlist
          unblocks. http defaults follow GET=rerun rule (non-GET awaits
          v0.8.2 http_method field).
          """
          # 1. e2e type bypass — always block, no override.
          if criterion.type == "e2e":
              return IdempotencyVerdict(
                  "block_in_flight",
                  "e2e type is always non-idempotent (PRD §1.3); "
                  "no override accepted on in-flight interrupt",
              )

          # 2. Read-only methods: rerun.
          if criterion.method in ("file_exists", "json_query"):
              return IdempotencyVerdict(
                  "auto_rerun",
                  f"{criterion.method} is read-only; safe to rerun",
              )

          # 3. http: GET-only in T7 → safe by default. Non-GET deferred.
          if criterion.method == "http":
              return IdempotencyVerdict(
                  "auto_rerun",
                  "http GET is idempotent per RFC 7231; "
                  "non-GET methods land with v0.8.2 http_method field",
              )

          # 4. cmd: default block. Two override paths.
          if criterion.method == "cmd":
              # 4a. per-criterion idempotent override (R8 rationale path)
              idem = criterion.idempotent
              if (isinstance(idem, dict)
                      and idem.get("value") is True
                      and idem.get("rationale")):
                  return IdempotencyVerdict(
                      "auto_rerun",
                      f"per-criterion override: {idem['rationale']!r} "
                      f"(side_effect_class={idem.get('side_effect_class')})",
                  )

              # 4b. allowlist match
              binary = (criterion.command or "").strip().split()[:1]
              binary = binary[0] if binary else ""
              for allowed in (contract.idempotent_cmd_allowlist or ()):
                  if binary == allowed or (criterion.command or "").startswith(allowed + " "):
                      return IdempotencyVerdict(
                          "auto_rerun",
                          f"command starts with allowlist entry {allowed!r}",
                      )

              return IdempotencyVerdict(
                  "block_in_flight",
                  f"cmd is non-idempotent by default (R8); no allowlist match "
                  f"for {binary!r} and no per-criterion rationale",
              )

          return IdempotencyVerdict(
              "block_in_flight",
              f"unknown method {criterion.method!r}; conservative block",
          )
  ```

  Re-run Step 9.3 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 9.5: Failing test — `resume_attempt` end-to-end (find_resume_point + classify + dispatch)**

  ```python
  class TestResumeAttempt(unittest.TestCase):
      def setUp(self):
          self.tmp = tempfile.mkdtemp()
          self.addCleanup(lambda: __import__("shutil").rmtree(self.tmp))
          self.runner = AcceptanceRunner(
              worktree_root=Path(self.tmp), log_dir=Path(self.tmp) / "l",
              slug="d", task_id="T", run_id="r", worktree_id="w",
          )

      def test_resume_with_in_flight_safe_method_continues(self):
          """file_exists in-flight → resume continues."""
          (Path(self.tmp) / "VERSION").write_text("0.8.1\n")
          # Simulate a crash: write started but no completed for idx=1
          self._write_completed_pair(0, attempt_id="a1")
          self._write_started_only(1, attempt_id="a1",
              type="smoke", method="file_exists", path="VERSION")
          contract = self._contract()
          criteria = [
              # idx=0 already completed; idx=1 in-flight; idx=2 fresh
              self._crit(),
              self._crit(method="file_exists", path="VERSION", type="smoke"),
              self._crit(),
          ]
          verdict, resume_point = self.runner.resume_attempt(
              Path(self.tmp), attempt_id="a1",
              criteria=criteria, contract=contract,
          )
          self.assertEqual(verdict.decision, "auto_rerun")
          self.assertEqual(resume_point.in_flight_criterion_idx, 1)

      def test_resume_with_in_flight_unsafe_cmd_blocks(self):
          self._write_started_only(0, attempt_id="a1",
              type="unit", method="cmd")
          contract = self._contract()  # empty allowlist by default? No — default has pytest etc.
          criteria = [self._crit(command="rm -rf build")]
          verdict, _ = self.runner.resume_attempt(
              Path(self.tmp), attempt_id="a1",
              criteria=criteria, contract=contract,
          )
          self.assertEqual(verdict.decision, "block_in_flight")
  ```

- [ ] **Step 9.6: Implement `resume_attempt` orchestration helper**

  ```python
  def resume_attempt(
      self,
      task_dir: Path,
      *,
      attempt_id: str,
      criteria: list[AcceptanceCriterion],
      contract,
  ) -> tuple[IdempotencyVerdict, ResumePoint]:
      """Convenience: orchestrator calls this after detect_auto_prepare_state
      reports clean_post_engagement OR a fresh start. Returns:
        - IdempotencyVerdict: auto_rerun (caller proceeds from next_idx OR
          re-runs in_flight_criterion_idx) OR block_in_flight (caller writes
          blocked.md per §6 R8).
        - ResumePoint: where to resume in the criteria list.
      No in-flight criterion → IdempotencyVerdict("auto_rerun", "no in-flight").
      """
      rp = self.find_resume_point(task_dir, attempt_id=attempt_id)
      if rp.in_flight_criterion_idx is None:
          return (
              IdempotencyVerdict("auto_rerun", "no in-flight criterion"),
              rp,
          )
      criterion = criteria[rp.in_flight_criterion_idx]
      verdict = self.resolve_in_flight_idempotency(
          criterion, contract=contract, in_flight_event=rp.in_flight_event,
      )
      return (verdict, rp)
  ```

  Re-run Step 9.5 → PASS.

### Task 10: Worktree creation + naming + dual-base + orchestrator-derives-facts

**Files:**
- Modify: `scripts/flow_orchestrator.py`
- Create: `tests/smoke/test_orchestrator_worktree.py`

**Design refs:** §4 Q4.1 (`<slug>+t<n>+<shortsha>` naming; shortsha from base commit at create-time, stable across retries), §4 S6 (dual base commit recording: `original_base_commit` + `current_base_commit`), PRD §1.2 (orchestrator-derives-facts: subagent narrative only — facts come from git diff + test logs).

**Goal:** Replace v0.8.0's `--auto-execute` exit-2 stub with the real per-task worktree creation step. For each task the orchestrator (a) creates `.claude/worktrees/<slug>+t<n>+<shortsha>/` from `git worktree add`, (b) records dual-base commits + worktree id in a `WorktreeContext` value object, (c) on subagent return, **ignores** the subagent's self-report fields and instead reads `git diff` + test log paths to derive `final_diff_hash`, `target_commit_pre_merge`, etc. T10 also wires the `auto_engaged` event emission (per §7 Q7.2 + §8.4 R6+Y3 14-field schema) BEFORE first subagent dispatch — boundary must exist even if dispatch crashes immediately.

**`WorktreeContext` schema**:

```python
@dataclass
class WorktreeContext:
    slug: str
    task_idx: int                      # zero-based — the t<n> in branch name
    worktree_id: str                   # = `<slug>+t<n>+<shortsha>`
    worktree_path: Path
    branch: str                        # same as worktree_id
    integration_target: str            # parent branch (e.g., master)
    original_base_commit: str          # full sha at creation
    current_base_commit: str           # full sha after any rebase (S6)
    base_shortsha: str                 # 7-char short of original
    lifecycle_state: str               # active | merging | merged | aborted | blocked
    created_at: str                    # ISO 8601
```

**Subagent boundary (DECIDED PRD §1.2)**: orchestrator's contract with the subagent is:
- Subagent receives a per-task prompt + worktree path + scope manifest.
- Subagent returns ONLY a free-form narrative summary (no structured fields).
- Orchestrator reads facts from disk: `git diff <original_base_commit>..HEAD` for changed files; `git rev-parse HEAD` for `target_commit_pre_merge`; baseline + acceptance log paths for fail set.

T10 lands the worktree + `derive_task_facts` infrastructure; T11+ wire the gates that consume the facts.

- [ ] **Step 10.1: Failing test — `create_task_worktree` builds path with shortsha**

  ```python
  # tests/smoke/test_orchestrator_worktree.py
  import json, os, subprocess, sys, tempfile, unittest
  from pathlib import Path

  REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent.parent
  sys.path.insert(0, str(REPO_ROOT / "scripts"))
  from flow_orchestrator import (  # type: ignore
      WorktreeContext, create_task_worktree, derive_task_facts,
  )


  class TestCreateTaskWorktree(unittest.TestCase):
      def setUp(self):
          self.tmp = tempfile.mkdtemp()
          self.addCleanup(lambda: __import__("shutil").rmtree(self.tmp))
          # init a fresh git repo for the test (orchestrator's `git worktree
          # add` requires a real repo).
          subprocess.run(["git", "init", "-q", "-b", "master", self.tmp], check=True)
          subprocess.run(["git", "-C", self.tmp, "config", "user.email", "x@y"], check=True)
          subprocess.run(["git", "-C", self.tmp, "config", "user.name", "x"], check=True)
          (Path(self.tmp) / "VERSION").write_text("0.0.0\n")
          subprocess.run(["git", "-C", self.tmp, "add", "."], check=True)
          subprocess.run(["git", "-C", self.tmp, "commit", "-q", "-m", "init"], check=True)

      def test_worktree_id_uses_shortsha_naming(self):
          ctx = create_task_worktree(
              repo_root=Path(self.tmp), slug="demo",
              task_idx=1, integration_target="master",
          )
          self.assertEqual(ctx.task_idx, 1)
          self.assertTrue(ctx.worktree_id.startswith("demo+t1+"))
          # 7-char shortsha
          self.assertEqual(len(ctx.worktree_id.split("+")[-1]), 7)
          self.assertTrue(ctx.worktree_path.is_dir())
          self.assertEqual(ctx.lifecycle_state, "active")

      def test_dual_base_commits_match_at_creation(self):
          ctx = create_task_worktree(
              repo_root=Path(self.tmp), slug="demo",
              task_idx=0, integration_target="master",
          )
          # S6: at creation, original == current.
          self.assertEqual(ctx.original_base_commit, ctx.current_base_commit)
          self.assertEqual(len(ctx.original_base_commit), 40)  # full sha
  ```

  Run → `ImportError`.

- [ ] **Step 10.2: Implement `WorktreeContext` + `create_task_worktree`**

  ```python
  WORKTREE_ROOT = Path(".claude/worktrees")  # relative to repo root


  @dataclass
  class WorktreeContext:
      slug: str
      task_idx: int
      worktree_id: str
      worktree_path: Path
      branch: str
      integration_target: str
      original_base_commit: str
      current_base_commit: str
      base_shortsha: str
      lifecycle_state: str
      created_at: str


  def _git(repo_root: Path, *args: str, check: bool = True) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess:
      return subprocess.run(
          ["git", "-C", str(repo_root), *args],
          check=check, capture_output=True, text=True,
      )


  def create_task_worktree(
      *, repo_root: Path, slug: str, task_idx: int, integration_target: str,
  ) -> WorktreeContext:
      """§4 Q4.1: name = `<slug>+t<n>+<shortsha>`. shortsha from
      integration_target HEAD at create-time, stable for retries.
      S6: record both original and current base commit.
      """
      head = _git(repo_root, "rev-parse", integration_target).stdout.strip()
      shortsha = head[:7]
      worktree_id = f"{slug}+t{task_idx}+{shortsha}"
      worktree_path = repo_root / WORKTREE_ROOT / worktree_id
      worktree_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
      _git(repo_root, "worktree", "add", "-b", worktree_id,
           str(worktree_path), integration_target)
      now = datetime.datetime.now(datetime.UTC).strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ")
      return WorktreeContext(
          slug=slug, task_idx=task_idx,
          worktree_id=worktree_id, worktree_path=worktree_path,
          branch=worktree_id, integration_target=integration_target,
          original_base_commit=head, current_base_commit=head,
          base_shortsha=shortsha, lifecycle_state="active", created_at=now,
      )
  ```

  Add `import datetime`, `import subprocess` to top-of-file imports if missing.

  Re-run Step 10.1 → PASS.

  ```python
  def test_derive_task_facts_reads_git_diff(self):

          repo_root=Path(self.tmp), slug="demo",

                      "commit", "-q", "-m", "add feature"], check=True)
      facts = derive_task_facts(ctx)
      self.assertIn("feature.py", facts.changed_files)
      self.assertNotEqual(facts.target_commit_pre_merge, ctx.original_base_commit)
  ```

- [ ] **Step 10.4: Implement `TaskFacts` + `derive_task_facts`**

  ```python
  @dataclass
  class TaskFacts:
      changed_files: list[str]
      diff_hash: str                      # sha256 over the unified diff bytes
      target_commit_pre_merge: str        # worktree HEAD after subagent
      newly_added_files: list[str]


  def derive_task_facts(ctx: WorktreeContext) -> TaskFacts:
      """PRD §1.2: facts come from disk, not subagent self-report.
      Diff is computed against `current_base_commit` (S6 dual-base — handles
      stale-rebase case correctly: branch name shortsha is original, but
      facts must compare to wherever HEAD started for THIS attempt).
      """
      diff = _git(ctx.worktree_path, "diff", "--unified=0",
                  f"{ctx.current_base_commit}..HEAD").stdout
      diff_hash = hashlib.sha256(diff.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
      changed_files = _git(
          ctx.worktree_path, "diff", "--name-only",
          f"{ctx.current_base_commit}..HEAD",
      ).stdout.strip().splitlines()
      newly = _git(
          ctx.worktree_path, "diff", "--name-only", "--diff-filter=A",
          f"{ctx.current_base_commit}..HEAD",
      ).stdout.strip().splitlines()
      head = _git(ctx.worktree_path, "rev-parse", "HEAD").stdout.strip()
      return TaskFacts(
          changed_files=changed_files,
          diff_hash=diff_hash,
          target_commit_pre_merge=head,
          newly_added_files=newly,
      )
  ```

  Add `import hashlib` to imports. Re-run Step 10.3 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 10.6: Implement `auto_dispatch_task` orchestration shell**

  ```python
  def auto_dispatch_task(
      *, slug: str, task_idx: int, repo_root: Path,
      dispatch_fn,                # callable(ctx, **kw) → TaskFacts
      contract,                   # parsed Contract
      run_id: str,
      contract_path: Path,
      contract_hash: str,
      integration_target: str = "master",
  ) -> TaskFacts:
      """T10's orchestration shell:
      1. create worktree (S6 dual-base).
      2. emit auto_engaged event (Q7.2 + §8.4 R6+Y3).
      3. invoke dispatch_fn(ctx, ...) — opaque subagent boundary.
      4. derive_task_facts() — orchestrator reads, never trusts narrative.
      Steps 5+ (manifest verify / gates / merge / cleanup) live in T11–T15.
      """
      task_dir = repo_root / ".flow" / "tasks" / slug
      ctx = create_task_worktree(
          repo_root=repo_root, slug=slug,
          task_idx=task_idx, integration_target=integration_target,
      )
      append_autonomy_event(task_dir, EVENT_AUTO_ENGAGED, {
          "event_id": _new_event_id(),
          "ts": ctx.created_at,
          "slug": slug,
          "run_id": run_id,
          "task_id": f"T{task_idx}",
          "worktree_id": ctx.worktree_id,
          "worktree_path": str(ctx.worktree_path),
          "original_base_commit": ctx.original_base_commit,
          "current_base_commit": ctx.current_base_commit,
          "lifecycle_state": ctx.lifecycle_state,
          "checkpoint_id": None,
          "contract_path": str(contract_path),
          "contract_hash": contract_hash,
          "contract_schema_version": contract.contract_schema_version,
      })
      # Invoke subagent (orchestrator-as-coordinator boundary)
      dispatch_fn(ctx)
      # Authoritative facts from disk
      return derive_task_facts(ctx)
  ```

  Add imports: `from flow_state_writer import (EVENT_AUTO_ENGAGED, append_autonomy_event, _new_event_id)`. Re-run Step 10.5 → PASS.

### Task 11: Manifest violation enforcement (replaces v0.8.0 dry-run)

**Files:**
- Modify: `scripts/flow_orchestrator.py`
- Modify: `tests/smoke/test_orchestrator_worktree.py`

**Design refs:** §1 row 3 (manifest violation: file outside `scope.allowed` → block), §1 row 4 (manifest violation: untracked file outside scope → block), §6 R3 manifest-detect timing (run AFTER subagent return, BEFORE gate 4).

**Goal:** v0.8.0's `build_plan()` computes `forbidden_hits / shared_hits / out_of_scope` for **declared** writes (from `progress.md` `### Tasks` block). T11 extends this from advisory dry-run to enforcement: after `derive_task_facts()` returns, the orchestrator runs `verify_manifest_against_facts(ctx, manifest, facts)`. Any forbidden / out-of-scope file in `facts.changed_files` → `block` (§1 row 3+4). `shared_hits` is NOT a block (§1 row 14 wording is `shared` artifacts → serialize, not violate); kept as advisory and surfaced via Tier 1 message body.

**Verification rules**:

| Check | Source | Action on hit |
|-------|--------|---------------|
| forbidden_hits in facts.changed_files | contract.scope_forbidden globs | `block` row 3 |
| out_of_scope in facts.changed_files | NOT in `scope.allowed` AND NOT in SHARED_ARTIFACTS | `block` row 3 |
| untracked file added outside scope | facts.newly_added_files filtered by allowed/SHARED | `block` row 4 |
| shared_hits | SHARED_ARTIFACTS | warn-only; serialize via wave queue (T15 S1 logic for cross-task; not a block) |

T10's `verify_manifest_against_facts` returns a `ManifestVerdict`. Orchestrator dispatch loop (T15) consumes the verdict.

- [ ] **Step 11.1: Failing tests — `verify_manifest_against_facts` rejects forbidden + out-of-scope**

  Add to `test_orchestrator_worktree.py`:

  ```python
  class TestVerifyManifestAgainstFacts(unittest.TestCase):
      def setUp(self):
          self.contract = Contract(
              contract_schema_version=1, autonomy_mode="auto",
              created_at="2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
              scope_allowed=["src/**", "tests/**"],
              scope_forbidden=["src/secrets/**"],
          )
          self.manifest = TaskManifest(
              id="T1", writes_declared=["src/foo.py"],
              allowed_writes=["src/foo.py"],
              out_of_scope=[], forbidden_hits=[], shared_hits=[],
          )

      def test_forbidden_path_in_facts_blocks(self):
          facts = TaskFacts(
              changed_files=["src/foo.py", "src/secrets/key.pem"],
              newly_added_files=[], diff_hash="x", target_commit_pre_merge="y",
          )
          v = verify_manifest_against_facts(self.contract, self.manifest, facts)
          self.assertEqual(v.decision, "block")
          self.assertEqual(v.block_row, 3)
          self.assertIn("src/secrets/key.pem", v.violations)

      def test_out_of_scope_in_facts_blocks(self):
          facts = TaskFacts(
              changed_files=["src/foo.py", "infra/deploy.yml"],
              newly_added_files=[], diff_hash="x", target_commit_pre_merge="y",
          )
          v = verify_manifest_against_facts(self.contract, self.manifest, facts)
          self.assertEqual(v.decision, "block")
          self.assertEqual(v.block_row, 3)
          self.assertIn("infra/deploy.yml", v.violations)

      def test_untracked_added_outside_scope_blocks_row4(self):
          facts = TaskFacts(
              changed_files=["src/foo.py", "scripts/rogue.sh"],
              newly_added_files=["scripts/rogue.sh"],
              diff_hash="x", target_commit_pre_merge="y",
          )
          v = verify_manifest_against_facts(self.contract, self.manifest, facts)
          self.assertEqual(v.decision, "block")
          self.assertEqual(v.block_row, 4)

      def test_shared_artifact_warns_not_blocks(self):
          facts = TaskFacts(
              changed_files=["src/foo.py", "VERSION"],
              newly_added_files=[], diff_hash="x", target_commit_pre_merge="y",
          )
          v = verify_manifest_against_facts(self.contract, self.manifest, facts)
          self.assertEqual(v.decision, "pass")
          self.assertIn("VERSION", v.shared_artifacts_touched)

      def test_clean_facts_pass(self):
          facts = TaskFacts(
              changed_files=["src/foo.py", "tests/test_foo.py"],
              newly_added_files=["tests/test_foo.py"],
              diff_hash="x", target_commit_pre_merge="y",
          )
          v = verify_manifest_against_facts(self.contract, self.manifest, facts)
          self.assertEqual(v.decision, "pass")
          self.assertEqual(v.violations, [])
  ```

- [ ] **Step 11.2: Implement `ManifestVerdict` + `verify_manifest_against_facts`**

  ```python
  @dataclass
  class ManifestVerdict:
      decision: str                       # "pass" | "block"
      block_row: Optional[int] = None     # §1 row 3 or 4
      violations: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
      shared_artifacts_touched: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)


  def verify_manifest_against_facts(
      contract: Contract,
      manifest: TaskManifest,
      facts: TaskFacts,
  ) -> ManifestVerdict:
      verdict = ManifestVerdict(decision="pass")
      newly_set = set(facts.newly_added_files)

      for path in facts.changed_files:
          if _glob_match(contract.scope_forbidden, path):
              verdict.violations.append(path)
              verdict.decision = "block"
              verdict.block_row = 3
              continue
          if path in SHARED_ARTIFACTS:
              verdict.shared_artifacts_touched.append(path)
              continue
          if (contract.scope_allowed
                  and not _glob_match(contract.scope_allowed, path)):
              verdict.violations.append(path)
              verdict.decision = "block"
              # Row 4 if file is newly added (untracked-style); else row 3
              # (existing-file modification outside scope).
              row = 4 if path in newly_set else 3
              # If we already set a row, prefer the more severe (3 = file
              # outside scope > 4 = untracked outside) — equal severity.
              # Just keep the first row hit unless it's still None.
              if verdict.block_row is None or row < verdict.block_row:
                  verdict.block_row = row
      return verdict
  ```

  Re-run Step 11.1 → PASS.

  ```python
      → blocked.md written + decisions.jsonl block_event."""

      # ... fake_dispatch creates secrets/key.pem inside the worktree ...
      # Run auto_dispatch_task; assert blocked.md exists with block_type=manifest_violation
  ```

- [ ] **Step 11.4: Wire `verify_manifest_against_facts` into `auto_dispatch_task` + return `DispatchOutcome`**

  Extend Step 10.6's `auto_dispatch_task`: (a) accept a `manifest` parameter so the verdict computation has the per-task scope/forbidden globs; (b) accept an optional `notifier` parameter so block routing goes through T16's `Notifier` when the orchestrator entry passes one in; (c) change the return type from `TaskFacts` to a richer `DispatchOutcome` so the caller can branch on `status` without inspecting `blocked.md` on disk.

  ```python
  @dataclass
  class DispatchOutcome:
      """T11 return type: lets the orchestrator dispatch loop branch on
      block vs. ok without re-reading blocked.md from disk. ctx is
      always populated (worktree created); facts is None if dispatch
      itself failed to produce a usable diff (currently never — T10
      always returns facts post-dispatch); blocked_md_path is set only
      when status == "blocked"."""
      status: str                        # "ok" | "blocked"
      ctx: WorktreeContext
      facts: TaskFacts
      block_type: Optional[str] = None
      block_row: Optional[int] = None
      blocked_md_path: Optional[Path] = None


  def auto_dispatch_task(
      *, slug: str, task_idx: int, repo_root: Path,
      dispatch_fn,                       # callable(ctx, **kw) → None
      contract: Contract,
      manifest: TaskManifest,            # T11: per-task scope/forbidden
      run_id: str,
      contract_path: Path,
      contract_hash: str,
      integration_target: str = "master",
      notifier: Optional["Notifier"] = None,   # T16: optional block emitter
  ) -> DispatchOutcome:
      task_dir = repo_root / ".flow" / "tasks" / slug
      ctx = create_task_worktree(
          repo_root=repo_root, slug=slug,
          task_idx=task_idx, integration_target=integration_target,
      )
      append_autonomy_event(task_dir, EVENT_AUTO_ENGAGED, {
          "event_id": _new_event_id(), "ts": ctx.created_at,
          "slug": slug, "run_id": run_id, "task_id": manifest.id,
          "worktree_id": ctx.worktree_id,
          "worktree_path": str(ctx.worktree_path),
          "original_base_commit": ctx.original_base_commit,
          "current_base_commit": ctx.current_base_commit,
          "lifecycle_state": ctx.lifecycle_state,
          "checkpoint_id": None,
          "contract_path": str(contract_path),
          "contract_hash": contract_hash,
          "contract_schema_version": contract.contract_schema_version,
      })
      dispatch_fn(ctx)
      facts = derive_task_facts(ctx)

      verdict = verify_manifest_against_facts(contract, manifest, facts)
      if verdict.decision == "block":
          why = (f"manifest_violation (row {verdict.block_row}): "
                 f"{verdict.violations}")
          choices = ["abort_task", "switch_to_interactive",
                     "extend_scope_with_rationale"]
          resume = f"flow orchestrator --resume {slug}"
          if notifier is not None:
              blocked_md_path = notifier.fire_block(
                  block_type="manifest_violation", phase=2,
                  task_id=manifest.id, issue_id="manifest_violation",
                  why_blocked=why,
                  required_choice=choices,
                  safe_resume_command=resume,
                  frontmatter_extra={"block_row": verdict.block_row},
              )
          else:
              # Test/back-compat path: write_blocked directly when no
              # Notifier wired (e.g., unit tests that don't construct one).
              blocked_md_path = write_blocked(
                  task_dir, phase=2, task=manifest.id,
                  why_blocked=why, required_choice=choices,
                  safe_resume_command=resume,
              )
          return DispatchOutcome(
              status="blocked", ctx=ctx, facts=facts,
              block_type="manifest_violation",
              block_row=verdict.block_row,
              blocked_md_path=blocked_md_path,
          )
      return DispatchOutcome(status="ok", ctx=ctx, facts=facts)
  ```

  Both code paths (Notifier present / Notifier absent) write `blocked.md` — the difference is that the `Notifier` path also fires Tier 2 (OSC 9 + BEL) per T16. Step 19.11's dispatch loop always passes a real `Notifier`; unit tests in this step exercise the back-compat path. The existing Step 11.3 end-to-end test asserts on `blocked.md` content; add an assertion that `outcome.status == "blocked"` and `outcome.block_type == "manifest_violation"` to prove the new return type.

  ```bash
  feat(v0.8.1): manifest violation enforcement on subagent return (T11)

  scripts/flow_orchestrator.py:
    ManifestVerdict + verify_manifest_against_facts(): runs after
    derive_task_facts(). Forbidden glob hit OR out-of-scope path hit →
    block; row 3 (file outside scope) vs row 4 (untracked added outside
    scope) routing per §1. SHARED_ARTIFACTS hits surfaced as
    shared_artifacts_touched (advisory, not block — wave-serialize logic

        `notifier` (T16 Notifier; routes block through Tier 1+2 when
  ```

### Task 12: Gate harness — gates 1, 3, 5, 6 (baseline + manifest + acceptance + regression)

**Files:**
- Modify: `scripts/flow_orchestrator.py`
- Modify: `tests/smoke/test_orchestrator_worktree.py`

**Design refs:** §3 gate 1 (baseline tests inside worktree per Q3.1), §3 gate 3 (manifest verify — wires T11), §3 gate 5 (acceptance criteria — wires T7+T8 `evaluate_criterion`), §3 gate 6 (final regression smoke), §1 Q3.1 (baseline INSIDE worktree to catch state drift), §1 row 7 (baseline newly fail → block).

**Goal:** Add `GateRunner` class that wires 4 of the 8 gates (gates 2, 4, 7, 8 in T13/T14/T15). Each gate returns a `GateResult` with `{status, escalate, details}`. `GateRunner.run_phase2()` chains gates 1, 3, 5, 6 in order; first non-pass result halts and returns (caller routes block per `escalate` flag).

**Per-gate contract**:

| Gate | Owner | Inputs | Output |
|------|-------|--------|--------|
| 1 baseline | T12 | `WorktreeContext`, `BaselineRecord` (from prior run if any) | pass / fail (newly) |
| 3 manifest | T11 (T12 wires) | `Contract`, `TaskManifest`, `TaskFacts` | `ManifestVerdict` |
| 5 acceptance | T8 (T12 wires loop) | `list[AcceptanceCriterion]`, `phase=2` | first non-PASS halts |
| 6 regression | T12 | repo command (e.g., `bash tests/smoke/run.sh`) | pass/fail |

`run_phase2` returns a `Phase2Verdict` summarizing which gate halted (if any).

- [ ] **Step 12.1: Failing test — `GateRunner.gate1_baseline` records pre-existing fails**

  ```python
  class TestGate1Baseline(unittest.TestCase):
      def test_baseline_clean_passes(self):
          # ... worktree fixture with passing test suite ...
          gr = GateRunner(ctx=ctx, contract=contract, task_dir=task_dir,
                          run_id="r", task_id="T0")
          r = gr.gate1_baseline(test_command="true")  # always passes
          self.assertEqual(r.status, "pass")
          self.assertEqual(r.details["pre_existing_fails"], [])

      def test_baseline_newly_fail_blocks(self):
          """§1 row 7: newly broken baseline → block."""
          gr = GateRunner(ctx=ctx, contract=contract, task_dir=task_dir,
                          run_id="r", task_id="T0",
                          prior_baseline=BaselineRecord(failing=[]))
          r = gr.gate1_baseline(test_command="false")
          self.assertEqual(r.status, "fail")
          self.assertEqual(r.details["block_row"], 7)
  ```

- [ ] **Step 12.2: Implement `GateResult` + `BaselineRecord` + `gate1_baseline`**

  ```python
  @dataclass
  class GateResult:
      status: str                         # pass | fail | inconclusive
      escalate: bool = False              # Y1 e2e fail
      details: dict = field(default_factory=dict)


  @dataclass
  class BaselineRecord:
      failing: list[str]                  # test ids known to fail at start


  class GateRunner:
      def __init__(
          self, *, ctx: WorktreeContext, contract: Contract, task_dir: Path,
          run_id: str, task_id: str,
          prior_baseline: Optional[BaselineRecord] = None,
      ):
          self.ctx = ctx
          self.contract = contract
          self.task_dir = task_dir
          self.run_id = run_id
          self.task_id = task_id
          self.prior_baseline = prior_baseline

      def gate1_baseline(self, *, test_command: str) -> GateResult:
          """Q3.1: run inside the worktree, not main checkout. Catches
          worktree-induced state drift (lockfile diverged, submodule init
          missing). v0.8.1 cost: extra baseline run per worktree.
          """
          proc = subprocess.run(
              test_command, shell=True, cwd=str(self.ctx.worktree_path),
              capture_output=True, text=True,
          )
          if proc.returncode == 0:
              return GateResult("pass", details={"pre_existing_fails": []})
          # Newly failing? Compare against prior_baseline.
          if (self.prior_baseline is None
                  or self.prior_baseline.failing == []):
              # No prior — current fails are pre-existing for THIS run, but
              # since baseline runs at task START, any fail here is "newly
              # broken" relative to the integration target.
              return GateResult(
                  "fail", details={
                      "block_row": 7,
                      "stderr_tail": proc.stderr[-2000:],
                  })
          # Prior baseline existed; if same fail set → carry forward warning,
          # not a block. Out of scope for v0.8.1: full per-test diffing —
          # naive equality check on returncode is the pragmatic shortcut.
          return GateResult(
              "fail", details={
                  "block_row": 7, "stderr_tail": proc.stderr[-2000:],
              })
  ```

  Re-run Step 12.1 → PASS.

  ```python
  def gate3_manifest(
      self, *, manifest: TaskManifest, facts: TaskFacts,
  ) -> GateResult:
      v = verify_manifest_against_facts(self.contract, manifest, facts)
      if v.decision == "pass":
          return GateResult(
              "pass",
              details={"shared": v.shared_artifacts_touched})

          details={"block_row": v.block_row, "violations": v.violations},
  ```

  ```python
  def test_gate5_passes_when_all_criteria_pass(self):
      criteria = [
          AcceptanceCriterion(description="x", type="unit", method="cmd",
                              command="true", timeout_sec=30),
          AcceptanceCriterion(description="y", type="smoke", method="file_exists",
                              path="VERSION", timeout_sec=30),
      ]
      gr = GateRunner(...)
      r = gr.gate5_acceptance(criteria=criteria, attempt_id="a1", retry_idx=0)
      self.assertEqual(r.status, "pass")

  def test_gate5_halts_on_first_blocking_criterion(self):
      criteria = [
          AcceptanceCriterion(description="x", type="unit", method="cmd",
                              command="false", timeout_sec=30),  # fail
          AcceptanceCriterion(description="y", type="unit", method="cmd",
                              command="true", timeout_sec=30),   # would pass
      ]
      gr = GateRunner(...)
      r = gr.gate5_acceptance(criteria=criteria, attempt_id="a1", retry_idx=0)
      # Phase 2 unit fail → LOCAL_FIX_ALLOWED, not "fail" — gate returns
      # status="fail" with details["decision"]=LOCAL_FIX_ALLOWED so caller
      # can choose to retry.
      self.assertEqual(r.status, "fail")
      self.assertEqual(r.details["halted_at_idx"], 0)
      self.assertEqual(r.details["decision"], "local_fix_allowed")
  ```

- [ ] **Step 12.6: Implement `gate5_acceptance`**

  ```python
  def gate5_acceptance(
      self, *,
      criteria: list[AcceptanceCriterion],
      attempt_id: str, retry_idx: int,
  ) -> GateResult:
      """Iterate criteria in declared order; first non-PASS halts.
      Calls T7's run_one + T8's evaluate_criterion(phase=2).
      """
      from flow_acceptance import AcceptanceRunner, EvalDecision  # type: ignore
      runner = AcceptanceRunner(
          worktree_root=self.ctx.worktree_path,
          log_dir=self.task_dir / "logs" / "acceptance",
          slug=self.ctx.slug, task_id=self.task_id, run_id=self.run_id,
          worktree_id=self.ctx.worktree_id,
      )
      for idx, crit in enumerate(criteria):
          result = runner.run_one(
              crit, criterion_idx=idx,
              attempt_id=attempt_id, retry_idx=retry_idx,
              task_dir=self.task_dir,
          )
          decision = runner.evaluate_criterion(
              crit, phase=2, runner_result=result)
          if decision == EvalDecision.PASS:
              continue
          # Halt
          return GateResult(
              status="fail",
              escalate=(decision == EvalDecision.BLOCKED_ESCALATE_ROW6),
              details={
                  "halted_at_idx": idx,
                  "criterion_description": crit.description,
                  "decision": decision.value,
                  "run_status": result.status,
              },
          )
      return GateResult("pass", details={"criteria_count": len(criteria)})
  ```

  Re-run Step 12.5 → PASS.

  ```python
      self.assertIn("block_row", r.details)
  ```

- [ ] **Step 12.8: Implement `gate6_regression` + `run_phase2` chain**

  ```python
  def gate6_regression(self, *, smoke_command: str) -> GateResult:
      proc = subprocess.run(
          smoke_command, shell=True, cwd=str(self.ctx.worktree_path),
          capture_output=True, text=True,
      )
      if proc.returncode == 0:
          return GateResult("pass")
      return GateResult(
          "fail",
          details={"block_row": 5, "stderr_tail": proc.stderr[-2000:]},
      )

  def run_phase2(
      self, *,
      manifest: TaskManifest, facts: TaskFacts,
      criteria: list[AcceptanceCriterion],
      attempt_id: str, retry_idx: int,
      baseline_command: str, smoke_command: str,
  ) -> Phase2Verdict:
      """Chain gates 1 → 3 → 5 → 6 in order. T13 inserts gate 4 between
      3 and 5 in the full Phase 2 chain; T12 just covers the four T12 owns.
      """
      r = self.gate1_baseline(test_command=baseline_command)
      if r.status != "pass":
          return Phase2Verdict("blocked", "gate1_baseline", r)
      r = self.gate3_manifest(manifest=manifest, facts=facts)
      if r.status != "pass":
          return Phase2Verdict("blocked", "gate3_manifest", r)
      r = self.gate5_acceptance(
          criteria=criteria, attempt_id=attempt_id, retry_idx=retry_idx)
      if r.status != "pass":
          return Phase2Verdict("blocked", "gate5_acceptance", r)
      r = self.gate6_regression(smoke_command=smoke_command)
      if r.status != "pass":
          return Phase2Verdict("blocked", "gate6_regression", r)
      return Phase2Verdict("pass", None, None)


  @dataclass
  class Phase2Verdict:
      status: str                         # pass | blocked
      halted_at_gate: Optional[str]
      gate_result: Optional[GateResult]
  ```

  Re-run Step 12.7 → PASS.

### Task 13: Gate 4 codex review + retry whitelist + semantic-diff churn detection

**Files:**
- Modify: `scripts/flow_orchestrator.py`
- Create: `tests/smoke/test_semantic_retry_whitelist_violations.py` (ship-required)

**Design refs:** §3 gate 4 (per-task codex review; line 129: retry whitelist applies, churn detected → escalate), §3 R1/R2 (Phase 2/3 retry-whitelist scope), §3 line 141 (semantic-diff check: detect tests skipped/deleted, fixture narrowing, command flag suppression), §6 S7 (canonical `issue_id = sha256(file_path + line_range + issue_class + issue_message_normalized)[:12]` — same issue across rounds collides on id).

**Goal:** Add `gate4_codex_review` to `GateRunner`. Invokes codex CLI against current diff; parses verdict (GREEN / YELLOW / RED). On RED: extract issues, compute canonical S7 issue_ids, append to `review-issues.jsonl` (T6 helper), check for churn (same issue_id appearing across N retry rounds → escalate, do NOT consume more retry budget). After retry, runs **semantic-diff check**: BEFORE-retry diff vs AFTER-retry diff — if tests skipped / fixture narrowed / flags suppressed → escalate.

**Codex invocation (mirrors v0.8.0 pattern)**:
```bash
codex review --diff-only --output-format json
# OR via gstack:
gstack codex review
```

T13 wraps `subprocess.run` with a configurable command (default `codex review`); test fixture stubs the command for deterministic test output.

**Issue id (S7)**:
```python
def canonical_issue_id(file_path: str, line_range: str, issue_class: str, msg: str) -> str:
    norm_msg = " ".join(msg.lower().split())  # whitespace-normalize
    raw = f"{file_path}|{line_range}|{issue_class}|{norm_msg}"
    return hashlib.sha256(raw.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()[:12]
```

**Retry whitelist scope (§3 line 140–141)**:
- Whitelist applies ONLY to gate 4 + gate 5-unit/integration/behavior (the latter via T8's `LOCAL_FIX_ALLOWED`).
- Semantic-diff runs against BEFORE-retry diff vs AFTER-retry diff.

**Detection patterns (semantic-diff violations — escalate triggers)**:
1. Test files deleted (file in pre-diff `tests/` but missing post-diff)
2. Test functions `@unittest.skip`'d (regex match new `skipif|skip` decorators in test files)
3. Fixture narrowing (test data file shrunk; pre-diff bytes > 2× post-diff)
4. Command flag suppression (CI / Makefile / package.json scripts adding `--ignore`, `--no-fail-fast`, etc.)

  ```python
  class TestCanonicalIssueId(unittest.TestCase):
      def test_same_issue_same_id(self):
          a = canonical_issue_id("src/foo.py", "L10-15", "sql_safety",
                                 "  Possible SQL injection.  ")
          b = canonical_issue_id("src/foo.py", "L10-15", "sql_safety",
                                 "Possible SQL injection.")
          self.assertEqual(a, b)
          self.assertEqual(len(a), 12)

      def test_different_files_different_id(self):
          a = canonical_issue_id("src/foo.py", "L10-15", "sql", "x")
          b = canonical_issue_id("src/bar.py", "L10-15", "sql", "x")
          self.assertNotEqual(a, b)
  ```

  ```python
  def canonical_issue_id(
      file_path: str, line_range: str,
      issue_class: str, issue_message: str,
  ) -> str:
      norm_msg = " ".join(issue_message.lower().split())
      raw = f"{file_path}|{line_range}|{issue_class}|{norm_msg}"
      return hashlib.sha256(raw.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()[:12]
  ```
