- [ ] **Step 13.4: Implement `gate4_codex_review`**

  ```python
  def gate4_codex_review(
      self, *, codex_command: str = "codex review --diff-only --json",
  ) -> GateResult:
      proc = subprocess.run(
          codex_command, shell=True, cwd=str(self.ctx.worktree_path),
          capture_output=True, text=True,
      )
      if proc.returncode != 0:
          return GateResult(
              "inconclusive",
              details={"error": "codex CLI failed",
                       "stderr_tail": proc.stderr[-1000:]},
          )
      try:
          output = json.loads(proc.stdout)
      except json.JSONDecodeError:
          return GateResult(
              "inconclusive",
              details={"error": "codex output not JSON",
                       "stdout_tail": proc.stdout[-1000:]},
          )
      verdict = output.get("verdict", "INCONCLUSIVE")
      if verdict == "GREEN":
          return GateResult("pass", details={"verdict": "GREEN"})

      # Persist issues with S7 canonical ids
      issues = output.get("issues", [])
      for issue in issues:
          issue_id = canonical_issue_id(
              issue["file"], issue["line_range"],
              issue["class"], issue["message"],
          )
          append_review_issue(self.task_dir, ReviewIssueRecord(
              id=issue_id,
              ts=datetime.datetime.now(datetime.UTC).strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ"),
              task=self.task_id,
              severity=issue.get("severity", "med"),
              reviewer="codex",
              description=issue["message"],
              disposition="open",
          ))
      return GateResult(
          "fail" if verdict == "RED" else "pass",
          details={"verdict": verdict,
                   "issue_count": len(issues),
                   "issue_ids": [canonical_issue_id(
                       i["file"], i["line_range"],
                       i["class"], i["message"]) for i in issues]},
      )
  ```

  Re-run Step 13.3 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 13.5: Failing test — churn detection: same issue id across N rounds → escalate**

  ```python
  def test_gate4_churn_escalates_after_repeat(self):
      """Same issue_id appearing 3+ times → churn → escalate flag set."""
      gr = GateRunner(...)
      # Stub returns identical RED output 3 times
      stub_output = json.dumps({
          "verdict": "RED",
          "issues": [{"file": "x.py", "line_range": "L1",
                       "class": "c", "message": "m",
                       "severity": "high"}],
      })
      gr.gate4_codex_review(codex_command=f"echo '{stub_output}'")
      gr.gate4_codex_review(codex_command=f"echo '{stub_output}'")
      r = gr.gate4_codex_review(codex_command=f"echo '{stub_output}'")
      # Third hit triggers churn
      self.assertEqual(r.status, "fail")
      self.assertTrue(r.escalate)
      self.assertIn("churn", r.details)
  ```

- [ ] **Step 13.6: Implement churn tracking**

  ```python
  CHURN_THRESHOLD = 3  # same issue_id across N rounds → escalate

  def _count_issue_id_in_history(
      self, issue_id: str,
  ) -> int:
      path = self.task_dir / "review-issues.jsonl"
      if not path.is_file():
          return 0
      count = 0
      for line in path.read_text(encoding="utf-8").splitlines():
          try:
              rec = json.loads(line)
          except json.JSONDecodeError:
              continue
          if rec.get("id") == issue_id:
              count += 1
      return count

  # Inside gate4_codex_review, after computing issue_ids list, replace
  # the existing `return GateResult(...)` from Step 13.4 with a churn-
  # aware construction. `existing_details` is the dict that Step 13.4
  # was already building (verdict, issue_count, issue_ids); churn is
  # added only when non-empty so test assertions on absence still hold.
  churn_ids = [iid for iid in issue_ids
               if self._count_issue_id_in_history(iid) >= CHURN_THRESHOLD]
  existing_details = {
      "verdict": verdict,
      "issue_count": len(issues),
      "issue_ids": issue_ids,
  }
  if churn_ids:
      existing_details["churn"] = churn_ids
  result = GateResult(
      "fail" if verdict == "RED" else "pass",
      escalate=bool(churn_ids),
      details=existing_details,
  )
  ```

- [ ] **Step 13.7: Failing tests — semantic-diff escalation triggers (`test_semantic_retry_whitelist_violations.py`)**

  Per design §7 line 315 (ship-required smoke). Test the 4 escalation patterns:

  ```python
  # tests/smoke/test_semantic_retry_whitelist_violations.py
  import json, sys, tempfile, unittest
  from pathlib import Path

  REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent.parent
  sys.path.insert(0, str(REPO_ROOT / "scripts"))
  from flow_orchestrator import detect_semantic_violations  # type: ignore


  class TestSemanticRetryWhitelistViolations(unittest.TestCase):
      def test_test_file_deleted_escalates(self):
          before = "tests/test_foo.py\nsrc/foo.py\n"
          after = "src/foo.py\n"  # test file gone
          v = detect_semantic_violations(
              before_files=before.splitlines(),
              after_files=after.splitlines(),
              before_diff="def test_foo(): pass\n",
              after_diff="",
          )
          self.assertTrue(v.escalate)
          self.assertIn("test_file_deleted", v.violations)

      def test_skip_decorator_added_escalates(self):
          before_diff = "def test_x(): assert False"
          after_diff = "@unittest.skip\ndef test_x(): assert False"
          v = detect_semantic_violations(
              before_files=["tests/t.py"], after_files=["tests/t.py"],
              before_diff=before_diff, after_diff=after_diff,
          )
          self.assertTrue(v.escalate)
          self.assertIn("test_skipped", v.violations)

      def test_command_flag_no_fail_fast_escalates(self):
          before_diff = "pytest tests/"
          after_diff = "pytest --no-fail-fast --ignore=tests/auth tests/"
          v = detect_semantic_violations(
              before_files=["Makefile"], after_files=["Makefile"],
              before_diff=before_diff, after_diff=after_diff,
          )
          self.assertTrue(v.escalate)
          self.assertIn("flag_suppression", v.violations)

      def test_clean_diff_no_escalate(self):
          v = detect_semantic_violations(
              before_files=["src/foo.py"], after_files=["src/foo.py"],
              before_diff="def x(): return 1",
              after_diff="def x(): return 2",
          )
          self.assertFalse(v.escalate)

      def test_fixture_narrowing_escalates(self):
          # pre-diff fixture has 1000 rows; post-diff has 10 → 100x shrink
          before = "row\n" * 1000
          after = "row\n" * 10
          v = detect_semantic_violations(
              before_files=["tests/fixtures/data.csv"],
              after_files=["tests/fixtures/data.csv"],
              before_diff=before, after_diff=after,
          )
          self.assertTrue(v.escalate)
          self.assertIn("fixture_narrowing", v.violations)


  if __name__ == "__main__":
      unittest.main()
  ```

- [ ] **Step 13.8: Implement `detect_semantic_violations`**

  ```python
  @dataclass
  class SemanticViolations:
      escalate: bool
      violations: list[str]


  _SUPPRESS_FLAG_PATTERNS = (
      "--no-fail-fast", "--ignore", "--skip", "-k 'not ", "skipif",
  )

  _SKIP_DECORATOR_PATTERNS = ("@unittest.skip", "@pytest.mark.skip", "@skip")


  def detect_semantic_violations(
      *,
      before_files: list[str], after_files: list[str],
      before_diff: str, after_diff: str,
  ) -> SemanticViolations:
      """§3 line 141: detect retry-whitelist violations.
      Returns escalate=True with list of detected pattern names.
      """
      violations: list[str] = []

      # 1. Test files deleted
      before_tests = {f for f in before_files
                      if f.startswith("tests/") and f.endswith(".py")}
      after_tests = {f for f in after_files
                     if f.startswith("tests/") and f.endswith(".py")}
      if before_tests - after_tests:
          violations.append("test_file_deleted")

      # 2. Skip decorator added in test files
      for decorator in _SKIP_DECORATOR_PATTERNS:
          if decorator not in before_diff and decorator in after_diff:
              violations.append("test_skipped")
              break

      # 3. Flag suppression in CI / Makefile / package.json
      for flag in _SUPPRESS_FLAG_PATTERNS:
          if flag not in before_diff and flag in after_diff:
              violations.append("flag_suppression")
              break

      # 4. Fixture narrowing — pre-diff bytes > 2× post-diff (heuristic)
      common_fixtures = [f for f in (set(before_files) & set(after_files))
                         if "fixture" in f or "data" in f]
      if common_fixtures:
          if len(before_diff) > 2 * len(after_diff) and len(after_diff) < 1024:
              violations.append("fixture_narrowing")

      return SemanticViolations(escalate=bool(violations),
                                 violations=violations)
  ```

  Re-run Step 13.7 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 13.9: Failing test — `run_phase2` chain inserts gate 4 between gates 3 and 5**

  T12 Step 12.8's `run_phase2` chain is `1 → 3 → 5 → 6` (T12 doesn't own gate 4). T13 must extend the chain so the full Phase 2 gate sequence is `1 → 3 → 4 → 5 → 6`. The test pins both ordering (gate 4 runs AFTER gate 3 and BEFORE gate 5) and halt semantics (gate 4 RED halts before gate 5 + 6 run).

  ```python
  class TestRunPhase2InsertsGate4(unittest.TestCase):
      def test_gate4_runs_between_gate3_and_gate5(self):
          """T13 chain extension: pass-all dry-run records gate execution
          order. Stub each gate to record its name in a list and return
          PASS; assert order is [1,3,4,5,6]."""
          gr = GateRunner(ctx=ctx, contract=contract, task_dir=task_dir,
                          run_id="r", task_id="T0")
          calls: list[str] = []
          gr.gate1_baseline = lambda **_: (calls.append("1") or
                                            GateResult("pass"))
          gr.gate3_manifest = lambda **_: (calls.append("3") or
                                            GateResult("pass"))
          gr.gate4_codex_review = lambda **_: (calls.append("4") or
                                                 GateResult("pass"))
          gr.gate5_acceptance = lambda **_: (calls.append("5") or
                                               GateResult("pass"))
          gr.gate6_regression = lambda **_: (calls.append("6") or
                                               GateResult("pass"))
          v = gr.run_phase2(
              manifest=manifest, facts=facts,
              criteria=[], attempt_id="a", retry_idx=0,
              baseline_command="true",
              codex_command="echo '{\"verdict\":\"GREEN\",\"issues\":[]}'",
              smoke_command="true",
          )
          self.assertEqual(v.status, "pass")
          self.assertEqual(calls, ["1", "3", "4", "5", "6"])

      def test_gate4_red_halts_before_gate5_and_gate6(self):
          """Gate 4 RED → run_phase2 returns blocked + halted_at_gate
          ='gate4_codex_review'; gates 5 + 6 must NOT execute."""
          gr = GateRunner(...)
          calls: list[str] = []
          gr.gate1_baseline = lambda **_: (calls.append("1") or
                                            GateResult("pass"))
          gr.gate3_manifest = lambda **_: (calls.append("3") or
                                            GateResult("pass"))
          gr.gate4_codex_review = lambda **_: (calls.append("4") or
              GateResult("fail", details={"verdict": "RED"}))
          gr.gate5_acceptance = lambda **_: (calls.append("5") or
                                               GateResult("pass"))
          gr.gate6_regression = lambda **_: (calls.append("6") or
                                               GateResult("pass"))
          v = gr.run_phase2(
              manifest=manifest, facts=facts,
              criteria=[], attempt_id="a", retry_idx=0,
              baseline_command="true",
              codex_command="codex review",
              smoke_command="true",
          )
          self.assertEqual(v.status, "blocked")
          self.assertEqual(v.halted_at_gate, "gate4_codex_review")
          self.assertEqual(calls, ["1", "3", "4"])
  ```

- [ ] **Step 13.10: Implement `run_phase2` chain extension (replace T12's method)**

  T12 Step 12.8 defined `run_phase2` chaining 1→3→5→6. T13 replaces that body in-place (same `flow_orchestrator.py` file, same `GateRunner` class) so the full chain runs 1→3→4→5→6, and adds `codex_command: str` to the signature.

  ```python
  # In GateRunner — REPLACES the T12 Step 12.8 implementation in-place.
  def run_phase2(
      self, *,
      manifest: TaskManifest, facts: TaskFacts,
      criteria: list[AcceptanceCriterion],
      attempt_id: str, retry_idx: int,
      baseline_command: str, smoke_command: str,
      codex_command: str = "codex review --diff-only --json",
  ) -> Phase2Verdict:
      """Full Phase 2 chain: gates 1 → 3 → 4 → 5 → 6 in order. First
      non-pass result halts and returns Phase2Verdict (caller routes
      block per `escalate` flag — RED with churn / Y1 e2e fail).
      Gates 2/7/8 are NOT in this chain (gate 2 is Phase 1 plan review;
      gates 7/8 are post-Phase-2 merge + post-merge verify, owned by
      T14/T15).
      """
      r = self.gate1_baseline(test_command=baseline_command)
      if r.status != "pass":
          return Phase2Verdict("blocked", "gate1_baseline", r)
      r = self.gate3_manifest(manifest=manifest, facts=facts)
      if r.status != "pass":
          return Phase2Verdict("blocked", "gate3_manifest", r)
      r = self.gate4_codex_review(codex_command=codex_command)
      if r.status != "pass":
          return Phase2Verdict("blocked", "gate4_codex_review", r)
      r = self.gate5_acceptance(
          criteria=criteria, attempt_id=attempt_id, retry_idx=retry_idx)
      if r.status != "pass":
          return Phase2Verdict("blocked", "gate5_acceptance", r)
      r = self.gate6_regression(smoke_command=smoke_command)
      if r.status != "pass":
          return Phase2Verdict("blocked", "gate6_regression", r)
      return Phase2Verdict("pass", None, None)
  ```

  Re-run Step 13.9 → PASS. Also re-run T12's Step 12.7 chain test (if any caller test asserts on the 1→3→5→6 order) — update those assertions to expect the new 5-gate chain. The T12 commit message already foreshadows this ("T13 inserts 4 between 3 and 5 in the full chain"); T13's commit message body confirms the replacement.

### Task 14: Gate 7 local merge + 9-step transactional sequence

**Files:**
- Modify: `scripts/flow_orchestrator.py`
- Create: `tests/smoke/test_atomic_merge_crash_blocks.py` (ship-required)

**Design refs:** §6 R3 (9-step transactional sequence — see §6 line 242 transition table), §6 Y5 (explicit gap-by-gap crash behavior between any two ordered writes), §4 Y2 (cleanup AFTER gate 8 pass — T15 owns; T14 only emits events through `merge_applied`).

**Goal:** Implement steps 1–7 of the R3 transactional sequence:
1. gates 1–6 pass (caller asserts; T14 entry contract)
2. `decisions.jsonl` append `task_ready_to_merge`
3. `checkpoints/<ts>.md` write (`phase=pre_merge`)
4. `progress.md` task status → `merging`
5. `decisions.jsonl` append `merge_started`
6. git merge into integration target
7. `decisions.jsonl` append `merge_applied` with `target_commit_post_merge`

**Crash recovery (Y5)**: between any two ordered writes, on next-startup the reader detects mismatch:
- `task_ready_to_merge` exists, no `merge_started` → step 4/5 gap; orchestrator resumes from step 4.
- `merge_started` exists, no `merge_applied` → mid-merge crash; check git state (was merge applied? committed?) → block with reconcile choices `{replay_merge_from_diff_hash, abort_and_revert_partial, switch_to_interactive}` per §6 line 249.
- `merge_applied` exists, no `task_completed` AND no `post_merge_verify_failed` → mid-gate-8 → block per R10.

T14 owns step 1–7 + the mid-merge crash detection. T15 owns step 8 + 9a/9b (gate 8 + completion paths). T19 (Group G) owns the dispatch-side crash recovery routing.

  ```python
          events = [json.loads(l).get("event")
                    for l in (task_dir / "decisions.jsonl").read_text().splitlines()
                    if json.loads(l).get("event")]
          # Among other events emitted by upstream T10/T11/T12/T13, these
          # 4 must appear in this relative order:
          for needle, prior in [("task_ready_to_merge", None),
                                ("merge_started", "task_ready_to_merge"),
                                ("merge_applied", "merge_started")]:

                  self.assertLess(events.index(prior), events.index(needle))
  ```

- [ ] **Step 14.2: Implement `MergeRunner` skeleton + steps 2–4**

  ```python
  @dataclass
  class MergeResult:
      status: str                         # merged | blocked
      target_commit_pre_merge: Optional[str] = None
      target_commit_post_merge: Optional[str] = None
      block_reason: Optional[str] = None


  class MergeRunner:
      def __init__(
          self, *,
          ctx: WorktreeContext, contract: Contract, task_dir: Path,
          run_id: str, task_id: str,
      ):
          self.ctx = ctx
          self.contract = contract
          self.task_dir = task_dir
          self.run_id = run_id
          self.task_id = task_id

      def merge_task(self, *, facts: TaskFacts, merge_strategy: str) -> MergeResult:
          # Step 2: task_ready_to_merge
          append_autonomy_event(self.task_dir, EVENT_TASK_READY_TO_MERGE, {
              "event_id": _new_event_id(),
              "ts": _now_iso(),
              "slug": self.ctx.slug, "run_id": self.run_id, "task_id": self.task_id,
              "worktree_id": self.ctx.worktree_id,
              "worktree_path": str(self.ctx.worktree_path),
              "original_base_commit": self.ctx.original_base_commit,
              "current_base_commit": self.ctx.current_base_commit,
              "lifecycle_state": "merging",
              "diff_hash": facts.diff_hash,
              "target_commit_pre_merge": facts.target_commit_pre_merge,
          })
          # Step 3: pre_merge checkpoint
          ts = _now_iso()
          write_checkpoint(
              self.task_dir, ts=ts,
              body=(f"phase: pre_merge\n"
                    f"worktree_id: {self.ctx.worktree_id}\n"
                    f"worktree_path: {self.ctx.worktree_path}\n"
                    f"original_base_commit: {self.ctx.original_base_commit}\n"
                    f"current_base_commit: {self.ctx.current_base_commit}\n"
                    f"lifecycle_state: merging\n"
                    f"diff_hash: {facts.diff_hash}\n"
                    f"target_commit_pre_merge: {facts.target_commit_pre_merge}\n"),
              git_hash=facts.target_commit_pre_merge,
          )
          # Step 4: progress.md status → merging (T20 owns the lint;
          # for now write naïvely)
          self._update_task_status("merging")
          # Steps 5–7 in next implementation step
          return self._continue_merge(facts=facts, merge_strategy=merge_strategy)
  ```

- [ ] **Step 14.3: Implement steps 5–7 (merge_started → git merge → merge_applied)**

  ```python
  def _continue_merge(self, *, facts: TaskFacts, merge_strategy: str) -> MergeResult:
      # Step 5: merge_started
      append_autonomy_event(self.task_dir, EVENT_MERGE_STARTED, {
          "event_id": _new_event_id(),
          "ts": _now_iso(),
          "slug": self.ctx.slug, "run_id": self.run_id, "task_id": self.task_id,
          "worktree_id": self.ctx.worktree_id,
          "worktree_path": str(self.ctx.worktree_path),
          "integration_target": self.ctx.integration_target,
          "target_commit_pre_merge": facts.target_commit_pre_merge,
      })
      # Step 6: git merge — must run with HEAD on integration_target.
      # repo_root's HEAD is whatever the user last checked out; if they're
      # on a feature branch, `git merge` would silently merge into the
      # wrong branch. Assert HEAD ref matches integration_target FIRST;
      # if mismatched, refuse to merge (no auto-checkout — that would
      # mutate the user's working state without consent).
      repo_root = self.ctx.worktree_path.parents[2]  # .claude/worktrees/<id>/
      head_ref = subprocess.run(
          ["git", "-C", str(repo_root),
           "rev-parse", "--abbrev-ref", "HEAD"],
          capture_output=True, text=True,
      ).stdout.strip()
      if head_ref != self.ctx.integration_target:
          # R3 safety: refuse to merge into the wrong branch.
          return MergeResult(
              status="blocked",
              target_commit_pre_merge=facts.target_commit_pre_merge,
              block_reason=(f"refusing to merge into HEAD={head_ref!r}: "
                             f"expected integration_target="
                             f"{self.ctx.integration_target!r}; "
                             f"checkout integration_target manually "
                             f"and resume"),
          )
      proc = subprocess.run(
          ["git", "-C", str(repo_root),
           "merge", merge_strategy, self.ctx.branch],
          capture_output=True, text=True,
      )
      if proc.returncode != 0:
          # Merge conflict / non-ff push / etc. — write blocked.md per R3
          # mid-merge crash path (treated as "merge attempted but did not
          # complete cleanly")
          return MergeResult(
              status="blocked",
              target_commit_pre_merge=facts.target_commit_pre_merge,
              block_reason=f"git merge failed: {proc.stderr[-500:]}",
          )
      target_commit_post_merge = subprocess.run(
          ["git", "-C", str(repo_root), "rev-parse", "HEAD"],
          capture_output=True, text=True,
      ).stdout.strip()
      # Step 7: merge_applied
      append_autonomy_event(self.task_dir, EVENT_MERGE_APPLIED, {
          "event_id": _new_event_id(),
          "ts": _now_iso(),
          "slug": self.ctx.slug, "run_id": self.run_id, "task_id": self.task_id,
          "worktree_id": self.ctx.worktree_id,
          "target_commit_post_merge": target_commit_post_merge,
          "merge_strategy": merge_strategy,
      })
      return MergeResult(
          status="merged",
          target_commit_pre_merge=facts.target_commit_pre_merge,
          target_commit_post_merge=target_commit_post_merge,
      )

  def _update_task_status(self, status: str) -> None:
      """Naïve progress.md status mutation. T20 introduces lint + schema
      enforcement (status enum from §8.3.1); T14 just rewrites the line."""
      # Implementation: read progress.md, find `- [ ] T{idx}` line, update
      # trailing status marker. Out of scope for code sample; reuse
      # progress_meta.update_task_status if it exists.
      pass  # placeholder; full impl in T14 actual code.
  ```

  Re-run Step 14.1 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 14.3b: Failing test — refuse to merge when HEAD is not on integration_target (R9 safety)**

  Without the HEAD assertion, `git merge` would silently merge into whatever branch the user last checked out — a destructive footgun. This test pins the safety check.

  ```python
  class TestMergeRefusesWrongHead(unittest.TestCase):
      def test_refuses_when_head_is_feature_branch(self):
          # Fixture: repo_root with HEAD on a feature branch (NOT master)
          _git(repo_root, "checkout", "-b", "user-feature")
          merger = MergeRunner(ctx=ctx_targeting_master, contract=contract,
                                task_dir=task_dir, run_id="r", task_id="T0")
          result = merger.merge_task(facts=facts, merge_strategy="--ff-only")
          self.assertEqual(result.status, "blocked")
          self.assertIn("refusing to merge into HEAD='user-feature'",
                        result.block_reason)
          self.assertIn("integration_target='master'", result.block_reason)
          # No merge occurred — repo_root HEAD unchanged
          head_after = _git(repo_root, "rev-parse", "HEAD").stdout.strip()
          self.assertEqual(head_after, _git(repo_root, "rev-parse",
                                              "user-feature").stdout.strip())

      def test_proceeds_when_head_matches_integration_target(self):
          # Fixture: repo_root with HEAD on master (matches ctx.integration_target)
          _git(repo_root, "checkout", "master")
          merger = MergeRunner(
              ctx=ctx_targeting_master, contract=contract,
              task_dir=task_dir, run_id="r", task_id="T0",
          )
          result = merger.merge_task(facts=facts, merge_strategy="--ff-only")
          self.assertEqual(result.status, "merged")
  ```

  Re-run after Step 14.3 implementation lands → PASS (the HEAD assertion is in the same code block as the merge call).

  ```python
  class TestMidMergeCrashDetection(unittest.TestCase):
      def setUp(self):
          self.task_dir = Path(tempfile.mkdtemp())
          self.addCleanup(lambda: shutil.rmtree(self.task_dir,
                                                  ignore_errors=True))

      def _ev(self, kind: str, eid: str) -> dict:
          return {
              "event": kind, "event_id": eid, "ts": "2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
              "slug": "demo", "run_id": "r", "task_id": "T0",
              "worktree_id": "demo+t0+abcdefg",
              "worktree_path": str(self.task_dir / "wt"),
              "integration_target": "master",
              "target_commit_pre_merge": "deadbeef",
              "target_commit_post_merge": "cafebabe",
              "merge_strategy": "--ff-only",
          }

      def test_merge_started_without_merge_applied_blocks(self):
          append_autonomy_event(
              self.task_dir, EVENT_MERGE_STARTED,
              self._ev("merge_started", "e1"))
          state = detect_mid_merge_crash(
              self.task_dir, run_id="r", task_id="T0")
          self.assertEqual(state["state"], "mid_merge_crash")
          self.assertEqual(state["block_type"], "atomic_merge_crashed")
          self.assertIn("replay_merge_from_diff_hash", state["choices"])

      def test_merge_applied_after_merge_started_no_crash(self):
          append_autonomy_event(
              self.task_dir, EVENT_MERGE_STARTED,
              self._ev("merge_started", "e1"))
          append_autonomy_event(
              self.task_dir, EVENT_MERGE_APPLIED,
              self._ev("merge_applied", "e2"))
          state = detect_mid_merge_crash(
              self.task_dir, run_id="r", task_id="T0")
          self.assertEqual(state["state"], "merge_completed")
  ```

- [ ] **Step 14.5: Implement `detect_mid_merge_crash`**

  ```python
  def detect_mid_merge_crash(
      task_dir: Path, *, run_id: str, task_id: str,
  ) -> dict:
      """R3 mid-merge gap detection. Returns one of:
      - merge_completed: merge_applied + matching task_completed/post_merge_verify_failed
      - mid_merge_crash: merge_started without matching merge_applied
      - mid_gate8_crash: merge_applied without matching task_completed or
        post_merge_verify_failed
      - none: no merge events for this run/task
      """
      events = []
      path = task_dir / "decisions.jsonl"
      if path.is_file():
          for line in path.read_text(encoding="utf-8").splitlines():
              try:
                  rec = json.loads(line)
              except json.JSONDecodeError:
                  continue
              if (rec.get("run_id") == run_id
                      and rec.get("task_id") == task_id):
                  events.append(rec)
      kinds = [e.get("event") for e in events]
      if EVENT_MERGE_STARTED in kinds and EVENT_MERGE_APPLIED not in kinds:
          return {
              "state": "mid_merge_crash",
              "block_type": "atomic_merge_crashed",
              "choices": ["replay_merge_from_diff_hash",
                          "abort_and_revert_partial",
                          "switch_to_interactive"],
          }
      if (EVENT_MERGE_APPLIED in kinds
              and EVENT_TASK_COMPLETED not in kinds
              and EVENT_POST_MERGE_VERIFY_FAILED not in kinds):
          return {
              "state": "mid_gate8_crash",
              "block_type": "post_merge_verify_in_progress_crash",
              "choices": ["rerun_post_merge_verify",
                          "abort_and_revert_partial",
                          "switch_to_interactive"],
          }
      if EVENT_MERGE_APPLIED in kinds:
          return {"state": "merge_completed"}
      return {"state": "none"}
  ```

  ```python
  # tests/smoke/test_atomic_merge_crash_blocks.py

              "event_id": "e1", "ts": "2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
              "slug": "demo", "run_id": "r", "task_id": "T0",
              "worktree_id": "demo+t0+abc1234",
              "worktree_path": "/tmp/wt",

          })

              self.task_dir, run_id="r", task_id="T0")

          # User choices include the R3 reconcile set
          for needed in ("replay_merge_from_diff_hash",
                         "abort_and_revert_partial",
                         "switch_to_interactive"):
              self.assertIn(needed, state["choices"])
  ```

### Task 15: Gate 8 post-merge verify + verification worktree + S1 wave block + S3 skip rule

**Files:**
- Modify: `scripts/flow_orchestrator.py`
- Create: `tests/smoke/test_post_merge_verify_failed_blocks.py` (ship-required)
- Create: `tests/unit/test_merge_queue_serialization.py` (ship-required unit)

**Design refs:** §3 gate 8 (R4: post-merge verify in ephemeral verification worktree), §4 Y4 (verification worktree path: `.claude/worktrees/verify/<run_id>+t<n>+<post_merge_sha>/`; lifecycle: create at gate 8 start, cleanup on PASS, preserve on FAIL), §1 row 18 (`blocked_post_merge` — merge stays intact, NO auto-revert), §6 R3 9a/9b sub-steps + Y5 explicit gap-by-gap crash, §6 S1 (`blocked_post_merge` halts ENTIRE run; later tasks stay at `pending`), §4 S3 (`post_merge_skip: true` illegal for `regression` unless `contract.post_merge_regression_optional=true` — T1 enforces at parse time; T15 honors at runtime).

**Goal:** Implement step 8 of R3 sequence + 9a/9b completion paths. Add `Gate8VerificationRunner` that:
1. Creates ephemeral verification worktree at `.claude/worktrees/verify/<run_id>+t<n>+<post_merge_sha>/` from integration target.
2. Emits `post_merge_verification_started` event.
3. Runs full acceptance criteria (Phase 3 — T8's `evaluate_criterion(phase=3)`) + final regression smoke. Per-criterion `post_merge_skip: true` honored. Type=`regression` skip only allowed if `contract.post_merge_regression_optional=true` (T1 already validates).
4. PASS path (9a): emit `post_merge_verification_completed` + `task_completed` + `checkpoints/<ts>.md` (`phase=post_merge`) + `progress.md` → `merged` + cleanup BOTH worktrees.
5. FAIL path (9b): emit `post_merge_verify_failed` + write `blocked.md` (`block_type=post_merge_verify_failed`) + `progress.md` → `blocked_post_merge` + preserve verification worktree at `.claude/worktrees/verify/aborted/...`.

**S1 wave block (multi-task)**: `MergeQueue` class checks for ANY `blocked_post_merge` event in the current run before allowing a later task into gate 7. Earlier tasks complete; later tasks halt at `pending`.

- [ ] **Step 15.1: Failing test — verification worktree path scheme**

  ```python
  # tests/smoke/test_post_merge_verify_failed_blocks.py
  class TestVerificationWorktreePath(unittest.TestCase):
      def test_path_uses_run_id_taskidx_postmerge_sha(self):

              run_id="abc12345", task_id="T2",
              target_commit_post_merge="deadbeefdeadbeef",
          )

          self.assertEqual(
              path.name, "abc12345+t2+deadbee")  # 7-char shortsha
          self.assertEqual(path.parent.name, "verify")
  ```

- [ ] **Step 15.2: Implement `Gate8VerificationRunner` + verification worktree creation**

  ```python
  class Gate8VerificationRunner:
      def __init__(
          self, *,
          ctx: WorktreeContext, contract: Contract, task_dir: Path,
          run_id: str, task_id: str, target_commit_post_merge: str,
          notifier: Optional["Notifier"] = None,   # T16: routes 9b block
      ):
          self.ctx = ctx
          self.contract = contract
          self.task_dir = task_dir
          self.run_id = run_id
          self.task_id = task_id
          self.target_commit_post_merge = target_commit_post_merge
          self.notifier = notifier
          self.verification_id: Optional[str] = None

      def _verification_path(self) -> Path:
          short = self.target_commit_post_merge[:7]
          name = f"{self.run_id}+t{self.ctx.task_idx}+{short}"
          return (self.ctx.worktree_path.parents[2]  # repo root
                  / WORKTREE_ROOT / "verify" / name)

      def _create_verification_worktree(self) -> Path:
          path = self._verification_path()
          path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
          repo_root = self.ctx.worktree_path.parents[2]
          _git(repo_root, "worktree", "add", "--detach",
               str(path), self.target_commit_post_merge)
          self.verification_id = path.name
          return path
  ```

  ```python
  def test_pass_path_emits_completion_and_cleans_up(self):
      runner = Gate8VerificationRunner(...)
      result = runner.verify(
          criteria=[passing_criterion()],
          regression_command="true",
      )
      self.assertEqual(result.status, "completed")
      events = [json.loads(l).get("event") for l in
                (task_dir / "decisions.jsonl").read_text().splitlines()
                if "event" in json.loads(l)]
      self.assertIn("post_merge_verification_started", events)
      self.assertIn("post_merge_verification_completed", events)
      self.assertIn("task_completed", events)
      # Verification worktree cleaned up on PASS
      self.assertFalse(runner._verification_path().exists())
  ```

- [ ] **Step 15.4: Implement 9a PASS path**

  ```python
  @dataclass
  class Gate8Result:
      status: str                         # completed | blocked_post_merge
      verification_worktree_id: Optional[str] = None
      blocked_md_path: Optional[Path] = None
      criteria_results: list = field(default_factory=list)


  def verify(
      self, *,
      criteria: list[AcceptanceCriterion],
      regression_command: str,
  ) -> Gate8Result:
      vpath = self._create_verification_worktree()
      append_autonomy_event(self.task_dir, EVENT_POST_MERGE_VERIFICATION_STARTED, {
          "event_id": _new_event_id(),
          "ts": _now_iso(),
          "slug": self.ctx.slug, "run_id": self.run_id, "task_id": self.task_id,
          "verification_worktree_id": self.verification_id,
          "verification_worktree_path": str(vpath),
          "target_commit_post_merge": self.target_commit_post_merge,
      })
      # Apply S3 skip rules (per-criterion post_merge_skip)
      effective = [c for c in criteria if not c.post_merge_skip]
      from flow_acceptance import AcceptanceRunner, EvalDecision
      runner = AcceptanceRunner(
          worktree_root=vpath,
          log_dir=self.task_dir / "logs" / "post_merge",
          slug=self.ctx.slug, task_id=self.task_id,
          run_id=self.run_id, worktree_id=self.verification_id,
      )
      results = []
      gate_passed = True
      for idx, crit in enumerate(effective):
          rr = runner.run_one(
              crit, criterion_idx=idx,
              attempt_id=f"post_merge_{self.run_id}", retry_idx=0,
              task_dir=self.task_dir,
          )
          decision = runner.evaluate_criterion(
              crit, phase=3, runner_result=rr)
          results.append({"idx": idx, "status": rr.status,
                          "decision": decision.value})
          if decision != EvalDecision.PASS:
              gate_passed = False
              break
      # Final regression smoke
      if gate_passed:
          proc = subprocess.run(
              regression_command, shell=True, cwd=str(vpath),
              capture_output=True, text=True,
          )
          if proc.returncode != 0:
              gate_passed = False
              results.append({"regression_smoke": "fail",
                              "stderr_tail": proc.stderr[-500:]})

      append_autonomy_event(self.task_dir, EVENT_POST_MERGE_VERIFICATION_COMPLETED, {
          "event_id": _new_event_id(), "ts": _now_iso(),
          "slug": self.ctx.slug, "run_id": self.run_id, "task_id": self.task_id,
          "verification_worktree_id": self.verification_id,
          "status": "pass" if gate_passed else "fail",
          "criteria_results": results,
      })
      if gate_passed:
          return self._complete_9a(results)
      return self._fail_9b(results)


  def _complete_9a(self, results) -> Gate8Result:
      # 9a.1: task_completed event
      facts = TaskFacts(  # rebuild from worktree state
          changed_files=[], diff_hash="",  # filled below
          target_commit_pre_merge="",
          newly_added_files=[],
      )
      # Compute final_diff_hash from main worktree (before cleanup)
      final_diff = _git(self.ctx.worktree_path, "diff", "--unified=0",
                        f"{self.ctx.original_base_commit}..HEAD").stdout
      final_diff_hash = hashlib.sha256(final_diff.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
      append_autonomy_event(self.task_dir, EVENT_TASK_COMPLETED, {
          "event_id": _new_event_id(), "ts": _now_iso(),
          "slug": self.ctx.slug, "run_id": self.run_id, "task_id": self.task_id,
          "worktree_id": self.ctx.worktree_id,
          "final_diff_hash": final_diff_hash,
          "target_commit_post_merge": self.target_commit_post_merge,
      })
      # 9a.2: post_merge checkpoint
      write_checkpoint(self.task_dir, ts=_now_iso(),
          body=f"phase: post_merge\nfinal_diff_hash: {final_diff_hash}\n",
          git_hash=self.target_commit_post_merge)
      # 9a.3: progress.md → merged (T20 owns lint)
      # 9a.4: cleanup task worktree
      repo_root = self.ctx.worktree_path.parents[2]
      _git(repo_root, "worktree", "remove", "--force", str(self.ctx.worktree_path))
      _git(repo_root, "branch", "-D", self.ctx.branch, check=False)
      # 9a.5: cleanup verification worktree
      _git(repo_root, "worktree", "remove", "--force",
           str(self._verification_path()), check=False)
      return Gate8Result(
          status="completed",
          verification_worktree_id=self.verification_id,
          criteria_results=results,
      )
  ```

  ```python
                     "split_followup", "abort_run"):
          self.assertIn(choice, blocked)
      # Verification worktree preserved at verify/aborted/...
  ```

- [ ] **Step 15.6: Implement 9b FAIL path**

  ```python
  def _fail_9b(self, results) -> Gate8Result:
      # 9b.1: post_merge_verify_failed event
      blocked_md_path = self.task_dir / "blocked.md"
      choices = ["keep_and_fix_interactive", "revert_merge",
                 "split_followup", "abort_run"]
      why = f"post_merge_verify_failed: {len(results)} criteria checked"
      resume = f"flow orchestrator --resume {self.ctx.slug}"
      append_autonomy_event(self.task_dir, EVENT_POST_MERGE_VERIFY_FAILED, {
          "event_id": _new_event_id(), "ts": _now_iso(),
          "slug": self.ctx.slug, "run_id": self.run_id, "task_id": self.task_id,
          "verification_worktree_id": self.verification_id,
          "blocked_md_path": str(blocked_md_path),
          "user_choices": choices,
      })
      # 9b.2: blocked.md with §1 row 18 choices — route through Notifier
      # when present (Tier 1+2), else write_blocked (Tier 1 only) for
      # back-compat with unit tests that don't construct one.
      if self.notifier is not None:
          self.notifier.fire_block(
              block_type="post_merge_verify_failed", phase=3,
              task_id=self.task_id, issue_id="post_merge_verify_failed",
              why_blocked=why, required_choice=choices,
              safe_resume_command=resume,
          )
      else:
          write_blocked(
              self.task_dir, phase=3, task=self.task_id,
              why_blocked=why, required_choice=choices,
              safe_resume_command=resume,
          )
      # 9b.3: progress.md → blocked_post_merge (T20 enforces enum)
      # 9b.4: preserve verification worktree at verify/aborted/<id>+failed
      vpath = self._verification_path()
      aborted = vpath.parent / "aborted" / f"{vpath.name}+failed"
      aborted.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
      vpath.rename(aborted)
      return Gate8Result(
          status="blocked_post_merge",
          verification_worktree_id=self.verification_id,
          blocked_md_path=blocked_md_path,
          criteria_results=results,
      )
  ```

- [ ] **Step 15.7: Failing test — `MergeQueue.can_proceed` halts later tasks (S1)**

  Create `tests/unit/test_merge_queue_serialization.py`:

  ```python
  class TestMergeQueueSerialization(unittest.TestCase):
      def test_blocked_post_merge_halts_later_tasks(self):
          """S1: while ANY task in run is blocked_post_merge, later tasks
          must NOT enter gate 7."""
          append_autonomy_event(task_dir, EVENT_POST_MERGE_VERIFY_FAILED, {
              "event_id": "e1", "ts": "t",
              "slug": "demo", "run_id": "r", "task_id": "T0",
              "verification_worktree_id": "v", "blocked_md_path": "b",
              "user_choices": ["abort_run"],
          })
          q = MergeQueue(task_dir=task_dir, run_id="r")
          self.assertFalse(q.can_proceed(task_id="T1"))
          self.assertFalse(q.can_proceed(task_id="T2"))

      def test_clean_run_proceeds(self):
          q = MergeQueue(task_dir=task_dir, run_id="r")
          self.assertTrue(q.can_proceed(task_id="T0"))

      def test_resolved_unblocks_queue(self):
          """If blocked task resolves to abort_run, queue still halted —
          but if user picks revert_merge + the post_merge_verify_failed
          event has matching post-resolution event, queue proceeds."""
          # (Full resolution flow lives in T19 recovery dispatcher; T15
          # only checks raw event presence.)
          append_autonomy_event(task_dir, EVENT_POST_MERGE_VERIFY_FAILED, {
              "event_id": "e2", "ts": "2026-05-06T00:01:00Z",
              "slug": "demo", "run_id": "r", "task_id": "T0",
              "verification_worktree_id": "v",
              "blocked_md_path": str(task_dir / "blocked.md"),
              "user_choices": ["abort_run"],
          })
          q = MergeQueue(task_dir=task_dir, run_id="r")
          self.assertFalse(q.can_proceed(task_id="T1"))
  ```

- [ ] **Step 15.8: Implement `MergeQueue`**

  ```python
  class MergeQueue:
      """S1: while ANY task in this run has an unresolved
      post_merge_verify_failed event, later tasks halt at pending.
      Resolution is detected by T19's recovery dispatcher writing a
      `post_merge_resolved` event (introduced in T19 — for T15 the queue
      checks only for the failed event's presence).
      """
      def __init__(self, *, task_dir: Path, run_id: str):
          self.task_dir = task_dir
          self.run_id = run_id

      def can_proceed(self, *, task_id: str) -> bool:
          path = self.task_dir / "decisions.jsonl"
          if not path.is_file():
              return True
          for line in path.read_text(encoding="utf-8").splitlines():
              try:
                  rec = json.loads(line)
              except json.JSONDecodeError:
                  continue
              if (rec.get("run_id") == self.run_id
                      and rec.get("event") == EVENT_POST_MERGE_VERIFY_FAILED):
                  # Any task in run has unresolved blocked_post_merge → halt
                  return False
          return True
  ```

  Re-run Step 15.7 → PASS.

### Task 16: 3-tier notification with throttle + tier2_enabled

**Files:**
- Create: `scripts/flow_notification.py`
- Create: `tests/unit/test_notification_throttle_semantics.py` (ship-required unit)

**Design refs:** §5 R9 (`throttle_min` semantics: 0 = no throttle, every block fires; BEL safety floor still fires; `tier2_enabled` separate switch for full disable), §5 Q5.2 (OSC 9 + BEL only — no OSC 777), §5 Q5.3 (resume archives to `archive/blocked/<ts>.md`), §7 S4 (terminal capability auto-detect via `$TERM_PROGRAM`: kitty / Ghostty / iTerm.app supported), §5 line 211–212 (AFK-abort fires Tier 2 unconditionally — terminal events bypass throttle), §6 task-abort transition (Tier 1+2 fire as final emission for `aborted_*`).

**Goal:** Stand up `scripts/flow_notification.py` with the `Notifier` class that owns all 3 tiers:
- **Tier 1** (`blocked.md`): atomic write via T5/T6's `write_blocked` helper. ALWAYS writes — `throttle_min` does NOT affect Tier 1.
- **Tier 2** (OSC 9 + BEL): respects `throttle_min` (default 5 min, 0 = always fire) per `(task_id, issue_id)` key. `tier2_enabled=false` disables BOTH OSC 9 and BEL — only Tier 1 left. Terminal capability auto-detected via `$TERM_PROGRAM`; falls back to BEL-only if OSC 9 unsupported.
- **Tier 3** (shell hook): schema field `notification.command` ACCEPTED but NOT executed in v0.8.1 (deferred to v0.8.2 per PRD §3). T16 logs that the field was provided but skipped.

**Terminal OSC 9 capability matrix (S4 audit)**:

| `$TERM_PROGRAM` | OSC 9 supported? | Fallback |
|-----------------|------------------|----------|
| `kitty` | yes | n/a |
| `ghostty` | yes | n/a |
| `iTerm.app` | yes | n/a |
| anything else / unset | no | BEL-only (still respects `tier2_enabled`) |

**Throttle persistence**: state lives at `.flow/tasks/<slug>/.notification_throttle.json` (`atomic_write_json`):

```json
{"<task_id>::<issue_id>": "2026-05-06T00:05:00Z"}
```

Reader/writer locked via `fcntl.flock` (already wrapped by `safe_io.append_jsonl_locked` pattern; T16 uses a small read-modify-write helper analogous to `locked_text_rmw`).

**`Notifier` API**:

```python
class Notifier:
    def __init__(self, *, contract: Contract, slug: str, task_dir: Path,
                 term_program: Optional[str] = None): ...
    def fire_block(
        self, *,
        block_type: str, phase: int, task_id: str, issue_id: str,
        why_blocked: str, required_choice: list[str],
        safe_resume_command: str, frontmatter_extra: Optional[dict] = None,
    ) -> Path: ...
    def fire_terminal(
        self, *,
        block_type: str, task_id: str, issue_id: str, body: str,
    ) -> None:
        """For aborted_* states (§1 rows 12, 16). Tier 2 fires
        UNCONDITIONALLY — bypasses throttle. NO Tier 1 (aborts write to
        aborted/ directory, not blocked.md)."""
    def archive_on_resume(self, *, ts: str) -> Path: ...
```

- [ ] **Step 16.1: Failing test — Tier 2 OSC 9 emitted when `$TERM_PROGRAM=kitty`**

  ```python
  # tests/unit/test_notification_throttle_semantics.py
  import io, json, os, sys, tempfile, unittest
  from pathlib import Path
  from unittest.mock import patch

  REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent.parent
  sys.path.insert(0, str(REPO_ROOT / "scripts"))
  from flow_notification import Notifier  # type: ignore
  from flow_contract import Contract


  class TestTier2Emission(unittest.TestCase):
      def setUp(self):
          self.tmp = tempfile.mkdtemp()
          self.addCleanup(lambda: __import__("shutil").rmtree(self.tmp))
          self.contract = Contract(
              contract_schema_version=1, autonomy_mode="auto",
              created_at="2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
              notification={"command": None, "throttle_min": 0,
                            "tier2_enabled": True},
          )

      def _notifier(self, term="kitty"):
          n = Notifier(contract=self.contract, slug="demo",
                       task_dir=Path(self.tmp), term_program=term)
          n._stderr = io.StringIO()  # capture for test
          return n

      def test_kitty_emits_osc9_plus_bel(self):
          n = self._notifier(term="kitty")
          n.fire_block(
              block_type="acceptance_fail", phase=2,
              task_id="T1", issue_id="abc12345",
              why_blocked="x", required_choice=["abort_task"],
              safe_resume_command="flow resume demo",
          )
          out = n._stderr.getvalue()
          self.assertIn("\x1b]9;", out)  # OSC 9
          self.assertIn("\x07", out)     # BEL safety floor

      def test_unknown_terminal_falls_back_to_bel_only(self):
          n = self._notifier(term="screen")
          n.fire_block(
              block_type="acceptance_fail", phase=2,
              task_id="T1", issue_id="abc12345",
              why_blocked="x", required_choice=["abort_task"],
              safe_resume_command="flow resume demo",
          )
          out = n._stderr.getvalue()
          self.assertNotIn("\x1b]9;", out)
          self.assertIn("\x07", out)
  ```

- [ ] **Step 16.2: Implement `Notifier.__init__` + Tier 1+2 dispatch**

  ```python
  """flow_notification — Tier 1+2 emitter for v0.8.1 autonomy."""
  from __future__ import annotations

  import datetime, fcntl, json, os, sys
  from dataclasses import dataclass
  from pathlib import Path
  from typing import Optional

  sys.path.insert(0, str(Path(__file__).resolve().parent / "common"))
  from safe_io import atomic_write_json, locked_text_rmw

  sys.path.insert(0, str(Path(__file__).resolve().parent))
  from flow_contract import Contract
  from flow_state_writer import write_blocked  # T5/T6 v0.8.0 helper


  OSC9_TERM_ALLOWLIST = ("kitty", "ghostty", "iTerm.app")
  THROTTLE_FILENAME = ".notification_throttle.json"


  class Notifier:
      def __init__(
          self,
          *,
          contract: Contract,
          slug: str,
          task_dir: Path,
          term_program: Optional[str] = None,
      ):
          self.contract = contract
          self.slug = slug
          self.task_dir = task_dir
          self.term_program = term_program or os.environ.get("TERM_PROGRAM", "")
          self._stderr = sys.stderr  # overridable for testing

      def _osc9_supported(self) -> bool:
          return self.term_program in OSC9_TERM_ALLOWLIST

      def fire_block(
          self,
          *,
          block_type: str,
          phase: int,
          task_id: str,
          issue_id: str,
          why_blocked: str,
          required_choice: list[str],
          safe_resume_command: str,
          frontmatter_extra: Optional[dict] = None,
      ) -> Path:
          # Tier 1: ALWAYS write blocked.md
          path = write_blocked(
              self.task_dir, phase=phase, task=task_id,
              why_blocked=why_blocked,
              required_choice=required_choice,
              safe_resume_command=safe_resume_command,
          )
          # Tier 2: throttled
          self._maybe_fire_tier2(block_type=block_type,
                                  task_id=task_id,
                                  issue_id=issue_id,
                                  body=why_blocked)
          # Tier 3: schema-only (deferred v0.8.2)
          if self.contract.notification.get("command"):
              print(
                  f"NOTE: notification.command is set but Tier 3 hooks "
                  f"are deferred to v0.8.2 — field accepted, not executed.",
                  file=self._stderr,
              )
          return path

      def fire_terminal(
          self, *,
          block_type: str, task_id: str, issue_id: str, body: str,
      ) -> None:
          """§1 rows 12/16 + §5 line 211–212: terminal events bypass throttle."""
          self._emit_tier2(body=body, with_osc9=self._osc9_supported())

      def _maybe_fire_tier2(
          self, *,
          block_type: str, task_id: str, issue_id: str, body: str,
      ) -> None:
          if not self.contract.notification.get("tier2_enabled", True):
              return  # full disable: skip BOTH OSC 9 and BEL
          if not self._allowed_by_throttle(task_id=task_id,
                                            issue_id=issue_id):
              return  # throttled — no emission
          self._emit_tier2(body=body, with_osc9=self._osc9_supported())

      def _emit_tier2(self, *, body: str, with_osc9: bool) -> None:
          # OSC 9 desktop notification + BEL safety floor
          parts = []
          if with_osc9:
              # OSC 9 ; <text> BEL — Apple's iTerm format; kitty + Ghostty support same
              parts.append(f"\x1b]9;flow blocked: {body}\x07")
          else:
              # BEL-only floor
              parts.append("\x07")
          self._stderr.write("".join(parts))
          self._stderr.flush() if hasattr(self._stderr, "flush") else None
  ```

  Re-run Step 16.1 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 16.3: Failing tests — throttle semantics (R9 + Q5.1)**

  ```python
  class TestThrottleSemantics(unittest.TestCase):
      def setUp(self):
          self.tmp = tempfile.mkdtemp()
          self.addCleanup(lambda: __import__("shutil").rmtree(self.tmp))

      def _notifier(self, throttle_min, tier2_enabled=True):
          contract = Contract(
              contract_schema_version=1, autonomy_mode="auto",
              created_at="2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
              notification={"command": None,
                            "throttle_min": throttle_min,
                            "tier2_enabled": tier2_enabled},
          )
          n = Notifier(contract=contract, slug="d",
                       task_dir=Path(self.tmp), term_program="kitty")
          n._stderr = io.StringIO()
          return n

      def test_throttle_zero_fires_every_event(self):
          """R9 clarified: throttle_min=0 = no throttle, every event fires."""
          n = self._notifier(throttle_min=0)
          for _ in range(3):
              n.fire_block(block_type="x", phase=2, task_id="T1",
                           issue_id="i1", why_blocked="x",
                           required_choice=["abort"],
                           safe_resume_command="flow resume d")
          # 3 OSC 9 emissions (separated by other text)
          self.assertEqual(n._stderr.getvalue().count("\x1b]9;"), 3)

      def test_throttle_5min_suppresses_same_task_issue(self):
          n = self._notifier(throttle_min=5)
          for _ in range(3):
              n.fire_block(block_type="x", phase=2, task_id="T1",
                           issue_id="i1", why_blocked="x",
                           required_choice=["abort"],
                           safe_resume_command="flow resume d")
          # Only first emission; second + third throttled
          self.assertEqual(n._stderr.getvalue().count("\x1b]9;"), 1)

      def test_throttle_does_not_suppress_tier1(self):
          """§5 row Tier 1: always writes blocked.md regardless of throttle."""
          n = self._notifier(throttle_min=5)
          for i in range(3):
              n.fire_block(block_type="x", phase=2, task_id="T1",
                           issue_id="i1", why_blocked=f"event {i}",
                           required_choice=["abort"],
                           safe_resume_command="flow resume d")
          # blocked.md exists each time (overwritten); content reflects last event
          self.assertTrue((Path(self.tmp) / "blocked.md").exists())

      def test_tier2_disabled_silences_both_osc9_and_bel(self):
          n = self._notifier(throttle_min=0, tier2_enabled=False)
          n.fire_block(block_type="x", phase=2, task_id="T1",
                       issue_id="i1", why_blocked="x",
                       required_choice=["abort"],
                       safe_resume_command="flow resume d")
          self.assertNotIn("\x1b]9;", n._stderr.getvalue())
          self.assertNotIn("\x07", n._stderr.getvalue())

      def test_throttle_does_not_apply_across_different_issue_ids(self):
          n = self._notifier(throttle_min=5)
          n.fire_block(block_type="x", phase=2, task_id="T1",
                       issue_id="i1", why_blocked="x",
                       required_choice=["abort"],
                       safe_resume_command="flow resume d")
          n.fire_block(block_type="y", phase=2, task_id="T1",
                       issue_id="i2", why_blocked="y",
                       required_choice=["abort"],
                       safe_resume_command="flow resume d")
          # Different (task, issue) keys → both fire
          self.assertEqual(n._stderr.getvalue().count("\x1b]9;"), 2)

      def test_terminal_event_bypasses_throttle(self):
          """§5 line 211–212: AFK-abort terminal events fire unconditionally."""
          n = self._notifier(throttle_min=5)
          # Burn the throttle window
          n.fire_block(block_type="x", phase=2, task_id="T1", issue_id="i1",
                       why_blocked="x", required_choice=["abort"],
                       safe_resume_command="flow resume d")
          # Now fire terminal — should still emit
          n.fire_terminal(block_type="aborted_afk", task_id="T1",
                          issue_id="i1", body="afk timeout reached")
          # 2 emissions: 1 from fire_block + 1 from fire_terminal
          self.assertEqual(n._stderr.getvalue().count("\x1b]9;"), 2)
  ```

- [ ] **Step 16.4: Implement throttle persistence**

  ```python
  def _allowed_by_throttle(
      self, *, task_id: str, issue_id: str,
  ) -> bool:
      """Returns True if (task, issue) is OUTSIDE the throttle window.
      throttle_min=0 → always True (no throttle).
      Persisted state at task_dir/.notification_throttle.json.
      """
      throttle_min = int(self.contract.notification.get("throttle_min", 5))
      if throttle_min <= 0:
          return True
      key = f"{task_id}::{issue_id}"
      now = datetime.datetime.now(datetime.UTC)
      path = self.task_dir / THROTTLE_FILENAME

      def _read_state() -> dict:
          if not path.is_file():
              return {}
          try:
              return json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
          except json.JSONDecodeError:
              return {}

      state = _read_state()
      last_iso = state.get(key)
      if last_iso:
          try:
              last = datetime.datetime.fromisoformat(
                  last_iso.replace("Z", "+00:00"))
              age_sec = (now - last).total_seconds()
              if age_sec < throttle_min * 60:
                  return False
          except ValueError:
              pass  # malformed → re-fire is safer than silent suppression

      # Update state (record this firing)
      state[key] = now.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ")
      atomic_write_json(path, state)
      return True
  ```

  Re-run Step 16.3 → PASS.

  ```python
  def test_resume_archive_moves_blocked_md(self):
      """Q5.3: live blocked.md → archive/blocked/<ts>.md on resume."""
      n = self._notifier(throttle_min=0)
      n.fire_block(block_type="x", phase=2, task_id="T1", issue_id="i1",
                   why_blocked="x", required_choice=["abort"],
                   safe_resume_command="flow resume d")
      live_path = Path(self.tmp) / "blocked.md"
      self.assertTrue(live_path.exists())
      archived = n.archive_on_resume(ts="2026-05-06T00:05:00Z")
      self.assertFalse(live_path.exists())
      self.assertTrue(archived.exists())
      self.assertEqual(archived.parent.name, "blocked")
      self.assertEqual(archived.parent.parent.name, "archive")
  ```

- [ ] **Step 16.6: Implement `archive_on_resume`**

  ```python
  def archive_on_resume(self, *, ts: str) -> Path:
      """Q5.3: atomic-move blocked.md → archive/blocked/<ts>.md.
      Live blocked.md removed only after archive write succeeds (rename
      is atomic per POSIX within a filesystem)."""
      live = self.task_dir / "blocked.md"
      if not live.is_file():
          raise FileNotFoundError(f"no blocked.md to archive at {live}")
      archive_dir = self.task_dir / "archive" / "blocked"
      archive_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
      safe_ts = ts.replace(":", "-")
      target = archive_dir / f"{safe_ts}.md"
      os.replace(live, target)
      return target
  ```

  Re-run Step 16.5 → PASS.

### Task 19: Crash recovery dispatcher + verification-worktree orphan recovery

**Files:**
- Modify: `scripts/flow_orchestrator.py`
- Create: `tests/smoke/test_post_auto_engaged_crash_blocks.py` (ship-required) — owns the post-engaged subprocess assertion AND the related orchestrator-subprocess assertions for mid-merge + auto_prepare-lock recovery (consolidated here so the test file owner is unambiguous: T19 owns all orchestrator-entry recovery subprocess assertions; T5 + T14 unit tests stay in their respective ship-required files).

**Design refs:** §6 pre-`auto_prepare.lock` crash (fail-closed → interactive — legal, user never opted in), §6 R10 + §8.1 (lock+no-engaged+dead-pid → `block` with `block_type=auto_prepare_interrupted`), §6 + §7 contradiction-fix (post-`auto_engaged` crash → `block + user choice`, NEVER silent fallback to interactive), §6 R3 mid-merge crash (between `merge_started` and terminal merge event → reconcile block), §4 Y4 + §6 line 250 (verification-worktree orphan: live verify worktree without matching `post_merge_verification_completed` AND dead orchestrator pid → `block_type=verification_worktree_orphaned`).

**Goal:** Add `CrashRecoveryDispatcher` class — single entry point at orchestrator startup that classifies the run state and dispatches to one of 5 paths:

| State | Detection | Dispatch |
|-------|-----------|----------|
| 0 — clean | no lock + no `auto_engaged` events for run/task | proceed normally (T10's `auto_dispatch_task`) |
| 1 — pre-lock crash | no lock + no `auto_engaged` BUT `progress.md.autonomy_mode=auto` + no run history | fail-closed → interactive (legal; user never opted in) |
| 2 — lock+dead-pid | T5's `detect_auto_prepare_state` returns `interrupted_dead_pid` OR `interrupted_contract_changed` | block with `block_type=auto_prepare_interrupted` (R10) |
| 3 — post-`auto_engaged` crash | `auto_engaged` exists, no matching `task_completed` / `aborted_*` / `post_merge_verify_failed` (and no mid-merge case 4) | block with `block_type=auto_engaged_crashed`; choices `{resume_from_last_safe_state, abort_task, switch_to_interactive}` (Q7.2 + §6/§7 contradiction-fix) |
| 4 — mid-merge crash | T14's `detect_mid_merge_crash` returns `mid_merge_crash` or `mid_gate8_crash` | block with R3 reconcile choices |
| 5 — verification-worktree orphan | live verify worktree path exists; no matching `post_merge_verification_completed`; orchestrator pid (from lock or last run-record) is dead | block with `block_type=verification_worktree_orphaned` (Y4 + §6 line 250) |

T15 owns the verification worktree LIFECYCLE (create / cleanup-on-pass / preserve-on-fail). T19 owns orphan RECOVERY only — handles the case where orchestrator died WHILE gate 8 was still running (worktree alive on disk, no completion event written).

**Output**: `RecoveryVerdict { state, action, blocked_md_path?, choices? }`. Dispatcher caller (orchestrator main entry) consumes verdict + halts vs proceeds accordingly.

- [ ] **Step 19.1: Failing test — clean state returns `proceed`**

  ```python
  # tests/smoke/test_post_auto_engaged_crash_blocks.py
  class TestCrashRecoveryDispatcher(unittest.TestCase):
      def setUp(self):
          self.tmp = tempfile.mkdtemp()
          self.addCleanup(lambda: __import__("shutil").rmtree(self.tmp))
          self.task_dir = Path(self.tmp) / ".flow" / "tasks" / "demo"
          self.task_dir.mkdir(parents=True)

      def test_state0_clean_proceed(self):

              task_dir=self.task_dir, slug="demo",
              run_id="r1", task_id="T0",
              current_contract_hash="a"*64,
  ```

- [ ] **Step 19.2: Implement `CrashRecoveryDispatcher` skeleton + state 0/1**

  ```python
  @dataclass
  class RecoveryVerdict:
      state: str                              # clean | pre_lock_crash | auto_prepare_interrupted | auto_engaged_crashed | mid_merge_crash | mid_gate8_crash | verification_worktree_orphaned
      action: str                             # proceed | fail_closed_interactive | block
      block_type: Optional[str] = None
      choices: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
      blocked_md_path: Optional[Path] = None
      details: dict = field(default_factory=dict)


  class CrashRecoveryDispatcher:
      def __init__(
          self, *,
          task_dir: Path, slug: str, run_id: str, task_id: str,
          current_contract_hash: str,
          repo_root: Path,
          notifier=None,                        # T16 Notifier; optional for tests
      ):
          self.task_dir = task_dir
          self.slug = slug
          self.run_id = run_id
          self.task_id = task_id
          self.current_contract_hash = current_contract_hash
          self.repo_root = repo_root
          self.notifier = notifier

      def classify(self) -> RecoveryVerdict:
          # State 2: lock-based detection from T5
          lock_state = detect_auto_prepare_state(
              self.task_dir,
              run_id=self.run_id, task_id=self.task_id,
              current_contract_hash=self.current_contract_hash,
          )
          ls = lock_state["state"]
          if ls in ("interrupted_dead_pid", "interrupted_contract_changed"):
              return self._block_auto_prepare_interrupted(lock_state)

          # State 4: mid-merge / mid-gate-8 detection from T14
          merge_state = detect_mid_merge_crash(
              self.task_dir, run_id=self.run_id, task_id=self.task_id)
          if merge_state["state"] == "mid_merge_crash":
              return self._block_mid_merge_crash(merge_state)
          if merge_state["state"] == "mid_gate8_crash":
              # Could also be verification orphan — defer to state 5 check
              orphan = self._classify_verification_orphan()
              if orphan is not None:
                  return orphan
              return self._block_mid_gate8_crash(merge_state)

          # State 5: verification worktree orphan (only meaningful AFTER
          # merge_applied event exists)
          orphan = self._classify_verification_orphan()
          if orphan is not None:
              return orphan

          # State 3: post-auto_engaged crash (no matching terminal event)
          if self._has_post_auto_engaged_crash():
              return self._block_post_auto_engaged_crash()

          # State 1: pre-lock crash (autonomy_mode=auto in progress.md but
          # no lock + no engaged + no run history → first run aborted
          # before reaching contract parse)
          if ls == "no_run" and self._was_auto_intended():
              return RecoveryVerdict(
                  state="pre_lock_crash",
                  action="fail_closed_interactive",
                  details={"reason": "no auto run boundary written; "
                                       "user never opted in this attempt"},
              )

          # State 0: clean
          return RecoveryVerdict(state="clean", action="proceed")

      def _was_auto_intended(self) -> bool:
          progress_path = self.task_dir / "progress.md"
          if not progress_path.is_file():
              return False
          try:
              meta = read_progress_meta(progress_path)
              return meta.autonomy_mode == "auto"
          except Exception:
              return False
  ```

  Re-run Step 19.1 → PASS.

  ```python
          lock_version=1, slug="demo", run_id="r1", task_id="T0",
          contract_path="/c.json", contract_hash="a"*64,
  ```

- [ ] **Step 19.4: Implement `_block_auto_prepare_interrupted` + emit event (Y8 partner)**

  ```python
  def _block_auto_prepare_interrupted(self, lock_state: dict) -> RecoveryVerdict:
      """R10: write blocked.md (block_review_state variant) +
      emit auto_prepare_interrupted decision event (T6 EVENT_AUTO_PREPARE_INTERRUPTED)."""
      blocked_path = self.task_dir / "blocked.md"
      choices = ["resume_auto_from_prepare", "abort_task",
                  "switch_to_interactive"]
      # Use Notifier when present; else fall back to write_blocked
      if self.notifier is not None:
          self.notifier.fire_block(
              block_type="auto_prepare_interrupted", phase=2,
              task_id=self.task_id, issue_id="auto_prepare_interrupted",
              why_blocked=(f"auto preparation interrupted "
                           f"({lock_state['state']}); "
                           f"manual recovery required"),
              required_choice=choices,
              safe_resume_command=f"flow orchestrator --resume-auto-prepare {self.slug}",
          )
      else:
          write_blocked(
              self.task_dir, phase=2, task=self.task_id,
              why_blocked=f"auto_prepare_interrupted ({lock_state['state']})",
              required_choice=choices,
              safe_resume_command=f"flow orchestrator --resume-auto-prepare {self.slug}",
          )
      append_autonomy_event(
          self.task_dir, EVENT_AUTO_PREPARE_INTERRUPTED, {
              "event_id": _new_event_id(),
              "ts": _now_iso(),
              "slug": self.slug,
              "run_id": self.run_id, "task_id": self.task_id,
              "lock_path": str(self.task_dir / AUTO_PREPARE_LOCK_FILENAME),
              "blocked_md_path": str(blocked_path),
          })
      return RecoveryVerdict(
          state="auto_prepare_interrupted",
          action="block",
          block_type="auto_prepare_interrupted",
          choices=choices,
          blocked_md_path=blocked_path,
          details={"lock_state": lock_state["state"]},
      )
  ```

  Re-run Step 19.3 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 19.5: Failing test — state 3 post-`auto_engaged` crash blocks (ship-required smoke)**

  Per design §7 line 312:

  ```python
  def test_state3_post_auto_engaged_crash_blocks(self):
      """Q7.2 + §6/§7 contradiction-fix: post-auto_engaged crash MUST
      block + user choice — NEVER silent fallback to interactive."""
      # Write auto_engaged event but no terminal event
      append_autonomy_event(self.task_dir, EVENT_AUTO_ENGAGED, {
          "event_id": "e1", "ts": "2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
          "slug": "demo", "run_id": "r1", "task_id": "T0",
          "worktree_id": "demo+t0+abc1234",
          "worktree_path": str(self.tmp + "/wt"),
          "original_base_commit": "abc"*7+"1",
          "current_base_commit": "abc"*7+"1",
          "lifecycle_state": "active", "checkpoint_id": None,
          "contract_path": "/c.json", "contract_hash": "a"*64,
          "contract_schema_version": 1,
      })
      v = CrashRecoveryDispatcher(
          task_dir=self.task_dir, slug="demo",
          run_id="r1", task_id="T0",
          current_contract_hash="a"*64,
          repo_root=Path(self.tmp),
      ).classify()
      self.assertEqual(v.state, "auto_engaged_crashed")
      self.assertEqual(v.action, "block")
      for needed in ("resume_from_last_safe_state", "abort_task",
                     "switch_to_interactive"):
          self.assertIn(needed, v.choices)

  def test_state3_progress_md_autonomy_mode_unchanged(self):
      """The hard rule: post-auto_engaged crash NEVER silently switches mode."""
      (self.task_dir / "progress.md").write_text(
          "---\nautonomy_mode: auto\ncontract_path: contract.json\n---\n")
      append_autonomy_event(self.task_dir, EVENT_AUTO_ENGAGED, {
          "event_id": "e1", "ts": "2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
          "slug": "demo", "run_id": "r1", "task_id": "T0",
          "worktree_id": "demo+t0+abcdefg",
          "worktree_path": str(self.tmp + "/wt"),
          "original_base_commit": "a"*40,
          "current_base_commit": "a"*40,
          "lifecycle_state": "active", "checkpoint_id": None,
          "contract_path": "/c.json", "contract_hash": "a"*64,
          "contract_schema_version": 1,
      })
      CrashRecoveryDispatcher(
          task_dir=self.task_dir, slug="demo", run_id="r1", task_id="T0",
          current_contract_hash="a"*64,
          repo_root=Path(self.tmp),
      ).classify()
      meta = read_progress_meta(self.task_dir / "progress.md")
      self.assertEqual(meta.autonomy_mode, "auto")  # NOT silently flipped
  ```

- [ ] **Step 19.6: Implement `_has_post_auto_engaged_crash` + `_block_post_auto_engaged_crash`**

  ```python
  TERMINAL_TASK_EVENTS = (
      EVENT_TASK_COMPLETED,
      EVENT_POST_MERGE_VERIFY_FAILED,
      # aborted_* are recorded in decisions.jsonl too
  )

  def _has_post_auto_engaged_crash(self) -> bool:
      """auto_engaged event exists for this run/task, but no matching
      terminal event (task_completed / post_merge_verify_failed / aborted)."""
      events = []
      path = self.task_dir / "decisions.jsonl"
      if not path.is_file():
          return False
      for line in path.read_text(encoding="utf-8").splitlines():
          try:
              rec = json.loads(line)
          except json.JSONDecodeError:
              continue
          if (rec.get("run_id") == self.run_id
                  and rec.get("task_id") == self.task_id):
              events.append(rec)
      kinds = [e.get("event") for e in events]
      decisions = [e.get("decision") for e in events]
      if EVENT_AUTO_ENGAGED not in kinds:
          return False
      # Any terminal event present?
      for terminal in TERMINAL_TASK_EVENTS:
          if terminal in kinds:
              return False
      # aborted_* checked separately (lives in `decision` field, not `event`)
      if any(d and d.startswith("aborted_") for d in decisions):
          return False
      return True

  def _block_post_auto_engaged_crash(self) -> RecoveryVerdict:
      blocked_path = self.task_dir / "blocked.md"
      choices = ["resume_from_last_safe_state", "abort_task",
                  "switch_to_interactive"]
      if self.notifier is not None:
          self.notifier.fire_block(
              block_type="auto_engaged_crashed", phase=2,
              task_id=self.task_id, issue_id="auto_engaged_crashed",
              why_blocked=("auto run interrupted post-engagement; "
                            "explicit user choice required"),
              required_choice=choices,
              safe_resume_command=f"flow orchestrator --resume {self.slug}",
          )
      else:
          write_blocked(
              self.task_dir, phase=2, task=self.task_id,
              why_blocked="auto_engaged_crashed",
              required_choice=choices,
              safe_resume_command=f"flow orchestrator --resume {self.slug}",
          )
      return RecoveryVerdict(
          state="auto_engaged_crashed",
          action="block",
          block_type="auto_engaged_crashed",
          choices=choices,
          blocked_md_path=blocked_path,
      )
  ```

  Re-run Step 19.5 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 19.7: Failing test — state 4 mid-merge dispatcher routing (consumes T14)**

  ```python
  def test_state4_mid_merge_routes_to_block(self):
      append_autonomy_event(self.task_dir, EVENT_AUTO_ENGAGED, {
          "event_id": "e1", "ts": "t", "slug": "demo",
          "run_id": "r1", "task_id": "T0",
          "worktree_id": "w", "worktree_path": "/tmp/wt",
          "original_base_commit": "a"*40, "current_base_commit": "a"*40,
          "lifecycle_state": "active", "checkpoint_id": None,
          "contract_path": "/c.json", "contract_hash": "a"*64,
          "contract_schema_version": 1,
      })
      append_autonomy_event(self.task_dir, EVENT_MERGE_STARTED, {
          "event_id": "e2", "ts": "t", "slug": "demo",
          "run_id": "r1", "task_id": "T0",
          "worktree_id": "w", "worktree_path": "/tmp/wt",
          "integration_target": "master",
          "target_commit_pre_merge": "deadbeef",
      })
      v = CrashRecoveryDispatcher(
          task_dir=self.task_dir, slug="demo",
          run_id="r1", task_id="T0",
          current_contract_hash="a"*64,
          repo_root=Path(self.tmp),
      ).classify()
      self.assertEqual(v.state, "mid_merge_crash")

                "switch_to_interactive"):
  ```

- [ ] **Step 19.8: Implement `_block_mid_merge_crash` + `_block_mid_gate8_crash`**

  ```python
  def _block_mid_merge_crash(self, merge_state: dict) -> RecoveryVerdict:
      blocked_path = self.task_dir / "blocked.md"
      choices = merge_state.get("choices", [])
      if self.notifier is not None:
          self.notifier.fire_block(
              block_type="atomic_merge_crashed", phase=2,
              task_id=self.task_id, issue_id="atomic_merge_crashed",
              why_blocked=("git merge transaction crashed between "
                            "merge_started and merge_applied"),
              required_choice=choices,
              safe_resume_command=f"flow orchestrator --resume {self.slug}",
          )
      else:
          write_blocked(
              self.task_dir, phase=2, task=self.task_id,
              why_blocked="atomic_merge_crashed",
              required_choice=choices,
              safe_resume_command=f"flow orchestrator --resume {self.slug}",
          )
      return RecoveryVerdict(
          state="mid_merge_crash", action="block",
          block_type="atomic_merge_crashed",
          choices=choices, blocked_md_path=blocked_path,
      )

  def _block_mid_gate8_crash(self, merge_state: dict) -> RecoveryVerdict:
      # Mid-gate-8 without orphan worktree → orchestrator died after
      # merge_applied but before any verification event. Treated like
      # mid-merge crash but with different choices.
      blocked_path = self.task_dir / "blocked.md"
      choices = merge_state.get("choices",
          ["rerun_post_merge_verify", "abort_and_revert_partial",
           "switch_to_interactive"])
      if self.notifier is not None:
          self.notifier.fire_block(
              block_type="post_merge_verify_in_progress_crash",
              phase=3,
              task_id=self.task_id,
              issue_id="post_merge_verify_in_progress_crash",
              why_blocked=("post-merge verification was running when "
                            "orchestrator crashed; user must choose "
                            "rerun / revert / interactive"),
              required_choice=choices,
              safe_resume_command=f"flow orchestrator --resume {self.slug}",
          )
      return RecoveryVerdict(
          state="mid_gate8_crash", action="block",
          block_type="post_merge_verify_in_progress_crash",
          choices=choices, blocked_md_path=blocked_path,
      )
  ```

  Re-run Step 19.7 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 19.9: Failing test — state 5 verification-worktree orphan (Y4)**

  ```python
  def test_state5_verification_orphan_blocks(self):
      """§4 Y4: live verify worktree path AND no completion event AND
      orchestrator pid is dead → block_type=verification_worktree_orphaned."""
      # Simulate: merge_applied + post_merge_verification_started, no
      # completed event; verify worktree exists on disk.
      verify_path = (Path(self.tmp) / ".claude" / "worktrees" / "verify"
                     / "r1+t0+deadbee")
      verify_path.mkdir(parents=True)
      append_autonomy_event(self.task_dir, EVENT_MERGE_APPLIED, {
          "event_id": "e1", "ts": "t", "slug": "demo",
          "run_id": "r1", "task_id": "T0", "worktree_id": "w",
          "target_commit_post_merge": "deadbeef" + "0"*32,
          "merge_strategy": "--ff-only",
      })
      append_autonomy_event(self.task_dir, EVENT_POST_MERGE_VERIFICATION_STARTED, {
          "event_id": "e2", "ts": "t", "slug": "demo",
          "run_id": "r1", "task_id": "T0",
          "verification_worktree_id": "r1+t0+deadbee",
          "verification_worktree_path": str(verify_path),
          "target_commit_post_merge": "deadbeef" + "0"*32,
      })
      # No verification_completed; T19 must detect orphan
      v = CrashRecoveryDispatcher(
          task_dir=self.task_dir, slug="demo",
          run_id="r1", task_id="T0",

                "revert_merge", "switch_to_interactive"):
  ```
