- [ ] **Step 19.10: Implement `_classify_verification_orphan`**

  ```python
  def _classify_verification_orphan(self) -> Optional[RecoveryVerdict]:
      """§6 line 250 + §4 Y4: scan .claude/worktrees/verify/ for live
      verification worktrees with no matching post_merge_verification_completed
      event for this run/task. Pid liveness already covered by lock detection.
      """
      events = []
      path = self.task_dir / "decisions.jsonl"
      if not path.is_file():
          return None
      for line in path.read_text(encoding="utf-8").splitlines():
          try:
              rec = json.loads(line)
          except json.JSONDecodeError:
              continue
          if (rec.get("run_id") == self.run_id
                  and rec.get("task_id") == self.task_id):
              events.append(rec)

      started = [e for e in events
                  if e.get("event") == EVENT_POST_MERGE_VERIFICATION_STARTED]
      completed = [e for e in events
                    if e.get("event") == EVENT_POST_MERGE_VERIFICATION_COMPLETED]
      if not started or completed:
          return None  # never started, or properly completed

      latest = started[-1]
      verify_path = Path(latest.get("verification_worktree_path", ""))
      if not verify_path.is_dir():
          return None  # worktree already cleaned up — not orphaned

      # Live worktree, no completion event → orphan
      blocked_path = self.task_dir / "blocked.md"
      choices = ["rerun_post_merge_verify", "accept_merge_anyway",
                  "revert_merge", "switch_to_interactive"]
      if self.notifier is not None:
          self.notifier.fire_block(
              block_type="verification_worktree_orphaned",
              phase=3,
              task_id=self.task_id,
              issue_id="verification_worktree_orphaned",
              why_blocked=(f"verification worktree {verify_path} alive but "
                            f"no post_merge_verification_completed event "
                            f"for run={self.run_id} task={self.task_id}"),
              required_choice=choices,
              safe_resume_command=f"flow orchestrator --resume {self.slug}",
          )
      return RecoveryVerdict(
          state="verification_worktree_orphaned",
          action="block",
          block_type="verification_worktree_orphaned",
          choices=choices,
          blocked_md_path=blocked_path,
          details={"verification_worktree_path": str(verify_path)},
      )
  ```

  Re-run Step 19.9 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 19.11: Wire `_cmd_auto_execute` — full dispatch loop (recovery → dispatch → gates 1–6 → merge → gate 8)**

  The v0.8.0 `--auto-execute` was an exit-2 stub. T19 Step 19.11 replaces it with the **end-to-end dispatch loop** (post-rescope: dispatch + recovery + gates + merge + post-merge verify, no AFK / Budget / retry / in-loop-staleness — those are v0.8.2): T19 `CrashRecoveryDispatcher` (recovery gate), T10/T11 `auto_dispatch_task` (per-task worktree + manifest verify), T12+T13 `GateRunner.run_phase2` (gates 1→3→4→5→6 — runs ONCE, no retry loop), T14 `MergeRunner.merge_task` (gate 7 + R3 atomic-merge sequence), T15 `Gate8VerificationRunner.verify` (gate 8 + 9a/9b), and `MergeQueue.can_proceed` (S1 wave block). A single `Notifier` is created at entry and threaded through every component so Tier 1+2 routing is consistent. Staleness is checked out-of-band via `flow doctor <slug>` (T20) — NOT gated in this loop for v0.8.1.

  Per §6 line 250 + Q7.2: every block path returns exit 3 (caller distinguishes from exit 4 nested-abort and exit 0 happy / interactive-fallback). Loop exits on the first non-pass; subsequent tasks remain `pending`.

  ```python
  # ── Helper: source gate command lines from contract or v0.8.0 defaults ──
  # Contract `gates` field is added in v0.8.2 per PRD §3 Future. For
  # v0.8.1, gate commands fall back to repo conventions established in
  # v0.8.0 (`bash tests/smoke/run.sh` for both baseline + smoke;
  # `codex review --diff-only --json` for gate 4). Override per-contract
  # via the optional top-level `gates` dict if present (silently ignored
  # by the v0.8.1 schema validator — forward-compat field).
  def _resolve_gate_commands(contract: Contract) -> dict:
      raw = getattr(contract, "_raw_gates", None) or {}
      return {
          "baseline": raw.get("baseline_command", "bash tests/smoke/run.sh"),
          "smoke":    raw.get("smoke_command",    "bash tests/smoke/run.sh"),
          "codex":    raw.get("codex_command",    "codex review --diff-only --json"),
          "merge_strategy": raw.get("merge_strategy", "--ff-only"),
      }


  # ── Helper: integration target resolution ──────────────────────────────
  # Contract may carry `integration_target` (forward-compat field —
  # silently ignored by v0.8.1 schema validator). v0.8.1 default = "master".
  # v0.8.2 may promote to required-validated field.
  def _resolve_integration_target(contract: Contract) -> str:
      return getattr(contract, "integration_target", None) or "master"


  # ── Helper: subagent dispatch shim ──────────────────────────────────────
  # T22 owns the SKILL implementation that actually invokes Claude CLI
  # via the configured capability. T19 defines the import boundary so the
  # dispatch loop is testable with a fake_dispatch fixture. Production
  # callable resolved lazily from claude/capabilities/defaults.json
  # (T22 promotes `autonomy_orchestrator` capability with this entry point).
  def _invoke_subagent_dispatch(ctx: WorktreeContext, **kw) -> None:
      """Resolved at runtime via T22's capability binding. v0.8.1 uses
      `claude/capabilities/defaults.json::autonomy_orchestrator.dispatch_cmd`
      (a shell command template that receives the worktree path + manifest
      id via env vars). The implementer wires this in T22 with a
      non-sandboxed shell call; codex-sandbox tests substitute a
      fake_dispatch via dependency injection (see Step 21.3 fixture)."""
      from importlib import import_module
      try:
          mod = import_module("flow_subagent_dispatch")  # T22 module
          mod.invoke(ctx, **kw)
      except ImportError:
          raise RuntimeError(
              "subagent dispatch capability not wired — set "
              "FLOW_SUBAGENT_DISPATCH_CMD env var or implement "
              "scripts/flow_subagent_dispatch.py via T22 SKILL")


  def _cmd_auto_execute(slug: str) -> int:
      plan = build_plan(slug)
      if plan.contract is None:
          # v0.8.0 fallback: contract missing/invalid → interactive.
          # The S5 nested-autonomy guard in main() runs BEFORE this point,
          # so a missing contract here is an end-user state, not nested.
          print(f"INFO: {plan.fallback_reason} — running interactive instead.",
                file=sys.stderr)
          return 0

      task_dir = _resolve_slug_dir(slug)
      repo_root = task_dir.parents[2]               # .flow/tasks/<slug>/.. → repo root
      contract_path = task_dir / "contract.json"
      contract_hash = hashlib.sha256(contract_path.read_bytes()).hexdigest()
      run_id = _resolve_or_create_run_id(task_dir)
      gate_cmds = _resolve_gate_commands(plan.contract)
      integration_target = _resolve_integration_target(plan.contract)
      criteria = list(plan.contract.acceptance_criteria or [])
      notifier = Notifier(contract=plan.contract, slug=slug, task_dir=task_dir)

      for task_idx, manifest in enumerate(plan.manifests):
          task_id = manifest.id

          # ── R10 + Q7.2: classify pre-dispatch recovery state ────────
          dispatcher = CrashRecoveryDispatcher(
              task_dir=task_dir, slug=slug,
              run_id=run_id, task_id=task_id,
              current_contract_hash=contract_hash,
              repo_root=repo_root, notifier=notifier,
          )
          v = dispatcher.classify()
          if v.action == "block":
              # Recovery dispatcher already wrote blocked.md via notifier.
              print(f"BLOCKED: {v.block_type} → see {v.blocked_md_path}",
                    file=sys.stderr)
              return 3
          if v.action == "fail_closed_interactive":
              # Pre-lock crash: user never opted in; legal silent fallback.
              # Distinct from post-auto_engaged crash (which MUST block).
              print(f"WARN: {v.details.get('reason')} — interactive fallback",
                    file=sys.stderr)
              return 0
          # v.action == "proceed"

          # ── T10/T11: dispatch subagent + verify manifest ────────────
          outcome = auto_dispatch_task(
              slug=slug, task_idx=task_idx, repo_root=repo_root,
              dispatch_fn=_invoke_subagent_dispatch,   # T22 SKILL impl
              contract=plan.contract, manifest=manifest,
              run_id=run_id,
              contract_path=contract_path,
              contract_hash=contract_hash,
              integration_target=integration_target,
              notifier=notifier,
          )
          if outcome.status == "blocked":
              # T11 wrote blocked.md (manifest_violation) via notifier.
              print(f"BLOCKED: {outcome.block_type} → see "
                    f"{outcome.blocked_md_path}", file=sys.stderr)
              return 3
          ctx, facts = outcome.ctx, outcome.facts

          # ── T20 staleness — DEFERRED v0.8.2 ─────────────────────────
          # Codex round-4 R4: staleness gate position should be BEFORE
          # auto_dispatch_task (else worktree+auto_engaged+subagent run
          # against stale state). v0.8.1 punts to out-of-band check via
          # `flow doctor <slug>`; user runs manually before invoking
          # --auto-execute. v0.8.2 adds StalenessChecker.check_all here.

          # ── T12+T13: Phase 2 gates 1→3→4→5→6 ────────────────────────
          gate_runner = GateRunner(
              ctx=ctx, contract=plan.contract, task_dir=task_dir,
              run_id=run_id, task_id=task_id,
              prior_baseline=_load_prior_baseline(task_dir, task_id),
          )
          attempt_id = f"{run_id}+{task_id}"
          verdict = gate_runner.run_phase2(
              manifest=manifest, facts=facts,
              criteria=criteria,
              attempt_id=attempt_id, retry_idx=0,
              baseline_command=gate_cmds["baseline"],
              codex_command=gate_cmds["codex"],
              smoke_command=gate_cmds["smoke"],
          )
          if verdict.status != "pass":
              # GateRunner methods do NOT write blocked.md themselves —
              # they return GateResult and let the caller route. Fire
              # block here using the halted-gate context. Retry loop is
              # out of scope for v0.8.1's first wire-up; T22's SKILL +
              # subagent retry budget (T18) handles round-N retries
              # before reaching this final-block step.
              gr = verdict.gate_result
              notifier.fire_block(
                  block_type=verdict.halted_at_gate,
                  phase=2, task_id=task_id,
                  issue_id=(gr.details or {}).get(
                      "issue_id", verdict.halted_at_gate),
                  why_blocked=(f"phase 2 halted at "
                                f"{verdict.halted_at_gate}: "
                                f"{(gr.details or {}).get('block_row', '?')}"),
                  required_choice=["abort_task", "switch_to_interactive"],
                  safe_resume_command=f"flow orchestrator --resume {slug}",
              )
              return 3

          # ── T14: gate 7 atomic merge (R3 9-step sequence steps 1–7) ─
          merger = MergeRunner(
              ctx=ctx, contract=plan.contract, task_dir=task_dir,
              run_id=run_id, task_id=task_id,
          )
          mr = merger.merge_task(
              facts=facts, merge_strategy=gate_cmds["merge_strategy"],
          )
          if mr.status != "merged":
              # MergeRunner returns blocked status on git-merge fail; T19
              # catches the mid-merge crash separately on next-startup.
              # Here the merge failed cleanly (returned, didn't crash).
              notifier.fire_block(
                  block_type="atomic_merge_failed", phase=2,
                  task_id=task_id, issue_id="atomic_merge_failed",
                  why_blocked=mr.block_reason or "git merge failed",
                  required_choice=["replay_merge_from_diff_hash",
                                    "abort_and_revert_partial",
                                    "switch_to_interactive"],
                  safe_resume_command=f"flow orchestrator --resume {slug}",
              )
              return 3

          # ── T15: gate 8 post-merge verify (9a PASS / 9b FAIL) ───────
          gate8 = Gate8VerificationRunner(
              ctx=ctx, contract=plan.contract, task_dir=task_dir,
              run_id=run_id, task_id=task_id,
              target_commit_post_merge=mr.target_commit_post_merge,
              notifier=notifier,
          )
          g8 = gate8.verify(
              criteria=criteria,
              regression_command=gate_cmds["smoke"],
          )
          if g8.status != "completed":
              # 9b path already wrote blocked.md via the injected notifier.
              print(f"BLOCKED: post_merge_verify_failed → see "
                    f"{g8.blocked_md_path}", file=sys.stderr)
              return 3

          # ── T15 S1: serialization gate before next task ─────────────
          if not MergeQueue(task_dir=task_dir,
                             run_id=run_id).can_proceed(task_id=task_id):
              # Earlier task in this run is unresolved blocked_post_merge.
              # MergeQueue is the wave-level halt; no notifier fire needed
              # because the originating block was already emitted.
              print(f"WAVE_HALTED: prior task in run {run_id} is "
                    f"unresolved blocked_post_merge", file=sys.stderr)
              return 3

      # All manifests merged + verified.
      return 0
  ```

  **Helpers introduced or referenced** (unchanged from prior steps unless noted):
  - `_resolve_gate_commands(contract)` — NEW. Sources baseline / smoke / codex / merge_strategy commands; honors a forward-compat `gates` dict on the contract raw, else uses v0.8.0 defaults.
  - `_resolve_or_create_run_id(task_dir)` — exists from T6 (`decisions.jsonl` run boundary writer).
  - `_load_prior_baseline(task_dir, task_id)` — NEW small helper that reads any prior `BaselineRecord` from `acceptance-progress.jsonl` (T4 writer); returns `None` if no prior record exists. Two-line implementation; treat as part of this step.
  - `_invoke_subagent_dispatch(ctx, **kw)` — owned by T22 SKILL implementation; T19 references it as the abstract dispatch_fn callable. T22 lands the concrete subagent invocation (Claude CLI / SKILL prompt) before this loop is exercised end-to-end.

  **What this step does NOT do** (post-rescope; all handled in v0.8.2):
  - Subagent invocation mechanics — T22 owns the SKILL + `flow_subagent_dispatch.py` shim.
  - Phase 2 retry-budget loop — DEFERRED to v0.8.2 (loop runs gates ONCE; first non-pass blocks via Notifier, no retry attempt).
  - AFK timeout — DEFERRED to v0.8.2 (T17 not in v0.8.1 plan).
  - BudgetTracker enforcement — DEFERRED to v0.8.2 (T18 not in v0.8.1 plan; contract `budget` dict accepted forward-compat but unused at runtime).
  - In-loop staleness gate — DEFERRED to v0.8.2 (T20 ships doctor-only in v0.8.1).

- [ ] **Step 19.12: Failing tests — full ship-required smoke `test_post_auto_engaged_crash_blocks.py` (3 subprocess scenarios)**

  Subprocess-driven end-to-end tests covering all three orchestrator-entry recovery paths (post-engaged crash + mid-merge crash + auto_prepare-lock crash). One file owns all three because the assertions all share the same fixture scaffolding (subprocess invocation of `flow_orchestrator --auto-execute <slug>` + assertion on returncode + blocked.md + progress.md autonomy_mode invariant). Per design §7 lines 312–314 (ship-required for the no-silent-mode-switch hard rule).

  ```python
  # tests/smoke/test_post_auto_engaged_crash_blocks.py
  import json, os, shutil, subprocess, sys, tempfile, unittest
  from pathlib import Path

  REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent.parent
  ORCH = REPO_ROOT / "scripts" / "flow_orchestrator.py"


  def _seed_task(slug_dir: Path, *, autonomy_mode: str = "auto") -> None:
      """Write the minimal fixture for an --auto-execute invocation:
      contract.json + progress.md frontmatter + an empty manifest list
      (the recovery dispatcher runs BEFORE the manifest loop dispatches)."""
      slug_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
      (slug_dir / "contract.json").write_text(json.dumps({
          "contract_schema_version": 1,
          "autonomy_mode": autonomy_mode,
          "created_at": "2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
      }))
      (slug_dir / "progress.md").write_text(
          f"---\nautonomy_mode: {autonomy_mode}\n"
          f"contract_path: contract.json\n---\n")
      (slug_dir / "manifest.md").write_text(
          "# Tasks\n\n- [ ] T0: noop\n")


  def _run_orchestrator(slug: str, *, repo_root: Path) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess:
      env = os.environ.copy()
      env.pop("FLOW_AUTONOMY_PARENT_PID", None)        # ensure top-level
      return subprocess.run(
          [sys.executable, str(ORCH), "--auto-execute", slug],
          cwd=str(repo_root), env=env,
          capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=30,
      )


  class TestPostAutoEngagedCrashBlocksEndToEnd(unittest.TestCase):
      """ship-required (§7 line 312): orchestrator MUST NEVER silently
      flip auto → interactive after a post-auto_engaged crash. All 3
      subprocess scenarios assert: returncode == 3, blocked.md exists,
      progress.md autonomy_mode unchanged."""

      def setUp(self):
          self.repo_root = Path(tempfile.mkdtemp(prefix="flow-test-"))
          self.addCleanup(lambda: shutil.rmtree(self.repo_root,
                                                  ignore_errors=True))
          subprocess.run(["git", "init", "-q", str(self.repo_root)],
                         check=True)
          # Minimal repo state: one commit on master so integration_target
          # exists for the dispatcher's git-state checks.
          (self.repo_root / "README.md").write_text("# fixture\n")
          subprocess.run(["git", "-C", str(self.repo_root),
                          "add", "README.md"], check=True)
          subprocess.run(["git", "-C", str(self.repo_root), "commit",
                          "-q", "-m", "init"], check=True,
                         env={**os.environ,
                              "GIT_AUTHOR_NAME": "t", "GIT_AUTHOR_EMAIL": "t@t",
                              "GIT_COMMITTER_NAME": "t", "GIT_COMMITTER_EMAIL": "t@t"})
          self.slug = "demo"
          self.slug_dir = self.repo_root / ".flow" / "tasks" / self.slug
          _seed_task(self.slug_dir)

      def test_orchestrator_subprocess_blocks_on_post_engaged_crash(self):
          # Seed the post-auto_engaged crash state: auto_engaged event
          # written, no terminal event.
          (self.slug_dir / "decisions.jsonl").write_text(json.dumps({
              "event": "auto_engaged", "event_id": "e1",
              "ts": "2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
              "slug": self.slug, "run_id": "r1", "task_id": "T0",
              "worktree_id": "demo+t0+abcdefg",
              "worktree_path": "/tmp/wt",
              "original_base_commit": "a"*40, "current_base_commit": "a"*40,
              "lifecycle_state": "active", "checkpoint_id": None,
              "contract_path": "contract.json", "contract_hash": "a"*64,
              "contract_schema_version": 1,
          }) + "\n")
          r = _run_orchestrator(self.slug, repo_root=self.repo_root)
          self.assertEqual(r.returncode, 3,
              msg=f"expected exit 3 (block); got {r.returncode}\n"
                  f"stdout={r.stdout!r}\nstderr={r.stderr!r}")
          blocked = (self.slug_dir / "blocked.md").read_text()
          self.assertIn("auto_engaged_crashed", blocked)
          self.assertIn("resume_from_last_safe_state", blocked)
          # The hard rule: autonomy_mode MUST NOT be silently flipped.
          progress = (self.slug_dir / "progress.md").read_text()
          self.assertIn("autonomy_mode: auto", progress)

      def test_orchestrator_subprocess_blocks_on_mid_merge_crash(self):
          # R3: merge_started written, no merge_applied. T14's
          # detect_mid_merge_crash + T19's CrashRecoveryDispatcher route
          # to atomic_merge_crashed block.
          events = [
              {"event": "auto_engaged", "event_id": "e1", "ts": "t",
               "slug": self.slug, "run_id": "r1", "task_id": "T0",
               "worktree_id": "demo+t0+abcdefg", "worktree_path": "/tmp/wt",
               "original_base_commit": "a"*40, "current_base_commit": "a"*40,
               "lifecycle_state": "active", "checkpoint_id": None,
               "contract_path": "contract.json", "contract_hash": "a"*64,
               "contract_schema_version": 1},
              {"event": "merge_started", "event_id": "e2", "ts": "t",
               "slug": self.slug, "run_id": "r1", "task_id": "T0",
               "worktree_id": "demo+t0+abcdefg", "worktree_path": "/tmp/wt",
               "integration_target": "master",
               "target_commit_pre_merge": "deadbeef"},
          ]
          (self.slug_dir / "decisions.jsonl").write_text(
              "\n".join(json.dumps(e) for e in events) + "\n")
          r = _run_orchestrator(self.slug, repo_root=self.repo_root)
          self.assertEqual(r.returncode, 3,
              msg=f"stderr={r.stderr!r}")
          blocked = (self.slug_dir / "blocked.md").read_text()
          self.assertIn("atomic_merge_crashed", blocked)
          self.assertIn("replay_merge_from_diff_hash", blocked)
          self.assertIn("autonomy_mode: auto",
                        (self.slug_dir / "progress.md").read_text())

      def test_orchestrator_subprocess_blocks_on_auto_prepare_lock_crash(self):
          # R10: auto_prepare.lock present, no auto_engaged event,
          # pid is dead → interrupted_dead_pid → block with
          # auto_prepare_interrupted.
          (self.slug_dir / "auto_prepare.lock").write_text(json.dumps({
              "lock_version": 1, "slug": self.slug,
              "run_id": "r1", "task_id": "T0",
              "contract_path": "contract.json", "contract_hash": "a"*64,
              "contract_schema_version": 1,
              "created_at": "2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
              "pid": 2**31 - 1,                   # guaranteed-dead pid
              "host": "x", "cwd": str(self.slug_dir),
              "target_branch": "master",
              "intended_first_task_dispatch_at": "2026-05-06T00:00:01Z",
          }))
          r = _run_orchestrator(self.slug, repo_root=self.repo_root)
          self.assertEqual(r.returncode, 3,
              msg=f"stderr={r.stderr!r}")
          blocked = (self.slug_dir / "blocked.md").read_text()
          self.assertIn("auto_prepare_interrupted", blocked)
          self.assertIn("resume_auto_from_prepare", blocked)
          self.assertIn("autonomy_mode: auto",
                        (self.slug_dir / "progress.md").read_text())


  if __name__ == "__main__":
      unittest.main()
  ```

  Each method is a real failing test (concrete fixtures, concrete subprocess invocation, concrete assertions) — not a `...` placeholder. The 3 methods cover every state-3 / state-4 / state-2 path through `CrashRecoveryDispatcher.classify()`. The unit-level coverage of the same paths lives in Steps 19.3 / 19.5 / 19.7 (single-process, no subprocess overhead).

---

### Task 20: 5 trigger-based staleness checks (doctor-only in v0.8.1; in-loop routing deferred to v0.8.2)

**Files:**
- Modify: `scripts/flow_doctor.py`
- Modify: `scripts/flow_staleness.py` (already exists from v0.7; T20 extends with the 5 triggers)
- Modify: `tests/smoke/test_orchestrator_worktree.py` (add staleness-trigger unit cases for each detector)

**Design refs:** §1 row 8 (`staleness trigger fires mid-task` → `block` with status `blocked_stale`, Tier 1+2, NEVER silent switch), PRD §1.1 staleness triggers (5 explicit triggers per Y2), §6 line 247 (resume from `stale` requires staleness-trigger source re-validated).

**Goal:** Promote v0.7's coarse `flow_staleness.py` (currently checks only base-branch advance) to the **5 explicit triggers** Y2 demands. Each trigger is independently checkable. **In v0.8.1 the triggers are exposed via `flow doctor <slug>` only** — user runs the doctor manually before invoking `--auto-execute` to verify the workspace isn't stale. The in-loop integration (`StalenessChecker.check_all` called inside `auto_dispatch_task` before gate 1, with `block_type=staleness` → `progress.md.status=blocked_stale` routing) is **DEFERRED to v0.8.2** per route-A re-scope (codex round-4 R4 + round-5 R3). T20 ships the detector logic + doctor wiring; v0.8.2 promotes to gate-0 in the dispatch loop.

**5 Triggers (Y2 explicit)**:

| # | Trigger | Detection | Cost |
|---|---------|-----------|------|
| 1 | base branch moved | `git rev-parse <integration_target>` ≠ `original_base_commit` (T10) | O(1) |
| 2 | lockfile changed | sha256 of `package-lock.json` / `Cargo.lock` / `requirements.txt` / `poetry.lock` / `go.sum` ≠ snapshot at task start | O(file size) per file |
| 3 | `prd.md` edited | mtime of `.flow/tasks/<slug>/prd.md` > task-start mtime | O(1) |
| 4 | dependencies version changed | parse `package.json.dependencies` / `pyproject.toml.dependencies` / `Cargo.toml.dependencies` for any version-spec mismatch vs snapshot | O(file size) per file |
| 5 | baseline tests fail (now, but passed at start) | re-run baseline gate 1 command (Q3.1 inside worktree); compare returncode | O(suite runtime) |

**Trigger 5 cost note**: re-running baseline mid-task is expensive. In v0.8.1 (doctor-only scope), all 5 triggers run when the user invokes `flow doctor <slug>` — orchestrator does NOT call any of them in the dispatch loop. Triggers 1–4 are cheap; trigger 5 (re-run baseline) is gated behind explicit doctor invocation. v0.8.2 will promote triggers 1–4 to gate-0 in the dispatch loop (called BEFORE worktree creation) and keep trigger 5 doctor-only + resume-validation only.

**`StalenessVerdict`**:

```python
@dataclass
class StalenessVerdict:
    stale: bool
    triggered: list[str]                    # subset of {base_branch, lockfile, prd_mtime, dep_version, baseline_fail}
    details: dict = field(default_factory=dict)
```

`StalenessChecker.check_all()` runs triggers 1–4 (fast) + optionally 5. **In v0.8.1 the only caller is `flow doctor`** — output is printed to the user, who decides whether to abort `--auto-execute`. v0.8.2 will add the orchestrator-side caller that routes to `block` (block_type=staleness) on any trigger.

  ```python
  class TestStalenessTrigger1BaseBranchMoved(unittest.TestCase):
      def test_base_unchanged_returns_not_stale(self):
          # ctx with original_base_commit == current HEAD of integration target
          v = StalenessChecker.check_base_branch_moved(
              repo_root=self.repo_root, ctx=ctx)
          self.assertFalse(v[0])  # tuple (stale, details)

      def test_base_advanced_triggers(self):
          # Advance master beyond original_base_commit
          subprocess.run(["git", "-C", str(self.repo_root), "commit",
                          "--allow-empty", "-m", "advance"], check=True)
          v = StalenessChecker.check_base_branch_moved(
              repo_root=self.repo_root, ctx=ctx)
          self.assertTrue(v[0])
          self.assertIn("from_commit", v[1])
          self.assertIn("to_commit", v[1])
  ```

- [ ] **Step 20.2: Implement `StalenessChecker` skeleton + trigger 1**

  Extend `scripts/flow_staleness.py`:

  ```python
  @dataclass
  class StalenessVerdict:
      stale: bool
      triggered: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
      details: dict = field(default_factory=dict)


  class StalenessChecker:
      LOCKFILES = (
          "package-lock.json", "Cargo.lock", "requirements.txt",
          "poetry.lock", "go.sum", "Gemfile.lock",
      )

      def __init__(
          self, *,
          repo_root: Path, ctx: WorktreeContext, task_dir: Path,
          baseline_snapshot: Optional[dict] = None,
      ):
          self.repo_root = repo_root
          self.ctx = ctx
          self.task_dir = task_dir
          self.baseline_snapshot = baseline_snapshot or {}

      @staticmethod
      def check_base_branch_moved(
          *, repo_root: Path, ctx: WorktreeContext,
      ) -> tuple[bool, dict]:
          current = subprocess.run(
              ["git", "-C", str(repo_root), "rev-parse",
               ctx.integration_target],
              capture_output=True, text=True, check=False,
          ).stdout.strip()
          if not current:
              return (False, {"reason": "could not resolve integration_target"})
          if current == ctx.original_base_commit:
              return (False, {})
          return (True, {
              "from_commit": ctx.original_base_commit,
              "to_commit": current,
          })
  ```

  Re-run Step 20.1 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 20.3: Failing tests — trigger 2 lockfile hash mismatch**

  ```python
  def test_lockfile_unchanged_not_stale(self):
      (self.repo_root / "package-lock.json").write_text('{"v": 1}')
      snapshot = StalenessChecker.snapshot_lockfiles(self.repo_root)
      r = StalenessChecker.check_lockfile_changed(self.repo_root, snapshot)
      self.assertFalse(r[0])

  def test_lockfile_modified_triggers(self):
      (self.repo_root / "package-lock.json").write_text('{"v": 1}')
      snapshot = StalenessChecker.snapshot_lockfiles(self.repo_root)
      (self.repo_root / "package-lock.json").write_text('{"v": 2}')
      r = StalenessChecker.check_lockfile_changed(self.repo_root, snapshot)
      self.assertTrue(r[0])
      self.assertIn("package-lock.json", r[1]["changed"])
  ```

- [ ] **Step 20.4: Implement trigger 2 + lockfile snapshot helper**

  ```python
  @classmethod
  def snapshot_lockfiles(cls, repo_root: Path) -> dict[str, str]:
      out: dict[str, str] = {}
      for name in cls.LOCKFILES:
          p = repo_root / name
          if p.is_file():
              out[name] = hashlib.sha256(p.read_bytes()).hexdigest()
      return out

  @classmethod
  def check_lockfile_changed(
      cls, repo_root: Path, snapshot: dict[str, str],
  ) -> tuple[bool, dict]:
      current = cls.snapshot_lockfiles(repo_root)
      changed = [name for name, h in snapshot.items()
                  if current.get(name) != h]
      added = [name for name in current if name not in snapshot]
      if not changed and not added:
          return (False, {})
      return (True, {"changed": changed + added})
  ```

  Re-run Step 20.3 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 20.5: Failing tests — trigger 3 prd.md mtime + trigger 4 dep version + trigger 5 baseline fail**

  ```python
  def test_prd_mtime_advances_triggers(self):
      prd = self.task_dir / "prd.md"
      prd.write_text("# spec\n")
      snap = prd.stat().st_mtime
      time.sleep(0.05)
      prd.write_text("# spec v2\n")  # mtime advances
      r = StalenessChecker.check_prd_edited(prd_path=prd,
                                              snapshot_mtime=snap)
      self.assertTrue(r[0])

  def test_dep_version_change_triggers(self):
      (self.repo_root / "package.json").write_text(json.dumps({
          "dependencies": {"foo": "^1.0.0"}}))
      snap = StalenessChecker.snapshot_dep_versions(self.repo_root)
      (self.repo_root / "package.json").write_text(json.dumps({
          "dependencies": {"foo": "^2.0.0"}}))
      r = StalenessChecker.check_dep_versions_changed(
          self.repo_root, snap)
      self.assertTrue(r[0])
      self.assertIn("foo", r[1]["changed"])

  def test_baseline_now_fails_triggers(self):
      r = StalenessChecker.check_baseline_now_fails(
          worktree_root=self.ctx.worktree_path,
          baseline_command="false",
          baseline_was_passing=True,
      )
      self.assertTrue(r[0])

  def test_baseline_was_already_failing_no_trigger(self):
      """If baseline was failing at task start, current fail is NOT a trigger."""
      r = StalenessChecker.check_baseline_now_fails(
          worktree_root=self.ctx.worktree_path,
          baseline_command="false",
          baseline_was_passing=False,
      )
      self.assertFalse(r[0])
  ```

- [ ] **Step 20.6: Implement triggers 3, 4, 5**

  ```python
  @staticmethod
  def check_prd_edited(
      *, prd_path: Path, snapshot_mtime: float,
  ) -> tuple[bool, dict]:
      if not prd_path.is_file():
          return (False, {"reason": "prd.md missing"})
      current_mtime = prd_path.stat().st_mtime
      if current_mtime <= snapshot_mtime:
          return (False, {})
      return (True, {
          "snapshot_mtime": snapshot_mtime, "current_mtime": current_mtime,
      })

  DEP_FILES = ("package.json", "pyproject.toml", "Cargo.toml", "go.mod")

  @classmethod
  def snapshot_dep_versions(cls, repo_root: Path) -> dict[str, str]:
      """Crude content-hash of dependency declarations. v0.8.1 doesn't
      parse semver — any byte-level change in dep files counts. v0.8.2
      can refine to per-package version diffs."""
      out: dict[str, str] = {}
      for name in cls.DEP_FILES:
          p = repo_root / name
          if p.is_file():
              out[name] = hashlib.sha256(p.read_bytes()).hexdigest()
      return out

  @classmethod
  def check_dep_versions_changed(
      cls, repo_root: Path, snapshot: dict[str, str],
  ) -> tuple[bool, dict]:
      current = cls.snapshot_dep_versions(repo_root)
      changed = [name for name, h in snapshot.items()
                  if current.get(name) != h]
      added = [name for name in current if name not in snapshot]
      if not changed and not added:
          return (False, {})
      return (True, {"changed": changed + added})

  @staticmethod
  def check_baseline_now_fails(
      *, worktree_root: Path, baseline_command: str,
      baseline_was_passing: bool,
  ) -> tuple[bool, dict]:
      if not baseline_was_passing:
          # Already failing at start — current fail is not a NEW trigger.
          return (False, {"reason": "baseline was failing at task start"})
      proc = subprocess.run(
          baseline_command, shell=True, cwd=str(worktree_root),
          capture_output=True, text=True,
      )
      if proc.returncode == 0:
          return (False, {})
      return (True, {
          "exit_code": proc.returncode,
          "stderr_tail": proc.stderr[-500:],
      })
  ```

  Re-run Step 20.5 → PASS.

- [ ] **Step 20.7: Implement `check_all` aggregator**

  ```python
  def check_all(
      self,
      *,
      include_baseline: bool = False,
      baseline_command: str = "",
      baseline_was_passing: bool = True,
  ) -> StalenessVerdict:
      """Runs triggers 1-4 (cheap) + optionally 5 (expensive).
      Orchestrator runs include_baseline=False at gate 0 (start of task);
      flow doctor runs include_baseline=True for periodic re-validation.
      """
      verdict = StalenessVerdict(stale=False)
      r1, d1 = self.check_base_branch_moved(repo_root=self.repo_root, ctx=self.ctx)
      if r1:
          verdict.stale = True
          verdict.triggered.append("base_branch")
          verdict.details["base_branch"] = d1
      r2, d2 = self.check_lockfile_changed(
          self.repo_root, self.baseline_snapshot.get("lockfiles", {}))
      if r2:
          verdict.stale = True
          verdict.triggered.append("lockfile")
          verdict.details["lockfile"] = d2
      prd = self.task_dir / "prd.md"
      r3, d3 = self.check_prd_edited(
          prd_path=prd,
          snapshot_mtime=self.baseline_snapshot.get("prd_mtime", 0.0))
      if r3:
          verdict.stale = True
          verdict.triggered.append("prd_mtime")
          verdict.details["prd_mtime"] = d3
      r4, d4 = self.check_dep_versions_changed(
          self.repo_root, self.baseline_snapshot.get("dep_versions", {}))
      if r4:
          verdict.stale = True
          verdict.triggered.append("dep_version")
          verdict.details["dep_version"] = d4
      if include_baseline:
          r5, d5 = self.check_baseline_now_fails(
              worktree_root=self.ctx.worktree_path,
              baseline_command=baseline_command,
              baseline_was_passing=baseline_was_passing,
          )
          if r5:
              verdict.stale = True
              verdict.triggered.append("baseline_fail")
              verdict.details["baseline_fail"] = d5
      return verdict
  ```

- [ ] **Step 20.8: Wire into `flow_doctor` (v0.8.1) — orchestrator integration deferred to v0.8.2**

  Add a "Staleness" section to `flow_doctor` output that runs all 5 triggers (`include_baseline=True`) for each active task and prints a summary. This is the **only** staleness surface in v0.8.1 — user runs `flow doctor <slug>` manually before invoking `--auto-execute`.

  **Deferred to v0.8.2** (per route-A re-scope, codex round-4 R4): in-loop staleness gate in `flow_orchestrator.auto_dispatch_task`. The dispatch loop should call `StalenessChecker.check_all(include_baseline=False)` BEFORE worktree creation + `auto_engaged` event so stale state never wastes a subagent dispatch. v0.8.1 punts to the `flow doctor` out-of-band check; v0.8.2 promotes to gate-0 in the dispatch loop:

  ```python
  # v0.8.2 PREVIEW (NOT in v0.8.1 dispatch loop):
  if (verdict := staleness.check_all()).stale:
      notifier.fire_block(
          block_type="staleness", phase=2,
          task_id=manifest.id,
          issue_id="staleness::" + ",".join(verdict.triggered),
          why_blocked=f"staleness triggered: {verdict.triggered}",
          required_choice=["resume_after_rebase", "abort_task",
                           "switch_to_interactive"],
          safe_resume_command=f"flow orchestrator --resume {slug}",
      )
      return
  ```

### Task 21: Nested-autonomy mechanical detection (S5)

**Files:**
- Modify: `scripts/flow_orchestrator.py` (entry guard)
- Modify: `tests/smoke/test_orchestrator_worktree.py` (or new `tests/smoke/test_nested_autonomy_aborts.py`)

**Design refs:** §1 row 16 (nested-autonomy attempt → `abort` with `aborted_nested` status, Tier 1+2 final), §7 S5 mechanical-detection (subagent process inherits `FLOW_AUTONOMY_PARENT_PID=<orchestrator pid>`; subagent attempting `flow orchestrator --auto-execute <slug>` checks env at startup; if set → abort with `aborted_nested` + log to `decisions.jsonl`. Pre-exec check, NOT post-hoc. Detection in orchestrator CLI entry point, not subagent SKILL).

**Goal:** Add a mechanical pre-exec guard at the top of `flow_orchestrator.main()` that:
1. Reads `FLOW_AUTONOMY_PARENT_PID` env var.
2. If set AND `--auto-execute` flag present → abort with `aborted_nested` decision + Tier 2 final notification + exit code 4 (distinct from block exit 3).
3. Top-level orchestrator (no env var) sets `FLOW_AUTONOMY_PARENT_PID=<own pid>` in the env it propagates to subagent dispatch (extends T10's `auto_dispatch_task`).

The check is mechanical (env var presence) rather than parent-process tree walking — robust against process-group changes, container boundaries, sudo, etc.

**Why pre-exec, not post-hoc**: detecting after subagent has already run risks irreversible side effects (commits, network calls). Env var check at `main()` entry runs in microseconds and prevents the inner orchestrator from starting at all.

- [ ] **Step 21.1: Failing test — `flow orchestrator --auto-execute` aborts when `FLOW_AUTONOMY_PARENT_PID` is set**

  ```python
  # tests/smoke/test_nested_autonomy_aborts.py
  class TestNestedAutonomyAborts(unittest.TestCase):
      def test_subprocess_with_parent_pid_aborts(self):
          # Run the orchestrator as a subprocess WITH the env var set
          env = os.environ.copy()
          env["FLOW_AUTONOMY_PARENT_PID"] = str(os.getpid())
          slug_dir = self._setup_minimal_slug_dir()
          r = subprocess.run(
              [sys.executable, str(REPO_ROOT / "scripts" / "flow.py"),
               "orchestrator", "--auto-execute", "demo"],
              env=env, cwd=str(self.tmp),
              capture_output=True, text=True,
          )
          # Exit code 4 = aborted_nested
          self.assertEqual(r.returncode, 4)
          self.assertIn("aborted_nested", r.stderr.lower())
          # Decision logged
          dec = (slug_dir / "decisions.jsonl").read_text()
          self.assertIn("aborted_nested", dec)

      def test_top_level_no_env_var_proceeds(self):
          env = os.environ.copy()
          env.pop("FLOW_AUTONOMY_PARENT_PID", None)
          # ... slug fixture without contract.json — fallback to interactive ...
          r = subprocess.run(
              [sys.executable, str(REPO_ROOT / "scripts" / "flow.py"),
               "orchestrator", "--auto-execute", "demo"],
              env=env, cwd=str(self.tmp),
              capture_output=True, text=True,
          )
          # Exit 0 (interactive fallback) — NOT 4 (nested abort)
          self.assertEqual(r.returncode, 0)
          self.assertNotIn("aborted_nested", r.stderr.lower())
  ```

- [ ] **Step 21.2: Implement env guard at `main()` entry**

  ```python
  AUTONOMY_PARENT_PID_ENV = "FLOW_AUTONOMY_PARENT_PID"


  def _guard_against_nested_autonomy(slug: str) -> Optional[int]:
      """S5: subagent inherits FLOW_AUTONOMY_PARENT_PID from the parent
      orchestrator. If set, ANY --auto-execute attempt is a nested
      attempt and must abort. Returns exit code 4 if guard fires; None
      if guard passes (top-level orchestrator proceeds).
      """
      parent_pid = os.environ.get(AUTONOMY_PARENT_PID_ENV)
      if not parent_pid:
          return None
      try:
          task_dir = _resolve_slug_dir(slug)
      except SystemExit:
          # Slug doesn't exist; abort with the same exit code rather than
          # a confusing "not found" message — security-positive default.
          print(
              f"ERROR: nested autonomy attempt detected "
              f"(FLOW_AUTONOMY_PARENT_PID={parent_pid}); "
              f"slug {slug!r} not found. Aborting with aborted_nested.",
              file=sys.stderr,
          )
          return 4
      # Log decision
      append_decision(task_dir, DecisionRecord(
          id=f"aborted-nested-{_new_event_id()}",
          ts=_now_iso(),
          phase=2, task=slug,
          decision="aborted_nested",
          reason=(f"--auto-execute called with "
                   f"FLOW_AUTONOMY_PARENT_PID={parent_pid}; "
                   f"nested autonomy is forbidden (§1 row 16)"),
      ))
      print(
          f"ERROR: aborted_nested — orchestrator was invoked from a "
          f"subagent context (FLOW_AUTONOMY_PARENT_PID={parent_pid}). "
          f"Nested autonomy is forbidden; see §1 row 16.",
          file=sys.stderr,
      )
      return 4


  def main(argv: Optional[list[str]] = None) -> int:
      parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(prog="flow orchestrator")
      parser.add_argument("--dry-run", metavar="SLUG", help="Print plan + manifest")
      parser.add_argument("--auto-execute", metavar="SLUG",
                          help="Execute autonomously (v0.8.1+)")
      args = parser.parse_args(argv)

      if args.auto_execute:
          # S5 guard runs FIRST — before any other logic
          guard = _guard_against_nested_autonomy(args.auto_execute)
          if guard is not None:
              return guard
          return _cmd_auto_execute(args.auto_execute)
      if args.dry_run:
          return _cmd_dry_run(args.dry_run)
      parser.print_help()
      return 1
  ```

  Re-run Step 21.1 → PASS.

> When `progress.md.autonomy_mode == auto`, invoke `flow orchestrator --auto-execute <slug>`. The orchestrator owns: worktree-per-task dispatch, 8-gate runner (baseline / subagent / manifest verify / codex review / acceptance / regression / local merge / post-merge verify) — gates run ONCE per dispatch in v0.8.1, no retry loop, Tier 1+2 notification, crash recovery, and nested-autonomy abort. Subagent's role: execute the per-task prompt and return narrative summary only — orchestrator derives facts from worktree diff (PRD §1.2). DO NOT attempt manual worktree management or merge from inside this SKILL — the orchestrator has the authority. - [ ] **Step 22.0: Create `scripts/flow_subagent_dispatch.py` shim (round-5 R1 fix)**

  T19 Step 19.11's dispatch loop imports `flow_subagent_dispatch` to invoke the subagent. Without this module the loop crashes at first call. T22 creates the shim because T22 is the SKILL/capability owner — the shim is the bridge between the orchestrator (Python) and the subagent invocation mechanism (Claude CLI / SKILL prompt).

  The v0.8.1 shim resolves the dispatch command via env var → capability binding → fail-closed:
  1. **`FLOW_SUBAGENT_DISPATCH_CMD`** env var (highest priority — used in tests + manual override). A shell command template with `{worktree}`, `{slug}`, `{task_id}` placeholders.
  2. **`claude/capabilities/defaults.json::autonomy_orchestrator.dispatch_cmd`** (production default — set by Step 22.4 capability promotion to invoke the appropriate Claude CLI / SKILL command).
  3. If neither resolves → raise `RuntimeError` with actionable message (no silent skip — better to fail loudly than dispatch nothing and leave the worktree untouched).

  ```python
  # scripts/flow_subagent_dispatch.py
  """v0.8.1 dispatch shim. Bridges orchestrator (Python) to subagent
  invocation. Resolution order: env var → capability binding →
  RuntimeError. The shim is intentionally thin — Step 22.6 wires the
  capability binding to the real Claude CLI invocation; tests substitute
  via FLOW_SUBAGENT_DISPATCH_CMD env var (see test_subagent_dispatch_shim.py).
  """
  from __future__ import annotations

  import json, os, subprocess, sys
  from pathlib import Path
  from typing import Any


  ENV_VAR = "FLOW_SUBAGENT_DISPATCH_CMD"
  CAPABILITY_FILE = Path("claude/capabilities/defaults.json")


  def _resolve_cmd_template() -> str:
      cmd = os.environ.get(ENV_VAR)
      if cmd:
          return cmd
      if CAPABILITY_FILE.is_file():
          try:
              caps = json.loads(CAPABILITY_FILE.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
              entry = caps.get("autonomy_orchestrator", {})
              cmd = entry.get("dispatch_cmd")
              if cmd:
                  return cmd
          except (json.JSONDecodeError, AttributeError):
              pass
      raise RuntimeError(
          f"subagent dispatch not configured: set {ENV_VAR} env var "
          f"OR populate {CAPABILITY_FILE}::autonomy_orchestrator.dispatch_cmd. "
          f"v0.8.1 fails closed rather than silently skipping dispatch.")


  def invoke(ctx: Any, *, subagent_env: dict | None = None, **kw) -> None:
      """Called by orchestrator's _invoke_subagent_dispatch. ctx is the
      WorktreeContext; the resolved command template gets {worktree},
      {slug}, {task_id} substituted. Subagent runs as a subprocess so
      its crash doesn't take down the orchestrator."""
      template = _resolve_cmd_template()
      cmd_str = template.format(
          worktree=str(ctx.worktree_path),
          slug=ctx.slug,
          task_id=getattr(ctx, "task_id", ""),
      )
      env = {**os.environ, **(subagent_env or {})}
      proc = subprocess.run(
          cmd_str, shell=True, cwd=str(ctx.worktree_path),
          env=env, capture_output=False, text=True,
      )
      if proc.returncode != 0:
          # Subagent failure is a soft signal — orchestrator's manifest
          # verify (T11) and gate runner (T12) catch the empty/broken
          # diff and route appropriately. Don't raise here.
          print(
              f"WARN: subagent dispatch returned {proc.returncode} for "
              f"{ctx.slug}/{getattr(ctx, 'task_id', '?')} — orchestrator "
              f"will derive facts from worktree state and route per gates.",
              file=sys.stderr,
          )
  ```

- [ ] **Step 22.0b: Failing test — `test_subagent_dispatch_shim.py` (round-5 R1)**

  ```python
  # tests/smoke/test_subagent_dispatch_shim.py
  import os, subprocess, sys, tempfile, unittest
  from pathlib import Path
  from unittest.mock import patch

  REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent.parent
  sys.path.insert(0, str(REPO_ROOT / "scripts"))


  class TestSubagentDispatchShim(unittest.TestCase):
      def setUp(self):
          self.tmp = Path(tempfile.mkdtemp(prefix="flow-shim-"))
          self.addCleanup(lambda: __import__("shutil").rmtree(
              self.tmp, ignore_errors=True))
          # Minimal ctx duck-type
          class _Ctx: pass
          self.ctx = _Ctx()
          self.ctx.worktree_path = self.tmp
          self.ctx.slug = "demo"
          self.ctx.task_id = "T0"

      def test_env_var_template_invoked(self):
          """FLOW_SUBAGENT_DISPATCH_CMD env var → shell command runs."""
          marker = self.tmp / "dispatched"
          os.environ["FLOW_SUBAGENT_DISPATCH_CMD"] = (
              f"touch {marker}")
          try:
              from flow_subagent_dispatch import invoke
              invoke(self.ctx)
              self.assertTrue(marker.is_file(),
                  "shim must execute the env-var template")
          finally:
              os.environ.pop("FLOW_SUBAGENT_DISPATCH_CMD", None)

      def test_no_config_raises_runtime_error(self):
          """No env var + no capability file → RuntimeError (fail closed)."""
          os.environ.pop("FLOW_SUBAGENT_DISPATCH_CMD", None)
          # cd to a tmp dir so the relative capability path doesn't
          # resolve to the real repo's defaults.json
          orig_cwd = os.getcwd()
          os.chdir(self.tmp)
          try:
              from flow_subagent_dispatch import invoke
              with self.assertRaises(RuntimeError) as cm:
                  invoke(self.ctx)
              self.assertIn("FLOW_SUBAGENT_DISPATCH_CMD", str(cm.exception))
          finally:
              os.chdir(orig_cwd)

      def test_subagent_nonzero_returncode_warns_not_raises(self):
          """Subagent failure is soft — orchestrator handles via gates."""
          os.environ["FLOW_SUBAGENT_DISPATCH_CMD"] = "false"
          try:
              from flow_subagent_dispatch import invoke
              # Should NOT raise
              invoke(self.ctx)
          finally:
              os.environ.pop("FLOW_SUBAGENT_DISPATCH_CMD", None)


  if __name__ == "__main__":
      unittest.main()
  ```

- [ ] **Step 22.2: Replace v0.8.0 Phase 2 guard with v0.8.1 routing language**

  Use `Edit` on `claude/skills/flow/flow-phase2-execute/SKILL.md`. Old string = exact v0.8.0 paragraph; new string = the routing block above (under a heading like `## Auto mode (v0.8.1+)`). Preserve surrounding sections untouched. **DO NOT re-export structure / re-format rest of SKILL** — minimal-diff principle.

  Sample replacement (adapt to actual v0.8.0 wording):

  ```markdown
  ## Auto mode (v0.8.1+)

  When `progress.md.autonomy_mode == auto`, invoke:

      flow orchestrator --auto-execute <slug>

  The orchestrator owns (v0.8.1 dispatch foundation):
  - Worktree-per-task dispatch (`<slug>+t<n>+<shortsha>` naming, dual-base recording).
  - 8-gate runner: 1 baseline / 2 subagent execution / 3 manifest verify /
    4 codex review / 5 acceptance criteria / 6 regression smoke /
    7 local merge / 8 post-merge verify in ephemeral verification worktree.
    **Gates run ONCE per dispatch in v0.8.1** — no retry loop (deferred to v0.8.2).
  - Tier 1+2 notification (`blocked.md` + OSC 9 + BEL with throttle).
  - Crash recovery (5-state classifier: pre-lock / lock+dead-pid /
    auto_engaged crash / mid-merge / verification-orphan).
  - Nested-autonomy mechanical guard (`FLOW_AUTONOMY_PARENT_PID` env var).

  **NOT in v0.8.1** (deferred to v0.8.2): AFK timeout, budget enforcement
  (5 counters with paused clock), Phase 2 retry loop, in-loop staleness
  gate. v0.8.1 fails fast on first gate non-pass via Notifier. Run
  `flow doctor <slug>` BEFORE invoking `--auto-execute` to check
  staleness (the in-loop gate ships in v0.8.2).

  Subagent contract (PRD §1.2): execute the per-task prompt; return
  narrative summary ONLY. Orchestrator derives facts from worktree
  `git diff` and test logs — subagent self-report fields are ignored.

  **Hard rule (§7)**: once `auto_engaged` event has been written, any
  subsequent path to interactive mode MUST go through
  `block + user choice`. NEVER silently switch — this includes crash
  recovery on next-startup.

  If `flow orchestrator --auto-execute <slug>` exits non-zero, follow
  `blocked.md` instructions for the user choice. Exit codes:
  - 0 = clean completion or fail-closed-interactive (legal pre-lock).
  - 3 = block raised (`blocked.md` written; user resume needed).
  - 4 = `aborted_nested` (nested-autonomy attempt detected).
  ```

- [ ] **Step 22.3: Update `flow-phase3-finish/SKILL.md` for `flow acceptance --run`**

  ```markdown
  ## Verify gate (v0.8.1+)

  If contract has `acceptance_criteria`, invoke:

      flow acceptance --run <slug>

  This dispatches to `flow_acceptance.AcceptanceRunner` with `phase=3`.
  Phase 3 retry rules apply (R2: behavior/e2e/regression NEVER local —
  always escalate to `blocked_escalate` per §1 row 6).

  Legacy test+codex-only gate runs ONLY when `acceptance_criteria` is
  empty (backward compat for v0.6/0.7 plans without v0.8.1 contracts).
  ```

  ```json
  {

    },
    "acceptance_verify": {
      "default": "flow:acceptance_verify",
      "skip_if_not_available": false,

    }
  }
  ```

  **`dispatch_cmd` field** (round-5 R1): the shell command template that `scripts/flow_subagent_dispatch.py:invoke()` resolves at runtime. Placeholders `{worktree}`, `{slug}`, `{task_id}` are substituted via `str.format()`. - [ ] **Step 22.4b: Wire `flow acceptance --run` CLI subcommand (R5 fix)**

  The Phase 3 SKILL change (Step 22.3) calls `flow acceptance --run <slug>` but no v0.8.0 task implements that subcommand. Add it to `scripts/flow.py` (the existing `flow` CLI entry point) so the SKILL invocation actually has a target.

  Sample wiring (adapt to v0.8.0's existing argparse structure):

  ```python
  # In scripts/flow.py main() argparse setup, add a subparser:
  acceptance_parser = subparsers.add_parser(
      "acceptance", help="Acceptance criteria runner (v0.8.1+)")
  acceptance_parser.add_argument(
      "--run", metavar="SLUG", required=True,
      help="Run all acceptance criteria for the given task slug")
  acceptance_parser.add_argument(
      "--phase", type=int, choices=[2, 3], default=3,
      help="Phase 2 (during dispatch) or Phase 3 (post-merge verify; default)")

  # Dispatch handler:
  def _cmd_acceptance(args) -> int:
      from flow_acceptance import AcceptanceRunner, EvalDecision
      from flow_contract import parse_contract
      slug = args.run
      task_dir = _resolve_slug_dir(slug)
      contract = parse_contract(task_dir / "contract.json")
      criteria = list(contract.acceptance_criteria or [])
      if not criteria:
          print(f"INFO: contract has no acceptance_criteria — nothing to run.",
                file=sys.stderr)
          return 0
      runner = AcceptanceRunner(
          worktree_root=task_dir.parents[2],         # repo root
          log_dir=task_dir / "logs" / "acceptance",
          slug=slug, task_id="phase3", run_id="cli", worktree_id="cli",
      )
      run_id = f"cli+{int(time.time())}"
      for idx, crit in enumerate(criteria):
          rr = runner.run_one(
              crit, criterion_idx=idx,
              attempt_id=run_id, retry_idx=0,
              task_dir=task_dir,
          )
          d = runner.evaluate_criterion(
              crit, phase=args.phase, runner_result=rr)
          if d != EvalDecision.PASS:
              print(f"FAIL: criterion {idx} ({crit.description!r}) → "
                    f"decision={d.value}", file=sys.stderr)
              return 1
      return 0
  ```

- [ ] **Step 22.4c: Failing test — `flow acceptance --run` smoke**

  ```python
  # tests/smoke/test_flow_acceptance_cli.py
  import os, subprocess, sys, tempfile, unittest
  from pathlib import Path

  REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent.parent
  FLOW = REPO_ROOT / "scripts" / "flow.py"


  class TestFlowAcceptanceCLI(unittest.TestCase):
      def setUp(self):
          self.repo = Path(tempfile.mkdtemp(prefix="flow-acc-"))
          self.addCleanup(lambda: __import__("shutil").rmtree(
              self.repo, ignore_errors=True))
          subprocess.run(["git", "init", "-q", str(self.repo)], check=True)
          self.slug_dir = self.repo / ".flow" / "tasks" / "demo"
          self.slug_dir.mkdir(parents=True)

      def _write_contract(self, criteria_passing: bool):
          cmd = "true" if criteria_passing else "false"
          import json
          (self.slug_dir / "contract.json").write_text(json.dumps({
              "contract_schema_version": 1,
              "autonomy_mode": "auto",
              "created_at": "2026-05-06T00:00:00Z",
              "acceptance_criteria": [{
                  "description": "fixture",
                  "type": "smoke", "method": "cmd",
                  "command": cmd, "timeout_sec": 5,
              }],
          }))

      def test_run_pass_returns_zero(self):
          self._write_contract(criteria_passing=True)
          r = subprocess.run(
              [sys.executable, str(FLOW), "acceptance", "--run", "demo"],
              cwd=str(self.repo), capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=30)
          self.assertEqual(r.returncode, 0,
              msg=f"stderr={r.stderr!r}")

      def test_run_fail_returns_nonzero(self):
          self._write_contract(criteria_passing=False)
          r = subprocess.run(
              [sys.executable, str(FLOW), "acceptance", "--run", "demo"],
              cwd=str(self.repo), capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=30)
          self.assertNotEqual(r.returncode, 0)
          self.assertIn("FAIL", r.stderr)
  ```

- [ ] **Step 22.5: Failing tests — `test_no_silent_mode_switch.py` SKILL-routing assertions**

  Append SKILL-side assertions to the test class created in Step 22.4d:

  ```python
  class TestSkillRoutingNoSilentSwitch(unittest.TestCase):
      """§7 hard rule: every code path that could degrade auto → interactive
      must instead block. SKILLs are part of that surface."""

      def setUp(self):
          self.repo_root = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent.parent
          self.phase2 = (self.repo_root /
                         "claude/skills/flow/flow-phase2-execute/SKILL.md")
          self.phase3 = (self.repo_root /
                         "claude/skills/flow/flow-phase3-finish/SKILL.md")

      def test_phase2_skill_invokes_flow_orchestrator(self):
          text = self.phase2.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
          self.assertIn("flow orchestrator --auto-execute", text,
              "Phase 2 SKILL must invoke flow orchestrator --auto-execute "
              "on auto mode (T22 / §7 hard rule)")

      def test_phase2_skill_does_not_say_v0_8_1_reserved(self):
          """v0.8.0 guard must be removed."""
          text = self.phase2.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
          self.assertNotIn("reserved for v0.8.1", text)
          self.assertNotIn("ships in v0.8.1", text)

      def test_phase2_skill_states_no_silent_switch(self):
          """Hard rule must be present in the SKILL itself."""
          text = self.phase2.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
          self.assertIn("NEVER silently switch", text)

      def test_phase3_skill_invokes_flow_acceptance_run(self):
          text = self.phase3.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
          self.assertIn("flow acceptance --run", text,
              "Phase 3 SKILL must invoke flow acceptance --run for verify gate")

      def test_capabilities_default_promoted(self):
          path = self.repo_root / "claude/capabilities/defaults.json"
          caps = json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
          # autonomy_orchestrator + acceptance_verify both promoted
          self.assertNotEqual(
              caps["autonomy_orchestrator"].get("skip_if_not_available", True),
              True,
              "autonomy_orchestrator must NOT skip in v0.8.1")
          self.assertNotEqual(
              caps["acceptance_verify"].get("skip_if_not_available", True),
              True,
              "acceptance_verify must NOT skip in v0.8.1")
  ```

### Task 23: Release with Y7 7-step validation checklist + final consistency check

**Files:**
- Modify: `VERSION`
- Modify: `CHANGELOG.md`
- Modify: `README.md`
- Create: `docs/v0.8.1-autonomy-enabled.md`
- (validation runs every prior test)

**Design refs:** Y7 expanded validation checklist (codex round-3 plan-pass requirement); PRD §3 (v0.8.1 ships full safety stack).

**Goal:** Land VERSION + CHANGELOG + README + migration doc, run the 7-step Y7 validation checklist, do a final cross-task consistency review, then tag `v0.8.1` and push. **Hard gate**: if ANY of the 7 checks fails, ship aborts — fix the cause, do NOT downgrade the check.

**Y7 7-step validation checklist**:

| # | Check | How to run | Pass criterion |
|---|-------|-----------|----------------|
| a | Full smoke + unit suite green | `bash tests/smoke/run.sh` | exit 0; new total ≥ 477 |
| b | `flow doctor` clean (incl. new staleness section) | `flow doctor` | no errors; staleness section present + "all triggers OK" for the test fixture |
| c | `python3 scripts/flow_selftest.py` PASSED | direct invoke | "ALL CHECKS PASSED" |
| d | `flow contract --validate` against migration-doc fixtures | embed 3 example contracts in migration doc; validate each | all 3 pass; expected-fail negative example fails with documented error |
| e | v0.8.0 forward-compat (T3) green | `python3 -m unittest tests.smoke.test_v080_unknown_field_compat` | exit 0 |
| f | git diff sanity — no forbidden-path mods | `git diff master..HEAD --name-only` + cross-check against the file list in the "File Structure" section of this plan | every changed path appears in the planned list; nothing else |
| g | tag `v0.8.1` push | `git tag v0.8.1 && git push origin v0.8.1` | tag visible at `gh release view v0.8.1` |

**Migration doc structure (`docs/v0.8.1-autonomy-enabled.md`)**:

1. **What's new** — 5-bullet summary (autonomy_enabled, 8-gate runner, notification, AFK+budget, crash recovery).
2. **How to enable** — write a contract with `autonomy_mode: auto` + `acceptance_criteria` + budget; `flow doctor` shows readiness.
3. **`acceptance_criteria` writing guide** — 4 method × 6 type matrix; example for each common combination.
4. **Notification** — what `throttle_min` / `tier2_enabled` / OSC 9 do; how to disable; how `archive/blocked/` works.
5. **AFK semantics** — `afk_on_timeout: wait` vs `abort`; 24h cap; mechanical activity signals.
6. **Crash recovery walkthrough** — 5 states + what each `blocked.md` choice does.
7. **Reading `blocked.md`** — frontmatter fields + how `safe_resume_command` works.
8. **`flow audit <slug>`** — replay archived state from `archive/blocked/`.
9. **Migration from v0.8.0** — adding the new contract fields; nothing breaks (additive).
10. **3 example contracts** — minimal / typical / advanced (used for Y7-d validation).
11. **Troubleshooting** — common gotchas (forgotten `tier2_enabled` on CI; lockfile-staleness false positives; nested-autonomy abort).

  ```markdown
  ## v0.8.1 — 2026-05-XX

  **Autonomy enabled.** The execution refusal in v0.8.0 is replaced with
  a hardened 8-gate safety stack:

  - **Contract schema**: 6 new fields (`max_codex_rounds_per_task`,
    `notification.throttle_min`, `notification.tier2_enabled`,
    `idempotent_cmd_allowlist`, `post_merge_regression_optional`,
    criterion-level `idempotent` / `timeout_sec` / `post_merge_skip`).
    Schema version stays at `1` (additive); v0.8.0 readers ignore new
    fields with warning.
  - **8-gate runner**: baseline / subagent / manifest verify / codex
    review / acceptance criteria / regression smoke / local merge /
    post-merge verify (in ephemeral verification worktree).
  - **Atomic merge**: 9-step transactional sequence with explicit gap-
    by-gap crash recovery.
  - **Notification**: 3-tier with throttle + Tier 2 disable + OSC 9
    auto-detect + archive on resume.
  - **AFK + budget**: 24h wait cap; 5 counters with paused-clock; Q3.2
    dual-counter (`rejected_with_rationale` consumes codex round, not
    retry).
  - **Crash recovery**: 5-state classifier (pre-lock / lock+dead-pid /
    auto_engaged / mid-merge / verification-orphan).
  - **Staleness**: 5 explicit triggers (base branch / lockfile / prd
    mtime / dep version / baseline fail).
  - **Nested-autonomy**: `FLOW_AUTONOMY_PARENT_PID` env-var mechanical
    guard at orchestrator entry.

  No backward-incompatible changes. v0.6/0.7 plans without contracts
  continue to run interactively.
  ```

  ```bash
          docs/fixtures/v081-*.json

    (a) suite 477 cases passing

    (e) v0.8.0 forward-compat (T3) green

  )"

  git tag v0.8.1
  git push origin master
  git push origin v0.8.1
  ```
